Agentic Critical Training
Authors: Weize Liu, Minghui Liu, Sy-Tuyen Ho, Souradip Chakraborty, Xiyao Wang, Furong Huang
First: 2026-03-09T17:58:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T17:58:56+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://attention-is-all-i-need.github.io/ACT/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Training large language models (LLMs) as autonomous agents often begins with imitation learning, but it only teaches agents what to do without understanding why: agents never contrast successful actions against suboptimal alternatives and thus lack awareness of action quality. Recent approaches attempt to address this by introducing self-reflection supervision derived from contrasts between expert and alternative actions. However, the training paradigm fundamentally remains imitation learning: the model imitates pre-constructed reflection text rather than learning to reason autonomously. We propose Agentic Critical Training (ACT), a reinforcement learning paradigm that trains agents to identify the better action among alternatives. By rewarding whether the model's judgment is correct, ACT drives the model to autonomously develop reasoning about action quality, producing genuine self-reflection rather than imitating it. Across three challenging agent benchmarks, ACT consistently improves agent performance when combined with different post-training methods. It achieves an average improvement of 5.07 points over imitation learning and 4.62 points over reinforcement learning. Compared to approaches that inject reflection capability through knowledge distillation, ACT also demonstrates clear advantages, yielding an average improvement of 2.42 points. Moreover, ACT enables strong out-of-distribution generalization on agentic benchmarks and improves performance on general reasoning benchmarks without any reasoning-specific training data, highlighting the value of our method. These results suggest that ACT is a promising path toward developing more reflective and capable LLM agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：智能体批判性训练
将大型语言模型（LLM）训练为自主智能体通常从模仿学习开始，但这仅教会智能体执行动作而不理解原因：智能体从未对比成功动作与次优替代方案，因而缺乏对动作质量的认知。近期研究尝试通过引入专家动作与替代动作对比衍生的自反思监督来解决此问题。然而训练范式本质上仍是模仿学习：模型模仿预先构建的反思文本，而非学习自主推理。我们提出智能体批判性训练（ACT），这是一种强化学习范式，训练智能体在替代动作中识别更优选择。通过奖励模型判断的正确性，ACT驱动模型自主形成对动作质量的推理能力，产生真正的自反思而非模仿。在三个具有挑战性的智能体基准测试中，ACT与不同后训练方法结合时均能持续提升智能体性能，相较模仿学习平均提升5.07分，相较强化学习平均提升4.62分。与通过知识蒸馏注入反思能力的方法相比，ACT也展现出明显优势，平均提升2.42分。此外，ACT在智能体基准测试中实现了强大的分布外泛化能力，并在未使用任何推理专项训练数据的情况下，提升了通用推理基准测试的性能，凸显了本方法的价值。这些结果表明ACT是开发更具反思性和能力的大型语言模型智能体的可行路径。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for Agentic Critical Training (ACT) stems from the limitations of imitation learning in training LLM-based autonomous agents, which fails to teach agents why certain actions are better than others, leading to a lack of genuine self-reflection. To address this, ACT introduces a reinforcement learning paradigm where agents are trained to identify superior actions among alternatives by rewarding correct judgments, thereby fostering autonomous reasoning about action quality rather than merely imitating reflection text. Experimental results across three challenging agent benchmarks show that ACT consistently enhances performance, achieving average improvements of 5.07 points over imitation learning and 4.62 points over reinforcement learning, while also demonstrating strong out-of-distribution generalization and benefits on general reasoning tasks without specific training data.
Agentic Critical Training（ACT）的提出动机在于，基于模仿学习训练大型语言模型作为自主智能体时，仅教导智能体执行动作而无法理解动作优劣的原因，导致其缺乏真正的自我反思能力。为此，ACT采用强化学习范式，通过奖励智能体从备选动作中正确识别更优动作，驱动其自主发展对动作质量的推理能力，而非模仿预设的反思文本。在三个具有挑战性的智能体基准测试中，ACT持续提升了性能，相比模仿学习和强化学习分别平均提高5.07分和4.62分，同时展现出强大的分布外泛化能力，并在无需特定训练数据的情况下改善了通用推理任务的表现。
DemoDiffusion: One-Shot Human Imitation using pre-trained Diffusion Policy
Authors: Sungjae Park, Homanga Bharadhwaj, Shubham Tulsiani
Venue: ICRA 2026
First: 2025-06-25T17:59:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T17:58:20+00:00
Comments: 11 pages. Published at ICRA 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
We propose DemoDiffusion, a simple method for enabling robots to perform manipulation tasks by imitating a single human demonstration, without requiring task-specific training or paired human-robot data. Our approach is based on two insights. First, the hand motion in a human demonstration provides a useful prior for the robot's end-effector trajectory, which we can convert into a rough open-loop robot motion trajectory via kinematic retargeting. Second, while this retargeted motion captures the overall structure of the task, it may not align well with plausible robot actions in-context. To address this, we leverage a pre-trained generalist diffusion policy to modify the trajectory, ensuring it both follows the human motion and remains within the distribution of plausible robot actions. Unlike approaches based on online reinforcement learning or paired human-robot data, our method enables robust adaptation to new tasks and scenes with minimal effort. In real-world experiments across 8 diverse manipulation tasks, DemoDiffusion achieves 83.8\% average success rate, compared to 13.8\% for the pre-trained policy and 52.5\% for kinematic retargeting, succeeding even on tasks where the pre-trained generalist policy fails entirely. Project page: https://demodiffusion.github.io/
中文标题/摘要
标题：DemoDiffusion：基于预训练扩散策略的单次人类模仿方法
我们提出DemoDiffusion，一种使机器人通过单次人类演示即可执行操作任务的简易方法，无需任务特定训练或配对人机数据。该方法基于两点洞见：首先，人类演示中的手部运动为机器人末端执行器轨迹提供了有效先验，可通过运动学重定向转化为粗略的开环机器人运动轨迹；其次，重定向轨迹虽能捕捉任务整体结构，但可能与实际场景中的合理机器人动作存在偏差。为此，我们利用预训练的通用扩散策略修正轨迹，确保其既遵循人类运动模式，又保持在合理机器人动作分布内。与基于在线强化学习或配对人机数据的方法不同，本方法能以最小成本实现对新任务和场景的鲁棒适应。在8项多样化操作任务的真实实验中，DemoDiffusion平均成功率达83.8%，显著优于预训练策略的13.8%和运动学重定向的52.5%，甚至在预训练通用策略完全失败的任务中仍能成功。项目页面：https://demodiffusion.github.io/
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for robots to learn manipulation tasks from minimal human input without task-specific training, this paper introduces DemoDiffusion, a method for one-shot human imitation. The approach first extracts a rough robot motion trajectory from a single human demonstration via kinematic retargeting of hand movements, then refines it using a pre-trained generalist diffusion policy to ensure the trajectory aligns with plausible robot actions while following the human intent. Experimental results on eight diverse real-world manipulation tasks show that DemoDiffusion achieves an average success rate of 83.8%, significantly outperforming both the pre-trained policy alone (13.8%) and kinematic retargeting alone (52.5%), and it succeeds even where the pre-trained policy fails.
本文的动机是让机器人能够仅通过单次人类演示学习操作任务，而无需任务特定训练或配对的人机数据，为此提出了DemoDiffusion方法。该方法首先通过运动学重定向将人类手部运动转换为粗略的机器人末端轨迹，然后利用预训练的通用扩散策略对其进行修正，以确保轨迹既遵循人类演示又符合机器人动作的合理分布。在八个多样化真实世界操作任务上的实验结果表明，DemoDiffusion平均成功率达到83.8%，显著优于单独使用预训练策略（13.8%）和单独运动学重定向（52.5%），甚至在预训练策略完全失败的任务上也能成功。
Tree-based Dialogue Reinforced Policy Optimization for Red-Teaming Attacks
Authors: Ruohao Guo, Afshin Oroojlooy, Roshan Sridhar, Miguel Ballesteros, Alan Ritter, Dan Roth
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-02T17:57:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T17:54:56+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite recent rapid progress in AI safety, current large language models remain vulnerable to adversarial attacks in multi-turn interaction settings, where attackers strategically adapt their prompts across conversation turns and pose a more critical yet realistic challenge. Existing approaches that discover safety vulnerabilities either rely on manual red-teaming with human experts or employ automated methods using pre-defined templates and human-curated attack data, with most focusing on single-turn attacks. However, these methods did not explore the vast space of possible multi-turn attacks, failing to consider novel attack trajectories that emerge from complex dialogue dynamics and strategic conversation planning. This gap is particularly critical given recent findings that LLMs exhibit significantly higher vulnerability to multi-turn attacks compared to single-turn attacks. We propose DialTree, an on-policy reinforcement learning framework integrated with tree search that autonomously discovers diverse multi-turn attack strategies by treating the dialogue as a sequential decision-making problem, enabling systematic exploration without manually curated data. Through extensive experiments, our approach not only achieves more than 44.2% higher ASR across 12 target models compared to previous state-of-the-art approaches, but also effectively uncovers new attack strategies by learning optimal dialogue policies that maximize attack success across multiple turns.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于树形对话的强化策略优化在红队攻击中的应用
尽管人工智能安全领域近期进展迅速，当前大语言模型在多轮交互场景中仍易受对抗性攻击。攻击者通过跨对话轮次策略性调整提示，构成更严峻且现实的挑战。现有发现安全漏洞的方法依赖人工专家红队测试，或采用基于预定义模板和人工标注攻击数据的自动化方法，且多聚焦单轮攻击。然而，这些方法未探索多轮攻击的广阔可能性空间，未能考虑复杂对话动态和策略性会话规划产生的新型攻击轨迹。鉴于近期研究发现大语言模型对多轮攻击的脆弱性显著高于单轮攻击，这一空白尤为关键。我们提出DialTree框架：一种集成树搜索的在线策略强化学习方法，通过将对话建模为序列决策问题，无需人工标注数据即可系统探索并自主发现多样化的多轮攻击策略。大量实验表明，该方法在12个目标模型上的攻击成功率比现有最优方法提升超44.2%，并能通过学习最大化多轮攻击成功概率的最优对话策略，有效揭示新型攻击模式。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the heightened vulnerability of large language models to strategic multi-turn adversarial attacks compared to single-turn ones, this paper introduces DialTree, a method that frames dialogue-based red-teaming as a sequential decision problem. It employs an on-policy reinforcement learning framework integrated with tree search to autonomously explore diverse multi-turn attack strategies without relying on manually curated data. The main experimental results demonstrate that this approach achieves over 44.2% higher attack success rates across 12 target models than prior state-of-the-art methods and effectively uncovers novel attack strategies by learning optimal dialogue policies.
本文的动机在于，相比于单轮攻击，大型语言模型在策略性多轮对抗攻击面前表现出更高的脆弱性。为此，论文提出了DialTree方法，将基于对话的红队测试构建为一个序列决策问题，该方法融合了树搜索的在线策略强化学习框架，能够自主探索多样的多轮攻击策略，无需依赖人工标注数据。主要实验结果表明，该方法在12个目标模型上的攻击成功率比之前的最先进方法高出44.2%以上，并通过学习最优对话策略，有效发现了新的攻击策略。
How Far Can Unsupervised RLVR Scale LLM Training?
Authors: Bingxiang He, Yuxin Zuo, Zeyuan Liu, Shangziqi Zhao, Zixuan Fu, Junlin Yang, Cheng Qian, Kaiyan Zhang, Yuchen Fan, Ganqu Cui, Xiusi Chen, Youbang Sun, Xingtai Lv, Xuekai Zhu, Li Sheng, Ran Li, Huan-ang Gao, Yuchen Zhang, Bowen Zhou, Zhiyuan Liu, Ning Ding
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-09T17:38:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T17:38:11+00:00
Comments: Accepted to the ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unsupervised reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (URLVR) offers a pathway to scale LLM training beyond the supervision bottleneck by deriving rewards without ground truth labels. Recent works leverage model intrinsic signals, showing promising early gains, yet their potential and limitations remain unclear. In this work, we revisit URLVR and provide a comprehensive analysis spanning taxonomy, theory and extensive experiments. We first classify URLVR methods into intrinsic versus external based on reward sources, then establish a unified theoretical framework revealing that all intrinsic methods converge toward sharpening the model's initial distribution This sharpening mechanism succeeds when initial confidence aligns with correctness but fails catastrophically when misaligned. Through systematic experiments, we show intrinsic rewards consistently follow a rise-then-fall pattern across methods, with collapse timing determined by model prior rather than engineering choices. Despite these scaling limits, we find intrinsic rewards remain valuable in test-time training on small datasets, and propose Model Collapse Step to measure model prior, serving as a practical indicator for RL trainability. Finally, we explore external reward methods that ground verification in computational asymmetries, showing preliminary evidence they may escape the confidence-correctness ceiling. Our findings chart boundaries for intrinsic URLVR while motivating paths toward scalable alternatives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无监督RLVR能将LLM训练扩展到何种程度？
基于可验证奖励的无监督强化学习（URLVR）通过无需真实标签生成奖励，为突破监督瓶颈扩展大语言模型训练提供了路径。近期研究利用模型内在信号展现出早期潜力，但其潜能与局限尚不明确。本文重新审视URLVR，通过分类体系、理论框架与大量实验进行综合分析。首先依据奖励来源将URLVR方法分为内在型与外部型，继而建立统一理论框架，揭示所有内在方法均趋于强化模型的初始分布——当初始置信度与正确性一致时该强化机制有效，但二者错配时将导致灾难性失效。系统实验表明，内在奖励在所有方法中均呈现先升后降模式，其崩溃时机由模型先验而非工程选择决定。尽管存在扩展限制，我们发现内在奖励在小数据集测试时训练中仍具价值，并提出'模型崩溃步数'作为衡量模型先验的指标，为RL可训练性提供实践参照。最后，我们探索基于计算不对称性进行验证的外部奖励方法，初步证据显示其可能突破置信度-正确性天花板。本研究界定了内在URLVR的边界，同时为可扩展替代方案指明方向。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the scalability of unsupervised reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (URLVR) for large language model training, motivated by the need to overcome supervision bottlenecks. The authors classify URLVR methods into intrinsic and external reward types, develop a theoretical framework showing that intrinsic methods converge by sharpening the model's initial distribution, and conduct extensive experiments revealing that intrinsic rewards follow a rise-then-fall pattern, with collapse timing dictated by model prior rather than engineering. Key results indicate that while intrinsic methods face scaling limits due to confidence-correctness misalignment, they remain useful for test-time training on small datasets, and external reward methods grounded in computational asymmetries show preliminary potential to surpass these limitations.
本文研究了无监督可验证奖励强化学习在大型语言模型训练中的可扩展性，旨在突破监督学习的瓶颈。作者将URLVR方法分为内在奖励和外部奖励两类，建立了一个理论框架，表明内在方法通过锐化模型的初始分布而收敛，并通过大量实验揭示内在奖励呈现先升后降的模式，其崩溃时间由模型先验而非工程选择决定。主要实验结果表明，尽管内在方法因置信度与正确性错位而面临扩展限制，但在小数据集上的测试时训练中仍有价值，而基于计算不对称性的外部奖励方法初步显示出超越这些限制的潜力。
Towards Batch-to-Streaming Deep Reinforcement Learning for Continuous Control
Authors: Riccardo De Monte, Matteo Cederle, Gian Antonio Susto
First: 2026-03-09T16:40:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T16:40:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
State-of-the-art deep reinforcement learning (RL) methods have achieved remarkable performance in continuous control tasks, yet their computational complexity is often incompatible with the constraints of resource-limited hardware, due to their reliance on replay buffers, batch updates, and target networks. The emerging paradigm of streaming deep RL addresses this limitation through purely online updates, achieving strong empirical performance on standard benchmarks. In this work, we propose two novel streaming deep RL algorithms, Streaming Soft Actor-Critic (S2AC) and Streaming Deterministic Actor-Critic (SDAC), explicitly designed to be compatible with state-of-the-art batch RL methods, making them particularly suitable for on-device finetuning applications such as Sim2Real transfer. Both algorithms achieve performance comparable to state-of-the-art streaming baselines on standard benchmarks without requiring tedious hyperparameter tuning. Finally, we further investigate the practical challenges of transitioning from batch to streaming learning during finetuning and propose concrete strategies to tackle them.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向连续控制的批处理到流式深度强化学习研究
当前最先进的深度强化学习方法在连续控制任务中取得了显著性能，但由于其对经验回放缓冲区、批量更新和目标网络的依赖，其计算复杂度往往难以适配资源受限的硬件约束。新兴的流式深度强化学习范式通过纯在线更新解决了这一局限，在标准基准测试中展现出强大的实证性能。本研究提出两种新型流式深度强化学习算法——流式软演员-评论家（S2AC）与流式确定性演员-评论家（SDAC），其设计明确兼容最先进的批处理强化学习方法，特别适用于仿真到现实迁移等设备端微调应用。两种算法在标准基准测试中均达到与前沿流式基线相当的性能，且无需繁琐的超参数调优。最后，我们进一步探究了微调过程中从批处理学习转向流式学习的实际挑战，并提出具体应对策略。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to adapt high-performing but computationally heavy batch deep reinforcement learning (RL) methods for continuous control to resource-constrained hardware, where purely online streaming updates are more suitable. The authors propose two novel streaming algorithms, Streaming Soft Actor-Critic (S2AC) and Streaming Deterministic Actor-Critic (SDAC), designed to be compatible with state-of-the-art batch RL methods to facilitate on-device finetuning, such as in Sim2Real transfer. Their main experimental results show that both algorithms achieve performance comparable to existing streaming baselines on standard benchmarks without extensive hyperparameter tuning, and they further propose strategies to address practical challenges in transitioning from batch to streaming learning during finetuning.
本文的动机在于，高性能但计算复杂的批量深度强化学习方法难以适用于资源受限的硬件，因此需要转向更适合的纯在线流式更新范式。作者提出了两种新颖的流式算法——流式软演员-评论家（S2AC）和流式确定性演员-评论家（SDAC），这些算法设计为与最先进的批量强化学习方法兼容，特别适用于如仿真到现实迁移等设备端微调应用。主要实验结果表明，这两种算法在标准基准测试中达到了与现有流式基线相当的性能，且无需繁琐的超参数调优，同时作者还进一步研究了从批量学习过渡到流式学习在微调中的实际挑战，并提出了具体的应对策略。
MetaWorld-X: Hierarchical World Modeling via VLM-Orchestrated Experts for Humanoid Loco-Manipulation
Authors: Yutong Shen, Hangxu Liu, Penghui Liu, Jiashuo Luo, Yongkang Zhang, Rex Morvley, Chen Jiang, Jianwei Zhang, Lei Zhang
First: 2026-03-09T16:28:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T16:28:26+00:00
Comments: 8 figures, https://syt2004.github.io/metaworldX/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Learning natural, stable, and compositionally generalizable whole-body control policies for humanoid robots performing simultaneous locomotion and manipulation (loco-manipulation) remains a fundamental challenge in robotics. Existing reinforcement learning approaches typically rely on a single monolithic policy to acquire multiple skills, which often leads to cross-skill gradient interference and motion pattern conflicts in high-degree-of-freedom systems. As a result, generated behaviors frequently exhibit unnatural movements, limited stability, and poor generalization to complex task compositions. To address these limitations, we propose MetaWorld-X, a hierarchical world model framework for humanoid control. Guided by a divide-and-conquer principle, our method decomposes complex control problems into a set of specialized expert policies (Specialized Expert Policies, SEP). Each expert is trained under human motion priors through imitation-constrained reinforcement learning, introducing biomechanically consistent inductive biases that ensure natural and physically plausible motion generation. Building upon this foundation, we further develop an Intelligent Routing Mechanism (IRM) supervised by a Vision-Language Model (VLM), enabling semantic-driven expert composition. The VLM-guided router dynamically integrates expert policies according to high-level task semantics, facilitating compositional generalization and adaptive execution in multi-stage loco-manipulation tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MetaWorld-X：基于VLM编排专家策略的人形机器人分层世界建模与移动操作控制
为人形机器人实现自然、稳定且具备组合泛化能力的全身移动操作控制策略，始终是机器人学领域的核心挑战。现有强化学习方法通常依赖单一整体策略学习多种技能，在高自由度系统中易导致技能间梯度干扰与运动模式冲突，致使生成行为常出现动作不自然、稳定性受限及对复杂任务组合泛化能力差等问题。为此，我们提出MetaWorld-X——一种面向人形机器人控制的分层世界模型框架。该方法遵循分治原则，将复杂控制问题分解为一组专用专家策略。每个专家通过模仿约束强化学习在人体运动先验指导下训练，引入符合生物力学的归纳偏置，确保生成自然且物理合理的运动。在此基础上，我们进一步开发了由视觉语言模型监督的智能路由机制，实现语义驱动的专家策略组合。VLM引导的路由器依据高层任务语义动态整合专家策略，促进多阶段移动操作任务中的组合泛化与自适应执行。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitations of monolithic reinforcement learning policies for humanoid loco-manipulation, which often produce unnatural, unstable motions with poor compositional generalization. The proposed method, MetaWorld-X, employs a hierarchical world model that decomposes control into specialized expert policies trained with human motion priors via imitation-constrained RL, ensuring biomechanically plausible movements, and integrates them via a Vision-Language Model-guided intelligent router for semantic-driven composition. Experimental results demonstrate that the framework generates more natural and stable behaviors and achieves superior generalization in complex, multi-stage loco-manipulation tasks compared to prior approaches.
本研究的动机是解决人形机器人全身运动操控中单一强化学习策略常导致运动不自然、不稳定且组合泛化能力差的问题。所提出的MetaWorld-X方法采用分层世界模型，将控制分解为通过模仿约束强化学习结合人类运动先验训练的专业策略，确保生物力学合理的运动，并利用视觉语言模型指导的智能路由机制进行语义驱动的策略组合。实验结果表明，该框架能生成更自然稳定的行为，并在复杂的多阶段运动操控任务中实现了优于现有方法的组合泛化性能。
RetroAgent: From Solving to Evolving via Retrospective Dual Intrinsic Feedback
Authors: Xiaoying Zhang, Zichen Liu, Yipeng Zhang, Xia Hu, Wenqi Shao
First: 2026-03-09T16:23:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T16:23:33+00:00
Comments: 45 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM)-based agents trained with reinforcement learning (RL) have shown strong potential on complex interactive tasks. However, standard RL paradigms favor static problem-solving over continuous adaptation: agents often converge to suboptimal strategies due to insufficient exploration, while learned knowledge remains implicit within parameters rather than explicitly retrievable, limiting effective experiential learning. To address these limitations, we introduce RetroAgent, an online RL framework that empowers agents to master complex interactive environments not just by solving, but by evolving. Concretely, RetroAgent features a hindsight self-reflection mechanism that produces dual intrinsic feedback: (1) intrinsic numerical feedback that that tracks incremental subtask completion relative to prior attempts, rewarding promising explorations, and (2) intrinsic language feedback that distills reusable lessons into a memory buffer, retrieved via our proposed Similarity & Utility-Aware Upper Confidence Bound (SimUtil-UCB) strategy balancing relevance, utility, and exploration to effectively leverage past experiences. Extensive experiments on two model families across four challenging agentic tasks demonstrate that RetroAgent significantly outperforms existing methods, achieving state-of-the-art results -- e.g., surpassing Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO)-trained agents by +18.3% on ALFWorld, +15.4% on WebShop, +27.1% on Sokoban, and +8.9% on MineSweeper -- while exhibiting strong test-time adaptation and generalization to out-of-distribution scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RetroAgent：通过回顾式双重内在反馈实现从求解到进化的跨越
基于大语言模型（LLM）并通过强化学习（RL）训练的智能体在复杂交互任务中展现出巨大潜力。然而，标准RL范式偏向静态问题求解而非持续适应：智能体常因探索不足而收敛至次优策略，且习得知识仅隐式存储于参数中而非显式可检索，限制了有效的经验学习。为突破这些局限，我们提出RetroAgent——一种在线RL框架，使智能体不仅能通过求解，更能通过进化来掌握复杂交互环境。具体而言，RetroAgent具备事后自省机制，可生成双重内在反馈：（1）追踪相较于先前尝试的子任务完成进度的内在数值反馈，以奖励有潜力的探索；（2）将可复用经验提炼至记忆缓冲区的内在语言反馈，通过我们提出的相似性与效用感知上置信界（SimUtil-UCB）策略进行检索，该策略平衡相关性、效用性与探索性，从而有效利用过往经验。在两类模型族、四项挑战性智能体任务上的大量实验表明，RetroAgent显著优于现有方法，取得最先进成果——例如在ALFWorld超越GRPO训练智能体18.3%、WebShop提升15.4%、Sokoban提高27.1%、MineSweeper增长8.9%——同时展现出强大的测试时适应能力及对分布外场景的泛化性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of standard reinforcement learning (RL) paradigms for large language model (LLM)-based agents, which often lead to suboptimal strategies and implicit, non-retrievable knowledge, this paper introduces RetroAgent, an online RL framework designed to enable continuous adaptation and evolution. The method employs a hindsight self-reflection mechanism that generates dual intrinsic feedback: numerical feedback to reward incremental subtask progress and language feedback that distills reusable lessons into a memory buffer, which is retrieved via a novel Similarity & Utility-Aware Upper Confidence Bound (SimUtil-UCB) strategy to balance relevance, utility, and exploration. Experimental results on four challenging agentic tasks (ALFWorld, WebShop, Sokoban, and MineSweeper) across two model families show that RetroAgent significantly outperforms existing methods, achieving state-of-the-art performance gains of up to +27.1% and demonstrating strong test-time adaptation and generalization to out-of-distribution scenarios.

Impact of Connectivity on Laplacian Representations in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tommaso Giorgi, Pierriccardo Olivieri, Keyue Jiang, Laura Toni, Matteo Papini
First: 2026-03-09T16:20:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T16:20:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning compact state representations in Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) has proven crucial for addressing the curse of dimensionality in large-scale reinforcement learning (RL) problems. Existing principled approaches leverage structural priors on the MDP by constructing state representations as linear combinations of the state-graph Laplacian eigenvectors. When the transition graph is unknown or the state space is prohibitively large, the graph spectral features can be estimated directly via sample trajectories. In this work, we prove an upper bound on the approximation error of linear value function approximation under the learned spectral features. We show how this error scales with the algebraic connectivity of the state-graph, grounding the approximation quality in the topological structure of the MDP. We further bound the error introduced by the eigenvector estimation itself, leading to an end-to-end error decomposition across the representation learning pipeline. Additionally, our expression of the Laplacian operator for the RL setting, although equivalent to existing ones, prevents some common misunderstandings, of which we show some examples from the literature. Our results hold for general (non-uniform) policies without any assumptions on the symmetry of the induced transition kernel. We validate our theoretical findings with numerical simulations on gridworld environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连通性对强化学习中拉普拉斯表示的影响
在马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中学习紧凑的状态表示，已被证明对解决大规模强化学习（RL）问题中的维度灾难至关重要。现有原理性方法通过将状态表示构建为状态图拉普拉斯特征向量的线性组合，来利用MDP的结构先验。当转移图未知或状态空间过大时，可通过采样轨迹直接估计图谱特征。本文证明了在习得谱特征下线性值函数逼近的近似误差上界，并展示了该误差如何随状态图的代数连通性变化，从而将逼近质量锚定于MDP的拓扑结构中。我们进一步界定了特征向量估计本身引入的误差，实现了对表示学习流程的端到端误差分解。此外，我们提出的RL场景下拉普拉斯算子表达式（虽与现有形式等价）避免了文献中常见的误解，并列举了相关示例。我们的结论适用于一般（非均匀）策略，且无需对诱导转移核的对称性作任何假设。通过在网格世界环境中的数值模拟验证了理论结果。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the impact of state-graph connectivity on the quality of Laplacian-based state representations in reinforcement learning, motivated by the need for compact representations to combat dimensionality in large MDPs. The method involves deriving an upper bound on the approximation error for linear value functions when using estimated spectral features from sample trajectories, explicitly linking this error to the algebraic connectivity of the underlying state-graph. Experimental results from gridworld simulations validate the theoretical bounds, demonstrating that the approximation quality is fundamentally tied to the MDP's topological structure, with the analysis applying to general policies without symmetry assumptions.
本文研究了状态图连通性对强化学习中基于拉普拉斯算子的状态表示质量的影响，其动机是为解决大规模马尔可夫决策过程中的维度灾难问题需要紧凑的表示。方法是通过从样本轨迹中估计谱特征，推导出线性值函数近似误差的上界，并将该误差明确关联于底层状态图的代数连通性。在网格世界环境中的数值模拟实验结果验证了理论边界，表明近似质量根本上与MDP的拓扑结构相关，且该分析适用于无对称性假设的一般策略。
Breaking the Bias Barrier in Concave Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Swetha Ganesh, Vaneet Aggarwal
First: 2026-03-09T15:49:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T15:49:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While standard reinforcement learning optimizes a single reward signal, many applications require optimizing a nonlinear utility $f(J_1^π,\dots,J_M^π)$ over multiple objectives, where each $J_m^π$ denotes the expected discounted return of a distinct reward function. A common approach is concave scalarization, which captures important trade-offs such as fairness and risk sensitivity. However, nonlinear scalarization introduces a fundamental challenge for policy gradient methods: the gradient depends on $\partial f(J^π)$, while in practice only empirical return estimates $\hat J$ are available. Because $f$ is nonlinear, the plug-in estimator is biased ($\mathbb{E}[\partial f(\hat J)] \neq \partial f(\mathbb{E}[\hat J])$), leading to persistent gradient bias that degrades sample complexity. In this work we identify and overcome this bias barrier in concave-scalarized multi-objective reinforcement learning. We show that existing policy-gradient methods suffer an intrinsic $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-4})$ sample complexity due to this bias. To address this issue, we develop a Natural Policy Gradient (NPG) algorithm equipped with a multi-level Monte Carlo (MLMC) estimator that controls the bias of the scalarization gradient while maintaining low sampling cost. We prove that this approach achieves the optimal $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ sample complexity for computing an $ε$-optimal policy. Furthermore, we show that when the scalarization function is second-order smooth, the first-order bias cancels automatically, allowing vanilla NPG to achieve the same $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ rate without MLMC. Our results provide the first optimal sample complexity guarantees for concave multi-objective reinforcement learning under policy-gradient methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破凹性多目标强化学习中的偏差壁垒
标准强化学习仅优化单一奖励信号，而许多应用需要在多个目标上优化非线性效用函数 $f(J_1^π,\dots,J_M^π)$，其中每个 $J_m^π$ 表示不同奖励函数的期望折扣回报。常用方法是凹标量化，它能捕捉公平性、风险敏感性等重要权衡。然而，非线性标量化给策略梯度方法带来根本性挑战：梯度依赖于 $\partial f(J^π)$，而实践中仅能获得经验回报估计 $\hat J$。由于 $f$ 的非线性特性，插件估计量存在偏差（$\mathbb{E}[\partial f(\hat J)] \neq \partial f(\mathbb{E}[\hat J])$），导致持续梯度偏差并恶化样本复杂度。 本研究识别并克服了凹标量化多目标强化学习中的这一偏差壁垒。我们证明现有策略梯度方法因该偏差存在固有的 $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-4})$ 样本复杂度。为解决此问题，我们开发了配备多级蒙特卡洛估计器的自然策略梯度算法，该算法在控制标量化梯度偏差的同时保持较低采样成本。我们证明该方法在计算 $ε$ 最优策略时达到了最优的 $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ 样本复杂度。此外，当标量化函数满足二阶光滑性时，一阶偏差会自动抵消，使得基础自然策略梯度算法无需多级蒙特卡洛即可实现相同的 $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ 收敛速率。我们的研究首次为策略梯度方法下的凹性多目标强化学习提供了最优样本复杂度保证。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the bias problem in multi-objective reinforcement learning when using concave scalarization to optimize a nonlinear utility over multiple reward signals, which is crucial for applications like fairness and risk-sensitive decision-making. The authors identify that standard policy gradient methods suffer from persistent gradient bias due to the nonlinearity, leading to suboptimal sample complexity of O(ε⁻⁴). To overcome this, they propose a Natural Policy Gradient algorithm enhanced with a multi-level Monte Carlo estimator that effectively controls bias while maintaining efficiency, achieving an optimal sample complexity of O(ε⁻²). Additionally, they demonstrate that for second-order smooth scalarization functions, vanilla NPG can automatically cancel first-order bias and attain the same optimal rate without the need for MLMC, establishing the first optimal sample complexity guarantees for concave multi-objective RL under policy gradient methods.
本文针对多目标强化学习中，使用凹标量化优化多个奖励信号的非线性效用时存在的偏差问题，这在公平性和风险敏感决策等应用中至关重要。作者指出，由于非线性特性，标准策略梯度方法存在持续梯度偏差，导致样本复杂度为O(ε⁻⁴)。为解决此问题，他们提出了一种结合多级蒙特卡洛估计器的自然策略梯度算法，有效控制偏差的同时保持效率，实现了O(ε⁻²)的最优样本复杂度。此外，他们证明对于二阶光滑的标量化函数，普通自然策略梯度能自动消除一阶偏差，无需多级蒙特卡洛即可达到相同最优速率，从而首次为凹多目标强化学习在策略梯度方法下建立了最优样本复杂度保证。
Oracle-Guided Soft Shielding for Safe Move Prediction in Chess
Authors: Prajit T Rajendran, Fabio Arnez, Huascar Espinoza, Agnes Delaborde, Chokri Mraidha
First: 2026-03-09T15:40:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T15:40:01+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication at the 24th International Conference on Machine Learning and Applications (ICMLA), 2025. Preprint version in Arxiv
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In high stakes environments, agents relying purely on imitation learning or reinforcement learning often struggle to avoid safety-critical errors during exploration. Existing reinforcement learning approaches for environments such as chess require hundreds of thousands of episodes and substantial computational resources to converge. Imitation learning, on the other hand, is more sample efficient but is brittle under distributional shift and lacks mechanisms for proactive risk avoidance. In this work, we propose Oracle-Guided Soft Shielding (OGSS), a simple yet effective framework for safer decision-making, enabling safe exploration by learning a probabilistic safety model from oracle feedback in an imitation learning setting. Focusing on the domain of chess, we train a model to predict strong moves based on past games, and separately learn a blunder prediction model from Stockfish evaluations to estimate the tactical risk of each move. During inference, the agent first generates a set of candidate moves and then uses the blunder model to determine high-risk options, and uses a utility function combining the predicted move likelihood from the policy model and the blunder probability to select actions that strike a balance between performance and safety. This enables the agent to explore and play competitively while significantly reducing the chance of tactical mistakes. Across hundreds of games against a strong chess engine, we compare our approach with other methods in the literature, such as action pruning, SafeDAgger, and uncertainty-based sampling. Our results demonstrate that OGSS variants maintain a lower blunder rate even as the agent's exploration ratio is increased by several folds, highlighting its ability to support broader exploration without compromising tactical soundness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：国际象棋安全走子预测的Oracle引导软屏蔽方法
在高风险环境中，仅依赖模仿学习或强化学习的智能体在探索过程中常难以避免安全关键错误。现有针对国际象棋等环境的强化学习方法需要数十万次对局和大量计算资源才能收敛；模仿学习虽样本效率更高，但存在分布偏移下的脆弱性且缺乏主动风险规避机制。本研究提出Oracle引导软屏蔽（OGSS）框架，通过从模仿学习场景的Oracle反馈中学习概率安全模型，实现更安全的决策与探索。在国际象棋领域，我们训练模型基于历史对局预测强着法，并另从Stockfish评估数据学习失误预测模型以估计每步棋的战术风险。推理时，智能体首先生成候选着法集合，随后利用失误模型识别高风险选项，并通过结合策略模型预测着法概率与失误概率的效用函数，选择兼顾性能与安全的行动。该方法使智能体在保持竞技水平的同时显著降低战术失误概率。通过与强象棋引擎的数百局测试，我们将OGSS与动作剪枝、SafeDAgger及基于不确定性的采样等方法对比。结果表明，即使智能体探索率提升数倍，OGSS变体仍能保持较低失误率，突显其在支持广泛探索时不损害战术稳健性的能力。

The method involves training a policy model to predict strong chess moves and a separate blunder prediction model from Stockfish evaluations; during inference, it combines their outputs via a utility function to select actions balancing performance and safety. Experimental results from hundreds of games against a strong chess engine show that OGSS variants maintain a lower blunder rate even with significantly increased exploration, outperforming methods like action pruning and SafeDAgger in reducing tactical mistakes while supporting broader exploration.

Integrating Lagrangian Neural Networks into the Dyna Framework for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Shreya Das, Kundan Kumar, Muhammad Iqbal, Outi Savolainen, Dominik Baumann, Laura Ruotsalainen, Simo Särkkä
First: 2026-03-09T15:06:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T15:06:10+00:00
Comments: 5 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) is sample-efficient but depends on the accuracy of the learned dynamics, which are often modeled using black-box methods that do not adhere to physical laws. Those methods tend to produce inaccurate predictions when presented with data that differ from the original training set. In this work, we employ Lagrangian neural networks (LNNs), which enforce an underlying Lagrangian structure to train the model within a Dyna-based MBRL framework. Furthermore, we train the LNN using stochastic gradient-based and state-estimation-based optimizers to learn the network's weights. The state-estimation-based method converges faster than the stochastic gradient-based method during neural network training. Simulation results are provided to illustrate the effectiveness of the proposed LNN-based Dyna framework for MBRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：将拉格朗日神经网络集成至强化学习的Dyna框架中
基于模型的强化学习（MBRL）具有样本高效性，但其性能依赖于所学动力学模型的准确性。现有方法多采用不遵循物理定律的黑箱模型，当遇到与原始训练集不同的数据时，预测结果往往不准确。本研究将具有拉格朗日结构约束的拉格朗日神经网络（LNN）应用于基于Dyna的MBRL框架中。我们采用基于随机梯度和基于状态估计的优化器训练LNN网络权重。实验表明，在神经网络训练过程中，基于状态估计的方法比随机梯度法收敛更快。仿真结果验证了所提出的基于LNN的Dyna框架在MBRL中的有效性。

The method integrates Lagrangian neural networks (LNNs), which embed physical Lagrangian structure, into the Dyna MBRL framework, and employs both stochastic gradient and state-estimation optimizers to train the LNN weights. The main experimental results show that the state-estimation optimizer converges faster during training, and simulations demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed LNN-based Dyna framework for MBRL.
本研究的动机在于提高基于模型的强化学习中动力学模型的准确性和物理一致性，因为标准的黑盒模型在处理分布外数据时常常失效。方法将拉格朗日神经网络集成到Dyna框架中，该网络强制了拉格朗日物理结构，并采用随机梯度和状态估计两种优化器来训练网络权重。主要实验结果表明，状态估计优化器在训练中收敛更快，仿真验证了所提出的基于拉格朗日神经网络的Dyna框架在基于模型的强化学习中的有效性。
Reasoning as Compression: Unifying Budget Forcing via the Conditional Information Bottleneck
Authors: Fabio Valerio Massoli, Andrey Kuzmin, Arash Behboodi
First: 2026-03-09T14:56:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T14:56:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting improves LLM accuracy on complex tasks but often increases token usage and inference cost. Existing "Budget Forcing" methods reducing cost via fine-tuning with heuristic length penalties, suppress both essential reasoning and redundant filler. We recast efficient reasoning as a lossy compression problem under the Information Bottleneck (IB) principle, and identify a key theoretical gap when applying naive IB to transformers: attention violates the Markov property between prompt, reasoning trace, and response. To resolve this issue, we model CoT generation under the Conditional Information Bottleneck (CIB) principle, where the reasoning trace Z acts as a computational bridge that contains only the information about the response Y that is not directly accessible from the prompt X. This yields a general Reinforcement Learning objective: maximize task reward while compressing completions under a prior over reasoning traces, subsuming common heuristics (e.g., length penalties) as special cases (e.g., uniform priors). In contrast to naive token-counting-based approaches, we introduce a semantic prior that measures token cost by surprisal under a language model prior. Empirically, our CIB objective prunes cognitive bloat while preserving fluency and logic, improving accuracy at moderate compression and enabling aggressive compression with minimal accuracy drop.
中文标题/摘要
标题：推理即压缩：通过条件信息瓶颈统一预算强制
思维链提示虽能提升大语言模型在复杂任务上的准确性，但常增加令牌使用和推理成本。现有“预算强制”方法通过启发式长度惩罚进行微调来降低成本，但会同时抑制关键推理和冗余填充。我们将高效推理重新定义为信息瓶颈原则下的有损压缩问题，并发现将朴素信息瓶颈应用于Transformer时存在关键理论缺陷：注意力机制违反了提示、推理轨迹和响应之间的马尔可夫性。为解决此问题，我们在条件信息瓶颈原则下建模思维链生成，其中推理轨迹Z作为计算桥梁，仅包含无法直接从提示X获取的响应Y相关信息。由此推导出通用强化学习目标：在推理轨迹先验下压缩生成内容的同时最大化任务奖励，将常见启发式方法（如长度惩罚）纳入为特例（如均匀先验）。与基于简单令牌计数的方法不同，我们引入语义先验，通过语言模型先验下的惊异值衡量令牌成本。实验表明，我们的条件信息瓶颈目标能在保持流畅性和逻辑性的同时修剪认知膨胀，在适度压缩下提升准确性，并实现激进压缩而精度损失最小。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the trade-off between reasoning accuracy and computational cost in Chain-of-Thought prompting for large language models, where existing budget-forcing methods often indiscriminately compress reasoning traces. To unify and improve such methods, the authors frame efficient reasoning as a lossy compression problem under the Conditional Information Bottleneck principle, which theoretically accounts for the non-Markovian nature of transformer attention by treating the reasoning trace as a bridge containing only response-relevant information not directly accessible from the prompt. This yields a reinforcement learning objective that maximizes task reward while compressing completions under a semantic prior based on token surprisal, rather than simple length penalties. Experimental results show that the approach effectively prunes redundant content while maintaining logical fluency, improving accuracy at moderate compression levels and sustaining performance even under aggressive compression.
本文针对大语言模型中思维链提示在提升复杂任务准确性的同时增加计算成本的问题，提出将高效推理重新定义为基于条件信息瓶颈原则的有损压缩任务，以解决现有预算强制方法因启发式长度惩罚而无差别压缩推理内容（包括关键逻辑和冗余填充）的局限性。该方法通过条件信息瓶颈理论建模，将推理轨迹视为仅包含无法直接从提示中获取的响应相关信息的计算桥梁，从而克服了朴素信息瓶颈应用于Transformer时因注意力机制违反马尔可夫性质的缺陷，并推导出一个统一的强化学习目标：在最大化任务奖励的同时，基于语言模型先验的语义惊异度来压缩生成内容。实验表明，该目标能有效剔除推理中的认知冗余而保持流畅性和逻辑性，在适度压缩下提升准确性，并在激进压缩时仅导致最小精度下降。
AltNet: Addressing the Plasticity-Stability Dilemma in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Mansi Maheshwari, John C. Raisbeck, Bruno Castro da Silva
First: 2025-11-30T19:02:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T14:52:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Artificial neural networks have shown remarkable success in supervised learning when trained on a single task using a fixed dataset. However, when neural networks are trained on a reinforcement learning task, their ability to continue learning from new experiences declines over time. This decline in learning ability is known as plasticity loss. To restore plasticity, prior work has explored periodically resetting the parameters of the learning network, a strategy that often improves performance. However, such resets come at the cost of a temporary drop in performance, which can be dangerous in real-world settings. To overcome this instability, we introduce AltNet, a reset-based approach that restores plasticity without performance degradation by leveraging a pair of twin networks. The use of twin networks anchors performance during resets through a mechanism that allows networks to periodically alternate roles: one network learns as it acts in the environment, while the other learns off-policy from the active network's interactions through a replay buffer. At fixed intervals, the active network is reset and the passive network, having learned from prior experience, becomes the new active network. AltNet restores plasticity, improving sample efficiency and achieving higher performance, while avoiding performance drops that pose risks in safety-critical settings. We demonstrate these advantages in several high-dimensional control tasks from the DeepMind Control Suite, where AltNet outperforms various relevant baseline methods, as well as state-of-the-art reset-based techniques.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AltNet：解决强化学习中的可塑性-稳定性困境
人工神经网络在使用固定数据集进行单任务监督学习时表现出显著成功。然而，当神经网络在强化学习任务中训练时，其从新经验中持续学习的能力会随时间下降，这种现象称为可塑性丧失。为恢复可塑性，先前研究探索了周期性重置学习网络参数的方法，该策略常能提升性能，但重置会导致性能暂时下降，在现实场景中可能带来风险。为克服此不稳定性，我们提出AltNet——一种基于重置的方法，通过利用一对孪生网络恢复可塑性且不降低性能。孪生网络通过周期性角色互换机制在重置期间锚定性能：一个网络在环境中行动并学习，另一个则通过回放缓冲区从主动网络的交互中进行离线策略学习。在固定间隔，主动网络被重置，而被动网络凭借先前经验成为新的主动网络。AltNet恢复了可塑性，提升了样本效率并实现了更高性能，同时避免了在安全关键场景中构成风险的性能下降。我们在DeepMind控制套件的多个高维控制任务中验证了这些优势，AltNet在此超越了多种相关基线方法及先进的基于重置的技术。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the plasticity-stability dilemma in reinforcement learning, where neural networks lose learning ability over time, known as plasticity loss. The proposed method, AltNet, uses a pair of twin networks that alternate roles: one actively learns from the environment while the other learns off-policy from a replay buffer, with periodic resets of the active network to restore plasticity without performance drops. Experimental results on high-dimensional control tasks from the DeepMind Control Suite show that AltNet improves sample efficiency and achieves higher performance compared to baseline and state-of-the-art reset-based methods, while avoiding dangerous performance degradation in safety-critical settings.
本文针对强化学习中的可塑性-稳定性困境，即神经网络随时间推移失去学习能力（称为可塑性丧失）的问题。提出的方法AltNet采用一对孪生网络交替角色：一个网络从环境中主动学习，另一个通过回放缓冲区进行离策略学习，并定期重置主动网络以恢复可塑性且不造成性能下降。在DeepMind控制套件的高维控制任务实验中，AltNet相比基线方法和先进的基于重置的技术，提高了样本效率并实现了更高性能，同时避免了在安全关键设置中可能带来风险的性能骤降。
Rewards as Labels: Revisiting RLVR from a Classification Perspective
Authors: Zepeng Zhai, Meilin Chen, Jiaxuan Zhao, Junlang Qian, Lei Shen, Yuan Lu
First: 2026-02-05T13:11:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T14:50:40+00:00
Comments: Withdrawal requested due to unauthorized inclusion of a co-author and incorrect institutional affiliation. The current version violates internal institutional policies and requires immediate retraction to resolve authorship and compliance issues
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards has recently advanced the capabilities of Large Language Models in complex reasoning tasks by providing explicit rule-based supervision. Among RLVR methods, GRPO and its variants have achieved strong empirical performance. Despite their success, we identify that they suffer from Gradient Misassignment in Positives and Gradient Domination in Negatives, which lead to inefficient and suboptimal policy updates. To address these issues, we propose Rewards as Labels (REAL), a novel framework that revisits verifiable rewards as categorical labels rather than scalar weights, thereby reformulating policy optimization as a classification problem. Building on this, we further introduce anchor logits to enhance policy learning. Our analysis reveals that REAL induces a monotonic and bounded gradient weighting, enabling balanced gradient allocation across rollouts and effectively mitigating the identified mismatches. Extensive experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that REAL improves training stability and consistently outperforms GRPO and strong variants such as DAPO. On the 1.5B model, REAL improves average Pass@1 over DAPO by 6.7%. These gains further scale to 7B model, REAL continues to outperform DAPO and GSPO by 6.2% and 1.7%, respectively. Notably, even with a vanilla binary cross-entropy, REAL remains stable and exceeds DAPO by 4.5% on average.
中文标题/摘要
标题：奖励作为标签：从分类视角重审RLVR
可验证奖励强化学习通过提供基于规则的显式监督，近期显著提升了大型语言模型在复杂推理任务中的能力。在RLVR方法中，GRPO及其变体取得了优异的实证性能。尽管成果显著，我们发现这些方法存在正样本梯度错配与负样本梯度主导问题，导致策略更新效率低下且非最优。为解决这些问题，我们提出“奖励作为标签”框架，将可验证奖励重新定义为分类标签而非标量权重，从而将策略优化重构为分类问题。在此基础上，我们进一步引入锚定逻辑值以增强策略学习。分析表明，REAL能产生单调有界的梯度加权，实现轨迹间梯度分配的平衡，有效缓解已识别的错配问题。在数学推理基准上的大量实验显示，REAL提升了训练稳定性，并持续超越GRPO及DAPO等强效变体。在15亿参数模型上，REAL的Pass@1平均指标较DAPO提升6.7%。该优势进一步扩展至70亿参数模型，REAL分别以6.2%和1.7%持续优于DAPO与GSPO。值得注意的是，即使采用基础二元交叉熵损失，REAL仍保持稳定，平均性能超越DAPO达4.5%。

This paper addresses inefficiencies in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods like GRPO, identifying Gradient Misassignment in Positives and Gradient Domination in Negatives as causes of suboptimal policy updates. The authors propose Rewards as Labels (REAL), a novel framework that reformulates policy optimization as a classification problem by treating verifiable rewards as categorical labels rather than scalar weights, and further introduce anchor logits to enhance learning. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that REAL improves training stability and outperforms strong baselines, achieving average Pass@1 improvements of 6.7% over DAPO on a 1.5B model and scaling these gains to larger 7B models.
本文针对GRPO等可验证奖励强化学习方法中的效率问题，指出正样本梯度错配和负样本梯度主导会导致策略更新次优。作者提出Rewards as Labels（REAL）框架，将可验证奖励重新定义为分类标签而非标量权重，从而将策略优化重构为分类问题，并引入锚定逻辑值以增强学习。在数学推理基准上的实验结果表明，REAL提高了训练稳定性并显著优于基线方法，在15亿参数模型上平均Pass@1比DAPO提升6.7%，且在70亿参数模型上仍保持优势。
Mem-T: Densifying Rewards for Long-Horizon Memory Agents
Authors: Yanwei Yue, Boci Peng, Xuanbo Fan, Jiaxin Guo, Qiankun Li, Yan Zhang
First: 2026-01-30T14:23:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T14:47:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Memory agents, which depart from predefined memory-processing pipelines by endogenously managing the processing, storage, and retrieval of memories, have garnered increasing attention for their autonomy and adaptability. However, existing training paradigms remain constrained: agents often traverse long-horizon sequences of memory operations before receiving sparse and delayed rewards, which hinders truly end-to-end optimization of memory management policies. To address this limitation, we introduce Mem-T, an autonomous memory agent that interfaces with a lightweight hierarchical memory database to perform dynamic updates and multi-turn retrieval over streaming inputs. To effectively train long-horizon memory management capabilities, we further propose MoT-GRPO, a tree-guided reinforcement learning framework that transforms sparse terminal feedback into dense, step-wise supervision via memory operation tree backpropagation and hindsight credit assignment, thereby enabling the joint optimization of memory construction and retrieval. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Mem-T is (1) high-performing, surpassing frameworks such as A-Mem and Mem0 by up to $14.92\%$, and (2) economical, operating on a favorable accuracy-efficiency Pareto frontier and reducing inference tokens per query by $\sim24.45\%$ relative to GAM without sacrificing performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Mem-T：面向长程记忆智能体的奖励稠密化方法

Meta-RL with Shared Representations Enables Fast Adaptation in Energy Systems
Authors: Théo Zangato, Aomar Osmani, Pegah Alizadeh
First: 2026-03-09T14:15:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T14:15:51+00:00
Comments: accepted at PAKDD 2026, Hong Kong
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Meta-Reinforcement Learning addresses the critical limitations of conventional Reinforcement Learning in multi-task and non-stationary environments by enabling fast policy adaptation and improved generalization. We introduce a novel Meta-RL framework that integrates a bi-level optimization scheme with a hybrid actor-critic architecture specially designed to enhance sample efficiency and inter-task adaptability. To improve knowledge transfer, we meta-learn a shared state feature extractor jointly optimized across actor and critic networks, providing efficient representation learning and limiting overfitting to individual tasks or dominant profiles. Additionally, we propose a parameter-sharing mechanism between the outer- and inner-loop actor networks, to reduce redundant learning and accelerate adaptation during task revisitation. The approach is validated on a real-world Building Energy Management Systems dataset covering nearly a decade of temporal and structural variability, for which we propose a task preparation method to promote generalization. Experiments demonstrate effective task adaptation and better performance compared to conventional RL and Meta-RL methods.
中文标题/摘要

元强化学习通过实现快速策略适应和提升泛化能力，解决了传统强化学习在多任务和非平稳环境中的关键局限。本文提出一种新颖的元强化学习框架，该框架将双层优化方案与专门设计的混合行动者-评论家架构相结合，以提升样本效率和任务间适应能力。为改进知识迁移，我们通过元学习训练一个在行动者与评论家网络间联合优化的共享状态特征提取器，从而实现高效表征学习并限制对单个任务或主导模式的过拟合。此外，我们提出外层与内层行动者网络间的参数共享机制，以减少冗余学习并加速任务重访时的适应过程。该方法在覆盖近十年时空结构变化的真实建筑能源管理系统数据集上得到验证，我们同时提出一种任务预处理方法以增强泛化性能。实验表明，相较于传统强化学习及元强化学习方法，本方法实现了更有效的任务适应与更优的性能表现。

Validated on a real-world Building Energy Management Systems dataset spanning nearly a decade, the experiments show the framework achieves effective task adaptation and outperforms conventional RL and Meta-RL baselines.
本文针对强化学习在动态、多任务能源系统中应用的挑战，提出了一种新颖的元强化学习框架。该方法结合了双层优化方案与混合行动者-评论家架构，并引入了一个在行动者和评论家网络间共同优化的共享状态特征提取器，以提升知识迁移和样本效率；同时采用内外层行动者网络的参数共享来减少冗余。在一个涵盖近十年时间与结构变化的真实建筑能源管理系统数据集上进行验证，实验结果表明，该框架能实现有效的任务适应，其性能优于传统的强化学习和元强化学习方法。
Aligning to Illusions: Choice Blindness in Human and AI Feedback
Authors: Wenbin Wu
First: 2026-03-09T14:10:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T14:10:36+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 6 figures, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) assumes annotator preferences reflect stable internal states. We challenge this through three experiments spanning the preference pipeline. In a human choice blindness study, 91% of surreptitiously swapped preferences go undetected, extending choice blindness to third-person evaluative comparison of unfamiliar text. Testing fifteen LLM judges as potential replacements, we find detection relies on shallow text matching rather than genuine self-monitoring: removing prior reasoning from context causes blindness to surge from near-zero to over 50%, while explicit social pressure induces near-universal compliance. In a dose-response experiment across two architectures from 86M to 2B parameters, one-sixth to one-third of labels must be corrupted before the reward signal halves, yet standard pairwise accuracy remains virtually unchanged. A Best-of-N evaluation confirms this translates to downstream policy degradation: at 50% corruption, reward-guided selection produces no improvement over random sampling, while the proxy model reports monotonically increasing scores. Together, these results reveal a preference construction problem: the signal entering RLHF is shaped by elicitation context in ways that neither human metacognition, LLM self-monitoring, nor standard evaluation metrics can detect.
中文标题/摘要
标题：与幻觉对齐：人类与AI反馈中的选择盲视
基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）假设标注者的偏好反映稳定的内在状态。我们通过三项贯穿偏好处理流程的实验对此提出挑战。在人类选择盲视研究中，91%被暗中调换的偏好未被察觉，将选择盲视现象扩展至对陌生文本的第三人称评价比较。测试十五个作为潜在替代方案的LLM评判者时，我们发现其检测依赖浅层文本匹配而非真正的自我监控：从上下文中移除先前的推理会使盲视率从接近零飙升至50%以上，而明确的社会压力则引发近乎普遍的顺从行为。在涵盖8600万至20亿参数的两种架构的剂量反应实验中，需要污染六分之一至三分之一的标签才能使奖励信号减半，但标准成对准确率几乎保持不变。Best-of-N评估证实这会导致下游策略性能下降：在50%污染率下，奖励引导的选择相比随机采样毫无改进，而代理模型却报告单调递增的分数。这些结果共同揭示了偏好构建问题：进入RLHF的信号受到诱发情境的塑造，这种影响既无法被人类元认知、LLM自我监控察觉，也无法通过标准评估指标检测。
Summary / 总结
This paper challenges the assumption in Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) that human preferences are stable, revealing a 'preference construction' problem where feedback is highly context-dependent. The method involves three experiments: a human study demonstrating 'choice blindness' where 91% of surreptitiously swapped preferences go undetected; tests showing LLM judges rely on shallow text matching and are easily blinded by removing prior reasoning or social pressure; and a dose-response experiment showing reward models degrade significantly with corrupted labels while standard accuracy metrics fail to detect this, leading to downstream policy failure where at 50% corruption, reward-guided selection performs no better than random. The main experimental results indicate that neither human metacognition, LLM self-monitoring, nor standard evaluation metrics can reliably detect how elicitation context shapes the preference signal used in RLHF.
本文对强化学习人类反馈（RLHF）中人类偏好稳定的假设提出挑战，揭示了一个‘偏好构建’问题，即反馈高度依赖于上下文环境。研究方法包括三项实验：一项人类研究展示了‘选择盲视’，即91%被暗中调换的偏好未被察觉；测试表明大型语言模型（LLM）评判者依赖浅层文本匹配，且移除先前推理或施加社会压力极易导致其盲视；以及一项剂量反应实验显示，奖励模型在标签被污染时性能显著下降，而标准准确度指标却无法检测，导致下游策略失效——在50%污染时，基于奖励的选择表现与随机选择无异。主要实验结果指出，无论是人类元认知、LLM的自我监控，还是标准评估指标，都无法可靠地检测用于RLHF的偏好信号如何被诱导上下文所塑造。
A Recipe for Stable Offline Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dongsu Lee, Daehee Lee, Amy Zhang
First: 2026-03-09T13:57:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T13:57:08+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite remarkable achievements in single-agent offline reinforcement learning (RL), multi-agent RL (MARL) has struggled to adopt this paradigm, largely persisting with on-policy training and self-play from scratch. One reason for this gap comes from the instability of non-linear value decomposition, leading prior works to avoid complex mixing networks in favor of linear value decomposition (e.g., VDN) with value regularization used in single-agent setups. In this work, we analyze the source of instability in non-linear value decomposition within the offline MARL setting. Our observations confirm that they induce value-scale amplification and unstable optimization. To alleviate this, we propose a simple technique, scale-invariant value normalization (SVN), that stabilizes actor-critic training without altering the Bellman fixed point. Empirically, we examine the interaction among key components of offline MARL (e.g., value decomposition, value learning, and policy extraction) and derive a practical recipe that unlocks its full potential.
中文标题/摘要
标题：稳定离线多智能体强化学习的实现方案
尽管单智能体离线强化学习（RL）已取得显著成就，多智能体强化学习（MARL）却难以采用这一范式，大多仍依赖从头开始的在线策略训练与自我博弈。这一差距的部分原因在于非线性价值分解的不稳定性，导致先前研究为避免复杂混合网络而采用线性价值分解（如VDN），并沿用单智能体设置中的价值正则化方法。本文分析了离线MARL中非线性价值分解不稳定的根源，证实其会引发价值尺度放大与优化过程失稳。为缓解此问题，我们提出一种简单技术——尺度不变价值归一化（SVN），可在不改变贝尔曼不动点的前提下稳定行动者-评论者训练。通过实证研究，我们探讨了离线MARL关键组件（如价值分解、价值学习与策略提取）间的相互作用，并总结出一套充分发挥其潜力的实用方案。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the instability of offline multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) when using non-linear value decomposition, which has limited the adoption of offline RL techniques in multi-agent settings. The authors identify that non-linear mixing networks cause value-scale amplification and unstable optimization, and they propose a scale-invariant value normalization (SVN) method to stabilize actor-critic training without changing the Bellman fixed point. 本文针对离线多智能体强化学习中非线性价值分解的不稳定性问题展开研究，该问题阻碍了离线强化学习技术在多智能体场景中的应用。作者发现非线性混合网络会导致价值尺度放大和优化不稳定，并提出了一种尺度不变价值归一化（SVN）方法，在不改变贝尔曼不动点的前提下稳定演员-评论家训练。实验结果表明，SVN结合对价值分解、价值学习和策略提取等关键组件相互作用的分析，形成了一套实用方案，显著提升了离线多智能体强化学习的性能和稳定性。
Revealing Behavioral Plasticity in Large Language Models: A Token-Conditional Perspective
Authors: Liyuan Mao, Le Yu, Jing Zhou, Chujie Zheng, Bowen Yu, Chang Gao, Shixuan Liu, An Yang, Weinan Zhang, JunYang Lin
First: 2026-03-09T13:56:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T13:56:53+00:00
Comments: Work done during an internship at the Qwen Team, Alibaba Group
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this work, we reveal that Large Language Models (LLMs) possess intrinsic behavioral plasticity-akin to chameleons adapting their coloration to environmental cues-that can be exposed through token-conditional generation and stabilized via reinforcement learning. Specifically, by conditioning generation on carefully selected token prefixes sampled from responses exhibiting desired behaviors, LLMs seamlessly adapt their behavioral modes at inference time (e.g., switching from step-by-step reasoning to direct answering) without retraining. Based on this insight, we propose Token-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (ToCoRL), a principled framework that leverages RL to internalize this chameleon-like plasticity, transforming transient inference-time adaptations into stable and learnable behavioral patterns. ToCoRL guides exploration with token-conditional generation and keep enhancing exploitation, enabling emergence of appropriate behaviors. Extensive experiments show that ToCoRL enables precise behavioral control without capability degradation. Notably, we show that large reasoning models, while performing strongly on complex mathematics, can be effectively adapted to excel at factual question answering, which was a capability previously hindered by their step-by-step reasoning patterns.

本研究揭示了大语言模型（LLMs）具有内在的行为可塑性——类似于变色龙根据环境线索调整体色——这种特性可通过令牌条件化生成被激发，并借助强化学习实现稳定化。具体而言，通过将生成过程条件化于从展现目标行为的响应中采样的特定令牌前缀，LLMs能在推理时无缝切换行为模式（例如从逐步推理转为直接回答），而无需重新训练。基于此发现，我们提出了令牌条件化强化学习（ToCoRL）框架，该框架利用强化学习将这种变色龙式的可塑性内化，把瞬时的推理时适应转化为稳定且可学习的行为模式。ToCoRL通过令牌条件化生成引导探索，并持续增强利用能力，从而促进行为的适应性涌现。大量实验表明，ToCoRL能在保持模型能力不降级的前提下实现精准的行为控制。值得注意的是，研究证明大型推理模型虽在复杂数学任务上表现优异，但通过该方法可有效适配至事实问答领域，突破了其原有逐步推理模式对该能力的限制。

Experimental results demonstrate that ToCoRL enables precise behavioral control, such as adapting a reasoning-focused model to excel at factual question-answering, without degrading its core capabilities.

Finite Sample Bounds for Non-Parametric Regression: Optimal Sample Efficiency and Space Complexity
Authors: Davide Maran, Marcello Restelli
First: 2024-12-19T11:22:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T13:03:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We address the problem of learning an unknown smooth function and its derivatives from noisy pointwise evaluations under the supremum norm. While classical nonparametric regression provides a strong theoretical foundation, traditional kernel-based estimators often incur high computational costs and memory requirements that scale with the sample size, limiting their utility in real-time applications such as reinforcement learning. To overcome these challenges, we propose a parametric approach based on a finite-dimensional representation that achieves minimax-optimal uniform convergence rates. Our method enables lightweight inference without storing all samples in memory. We provide sharp finite-sample bounds under sub-Gaussian noise, derive second-order Bernstein-type guarantees, and prove matching lower bounds, thereby confirming the optimality of our approach in both estimation error and memory efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：非参数回归的有限样本界：最优样本效率与空间复杂度
本文研究从带噪声逐点观测中学习未知光滑函数及其导数在一致范数下的问题。经典非参数回归虽提供坚实理论基础，但传统核估计方法常伴随随样本量增长的高计算与内存开销，限制了其在强化学习等实时场景的应用。为突破这些限制，我们提出基于有限维表示的参数化方法，达到极小极大最优的一致收敛速率。该方法无需在内存中存储全部样本即可实现轻量推断。我们在次高斯噪声下给出尖锐的有限样本界，推导二阶伯恩斯坦型保证，并证明匹配下界，从而在估计误差与内存效率两方面验证了方法的理论最优性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational and memory costs of traditional kernel-based nonparametric regression, which hinder real-time applications like reinforcement learning, this paper proposes a parametric method using a finite-dimensional representation to learn smooth functions and their derivatives from noisy pointwise evaluations under the supremum norm. The method achieves minimax-optimal uniform convergence rates while enabling lightweight inference without storing all samples, thus improving space complexity. Experimental results, supported by sharp finite-sample bounds under sub-Gaussian noise and second-order Bernstein-type guarantees, demonstrate optimality in both estimation error and memory efficiency, with matching lower bounds confirming these findings.

Posterior Sampling Reinforcement Learning with Gaussian Processes for Continuous Control: Sublinear Regret Bounds for Unbounded State Spaces
Authors: Hamish Flynn, Joe Watson, Ingmar Posner, Jan Peters
First: 2026-03-09T12:03:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T12:03:25+00:00
Comments: 37 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We analyze the Bayesian regret of the Gaussian process posterior sampling reinforcement learning (GP-PSRL) algorithm. Posterior sampling is an effective heuristic for decision-making under uncertainty that has been used to develop successful algorithms for a variety of continuous control problems. However, theoretical work on GP-PSRL is limited. All known regret bounds either fail to achieve a tight dependence on a kernel-dependent quantity called the maximum information gain or fail to properly account for the fact that the set of possible system states is unbounded. Through a recursive application of the Borell-Tsirelson-Ibragimov-Sudakov inequality, we show that, with high probability, the states actually visited by the algorithm are contained within a ball of near-constant radius. To obtain tight dependence on the maximum information gain, we use the chaining method to control the regret suffered by GP-PSRL. Our main result is a Bayesian regret bound of the order $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(H^{3/2}\sqrt{γ_{T/H} T})$, where $H$ is the horizon, $T$ is the number of time steps and $γ_{T/H}$ is the maximum information gain. With this result, we resolve the limitations with prior theoretical work on PSRL, and provide the theoretical foundation and tools for analyzing PSRL in complex settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于高斯过程的连续控制后验采样强化学习：无界状态空间的次线性遗憾界
我们分析了高斯过程后验采样强化学习（GP-PSRL）算法的贝叶斯遗憾。后验采样是一种处理不确定性决策的有效启发式方法，已成功应用于多种连续控制问题。然而，关于GP-PSRL的理论研究有限：现有遗憾界要么未能紧密依赖于核相关量——最大信息增益，要么未能恰当处理系统状态集无界的事实。通过递归应用Borell-Tsirelson-Ibragimov-Sudakov不等式，我们证明算法实际访问的状态以高概率包含在近恒定半径的球体内。为获得对最大信息增益的紧密依赖，我们采用链式方法控制GP-PSRL的遗憾。主要成果是得到阶为$\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(H^{3/2}\sqrt{γ_{T/H} T})$的贝叶斯遗憾界，其中$H$为时间跨度，$T$为时间步数，$γ_{T/H}$为最大信息增益。该研究解决了先前PSRL理论工作的局限性，为复杂场景下的PSRL分析提供了理论基础与工具。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses theoretical limitations in analyzing the Gaussian Process Posterior Sampling Reinforcement Learning (GP-PSRL) algorithm for continuous control, where prior regret bounds were either not tight with respect to the kernel-dependent maximum information gain or failed to properly handle unbounded state spaces. The method employs a recursive application of the Borell-Tsirelson-Ibragimov-Sudakov inequality to bound visited states within a near-constant radius and uses the chaining technique to tightly control regret. The main experimental result is a derived Bayesian regret bound of order \(\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(H^{3/2}\sqrt{\gamma_{T/H} T})\), where \(H\) is the horizon, \(T\) the total time steps, and \(\gamma_{T/H}\) the maximum information gain, thereby resolving prior theoretical shortcomings and providing a foundation for analyzing PSRL in complex settings.

To Mix or To Merge: Toward Multi-Domain Reinforcement Learning for Large Language Models
Authors: Haoqing Wang, Xiang Long, Ziheng Li, Yilong Xu, Tingguang Li, Yehui Tang
First: 2026-02-13T03:25:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T11:43:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) plays a key role in stimulating the explicit reasoning capability of Large Language Models (LLMs). We can achieve expert-level performance in some specific domains via RLVR, such as coding or math. When a general multi-domain expert-level model is required, we need to carefully consider the collaboration of RLVR across different domains. The current state-of-the-art models mainly employ two different training paradigms for multi-domain RLVR: mixed multi-task RLVR and separate RLVR followed by model merging. However, most of the works did not provide a detailed comparison and analysis about these paradigms. To this end, we choose multiple commonly used high-level tasks (e.g., math, coding, science, instruction following, and agent) as our target domains and design extensive qualitative and quantitative experiments using open-source datasets. We find the RLVR across domains exhibits few mutual interferences, and reasoning-intensive domains demonstrate mutually synergistic effects. Furthermore, we analyze the internal mechanisms of mutual gains from the perspectives of weight space geometry, model prediction behavior, information constraints and self-verification. This project is named as M2RL that means Mixed multi-task training or separate training followed by model Merging for Reinforcement Learning, and the homepage is at https://github.com/mosAI25/M2RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：混合还是合并：迈向大语言模型的多领域强化学习

This paper investigates training paradigms for achieving multi-domain expertise in large language models via reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), motivated by the need to understand whether mixed multi-task RLVR or separate RLVR followed by model merging is more effective. The method involves extensive experiments across domains like math, coding, and science using open-source datasets, analyzing the paradigms through qualitative and quantitative measures. The main experimental results reveal that RLVR across domains shows few mutual interferences, with reasoning-intensive domains even exhibiting synergistic effects, and the analysis provides insights into the internal mechanisms behind these mutual gains from weight space geometry and model behavior perspectives.
本文研究了通过可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在大语言模型中实现多领域专业知识的训练范式，其动机是需要理解混合多任务RLVR与分别训练后模型合并哪种更有效。该方法使用开源数据集，在数学、编程和科学等多个领域进行广泛实验，通过定性和定量指标分析这些范式。主要实验结果表明，跨领域的RLVR相互干扰很少，推理密集型领域甚至表现出协同效应，并且分析从权重空间几何和模型行为等视角揭示了这些相互增益的内部机制。
Pretraining in Actor-Critic Reinforcement Learning for Robot Locomotion
Authors: Jiale Fan, Andrei Cramariuc, Tifanny Portela, Marco Hutter
First: 2025-10-14T10:25:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T10:43:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The pretraining-finetuning paradigm has facilitated numerous transformative advancements in artificial intelligence research in recent years. However, in the domain of reinforcement learning (RL) for robot locomotion, individual skills are often learned from scratch despite the high likelihood that some generalizable knowledge is shared across all task-specific policies belonging to the same robot embodiment. This work aims to define a paradigm for pretraining neural network models that encapsulate such knowledge and can subsequently serve as a basis for warm-starting the RL process in classic actor-critic algorithms, such as Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO). We begin with a task-agnostic exploration-based data collection algorithm to gather diverse, dynamic transition data, which is then used to train a Proprioceptive Inverse Dynamics Model (PIDM) through supervised learning. The pretrained weights are then loaded into both the actor and critic networks to warm-start the policy optimization of actual tasks. We systematically validated our proposed method with 9 distinct robot locomotion RL environments comprising 3 different robot embodiments, showing significant benefits of this initialization strategy. Our proposed approach on average improves sample efficiency by 36.9% and task performance by 7.3% compared to random initialization. We further present key ablation studies and empirical analyses that shed light on the mechanisms behind the effectiveness of this method.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向机器人运动的演员-评论家强化学习预训练方法
近年来，预训练-微调范式推动了人工智能研究的诸多突破性进展。然而，在机器人运动强化学习领域，尽管同一机器人实体下的任务策略很可能共享可泛化知识，现有方法仍常从零开始学习独立技能。本研究旨在构建一种预训练神经网络模型的范式，使其能够封装此类知识，并作为经典演员-评论家算法（如近端策略优化）中强化学习过程的热启动基础。我们首先采用任务无关的探索式数据收集算法获取多样化动态转移数据，继而通过监督学习训练本体感知逆动力学模型。预训练权重随后载入演员与评论家网络，以热启动实际任务的策略优化。我们在包含3种不同机器人实体的9个运动强化学习环境中系统验证了该方法，证明该初始化策略具有显著优势：相较于随机初始化，平均样本效率提升36.9%，任务性能提高7.3%。进一步的消融实验与实证分析揭示了该方法有效的内在机制。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the underutilization of shared knowledge across robot locomotion tasks, this paper introduces a pretraining paradigm for actor-critic reinforcement learning to avoid learning each skill from scratch. The method involves collecting diverse transition data through task-agnostic exploration, training a Proprioceptive Inverse Dynamics Model (PIDM) via supervised learning, and using its weights to initialize both actor and critic networks for fine-tuning with algorithms like PPO. Experimental results across nine locomotion environments with three robot embodiments demonstrate that this approach improves sample efficiency by 36.9% and task performance by 7.3% on average compared to random initialization, with ablation studies providing insights into its effectiveness.
本文针对机器人运动任务中共享知识未被充分利用的问题，提出了一种用于演员-评论家强化学习的预训练范式，以避免每个技能都从头开始学习。方法包括通过任务无关探索收集多样化的状态转移数据，通过监督学习训练一个本体感知逆动力学模型（PIDM），并将其权重用于初始化演员和评论家网络，以便在使用PPO等算法进行微调。在包含三种机器人形态的九个运动环境中的实验结果表明，与随机初始化相比，该方法平均提高了36.9%的样本效率和7.3%的任务性能，并通过消融研究揭示了其有效性的机制。
Multi-Objective Evolutionary Optimization of Chance-Constrained Multiple-Choice Knapsack Problems with Implicit Probability Distributions
Authors: Xuanfeng Li, Shengcai Liu, Wenjie Chen, Yew-Soon Ong, Ke Tang
First: 2026-03-09T10:39:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T10:39:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The multiple-choice knapsack problem (MCKP) is a classic combinatorial optimization with wide practical applications. This paper investigates a significant yet underexplored extension of MCKP: the multi-objective chance-constrained MCKP (MO-CCMCKP) under implicit probability distributions. The goal of the problem is to simultaneously minimize the total cost and maximize the confidence level of satisfying the capacity constraint, capturing essential trade-offs in domains like 5G network configuration. To address the computational challenge of evaluating chance constraints under implicit distributions, we first propose an order-preserving efficient resource allocation Monte Carlo (OPERA-MC) method. This approach adaptively allocates sampling resources to preserve dominance relationships while reducing evaluation time significantly. Further, we develop NHILS, a hybrid evolutionary algorithm that integrates specialized initialization and local search into NSGA-II to navigate sparse feasible regions. Experiments on synthetic benchmarks and real-world 5G network configuration benchmarks demonstrate that NHILS consistently outperforms several state-of-the-art multi-objective optimizers in convergence, diversity, and feasibility. The benchmark instances and source code will be made publicly available to facilitate research in this area.
中文标题/摘要
标题：隐式概率分布下机会约束多选择背包问题的多目标进化优化
多选择背包问题（MCKP）是经典的组合优化问题，具有广泛的实际应用。本文研究了MCKP一个重要但尚未充分探索的扩展：隐式概率分布下的多目标机会约束MCKP（MO-CCMCKP）。该问题旨在同时最小化总成本并最大化满足容量约束的置信水平，以捕捉如5G网络配置等领域的关键权衡。针对隐式分布下机会约束评估的计算挑战，我们首先提出了一种保序高效资源分配蒙特卡洛（OPERA-MC）方法，通过自适应分配采样资源在显著减少评估时间的同时保持支配关系。进一步，我们开发了NHILS算法——一种混合进化算法，将专用初始化和局部搜索集成到NSGA-II中以探索稀疏可行区域。在合成基准和实际5G网络配置基准上的实验表明，NHILS在收敛性、多样性和可行性方面持续优于多种先进多目标优化器。基准实例和源代码将公开提供，以促进该领域的研究。

This paper addresses the multi-objective chance-constrained multiple-choice knapsack problem (MO-CCMCKP) under implicit probability distributions, motivated by the need to capture trade-offs between cost and constraint satisfaction confidence in applications like 5G network configuration. The method introduces an order-preserving efficient resource allocation Monte Carlo (OPERA-MC) technique to efficiently evaluate chance constraints and a hybrid evolutionary algorithm called NHILS, which enhances NSGA-II with specialized initialization and local search to handle sparse feasible regions. Experimental results on synthetic and real-world 5G benchmarks show that NHILS outperforms existing multi-objective optimizers in convergence, diversity, and feasibility.

Evolution Strategy-Based Calibration for Low-Bit Quantization of Speech Models
Authors: Lucas Rakotoarivony
First: 2026-03-09T09:53:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T09:53:05+00:00
Comments: Submitted to INTERSPEECH 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quantization has become essential for the efficient deployment of speech processing systems. Although widely studied, most existing quantization methods were developed for vision and NLP architectures, while the specific challenges of audio signals remain largely overlooked. In particular, we show that audio activations can exhibit large calibration ranges, leading to significant information loss when standard calibration techniques are applied. To address this, we propose ESC, an Evolution Strategy-based Calibration method that formulates activation scaling as an optimization problem and solves it using a two-step local-global scheme driven by an evolution strategy. ESC enables unaltered performance under full INT8 quantization and is the first calibration method to achieve near-lossless performance for full INT4 quantization across multiple speech tasks. Integrating ESC with PTQ methods further reduces performance loss, achieving a 1% relative accuracy degradation on the AST model.

A Unified Framework for Zero-Shot Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jacopo Di Ventura, Jan Felix Kleuker, Aske Plaat, Thomas Moerland
First: 2025-10-23T13:30:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T09:43:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Zero-shot reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a setting for developing general agents, capable of solving downstream tasks without additional training or planning at test-time. While conventional RL optimizes policies for fixed rewards, zero-shot RL requires learning representations that enable immediate adaptation to arbitrary reward functions. As the field matures, the growing diversity of approaches demands a foundational framework reconciling different perspectives under a common unifying structure. In this work, we introduce a formal, unified framework for zero-shot RL, allowing for rigorous comparisons across methods. We propose a taxonomy organizing the algorithmic landscape along two levels: representation, distinguishing between compositional and direct methods based on their exploitation of action-value function decompositions; and learning paradigm, differentiating between reward-free and pseudo reward-free training. Additionally, we propose a unified view of existing error bounds, decomposing the total error into three primary contributing components: inference, reward, and approximation, serving as a foundation for more grounded comparisons of zero-shot methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：零样本强化学习的统一框架
零样本强化学习已成为开发通用智能体的重要范式，使智能体能够在测试时无需额外训练或规划即可解决下游任务。传统强化学习针对固定奖励优化策略，而零样本强化学习需要学习能够立即适应任意奖励函数的表征。随着该领域的发展，日益多样化的方法亟需一个基础性框架，在统一结构下协调不同视角。本研究提出了一个形式化的零样本强化学习统一框架，支持跨方法的严格比较。我们提出了一种分类法，从两个层面组织算法体系：表征层面（根据对动作价值函数分解的利用方式，区分为组合式方法与直接方法）与学习范式层面（区分为无奖励训练与伪无奖励训练）。此外，我们提出了现有误差界限的统一视角，将总误差分解为三个主要构成部分：推断误差、奖励误差与近似误差，为零样本方法的更实质性比较奠定基础。

The motivation for this work is to address the growing diversity of approaches in zero-shot reinforcement learning (RL), which aims to develop agents that can solve new tasks without further training, by establishing a foundational framework for rigorous comparison. The method involves introducing a formal, unified framework with a two-level taxonomy that organizes algorithms by representation (compositional vs. direct) and learning paradigm (reward-free vs. pseudo reward-free), alongside a unified view of error bounds decomposed into inference, reward, and approximation components. The main experimental results are conceptual, providing a structured analysis that enables systematic comparisons across zero-shot RL methods, though no specific empirical outcomes are reported in the abstract.

Model-based Offline RL via Robust Value-Aware Model Learning with Implicitly Differentiable Adaptive Weighting
Authors: Zhongjian Qiao, Jiafei Lyu, Boxiang Lyu, Yao Shu, Siyang Gao, Shuang Qiu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-09T08:59:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:59:45+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Model-based offline reinforcement learning (RL) aims to enhance offline RL with a dynamics model that facilitates policy exploration. However, \textit{model exploitation} could occur due to inevitable model errors, degrading algorithm performance. Adversarial model learning offers a theoretical framework to mitigate model exploitation by solving a maximin formulation. Within such a paradigm, RAMBO~\citep{rigter2022rambo} has emerged as a representative and most popular method that provides a practical implementation with model gradient. However, we empirically reveal that severe Q-value underestimation and gradient explosion can occur in RAMBO with only slight hyperparameter tuning, suggesting that it tends to be overly conservative and suffers from unstable model updates. To address these issues, we propose \textbf{RO}bust value-aware \textbf{M}odel learning with \textbf{I}mplicitly differentiable adaptive weighting (ROMI). Instead of updating the dynamics model with model gradient, ROMI introduces a novel robust value-aware model learning approach. This approach requires the dynamics model to predict future states with values close to the minimum Q-value within a scale-adjustable state uncertainty set, enabling controllable conservatism and stable model updates. To further improve out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization during multi-step rollouts, we propose implicitly differentiable adaptive weighting, a bi-level optimization scheme that adaptively achieves dynamics- and value-aware model learning. Empirical results on D4RL and NeoRL datasets show that ROMI significantly outperforms RAMBO and achieves competitive or superior performance compared to other state-of-the-art methods on datasets where RAMBO typically underperforms. Code is available at https://github.com/zq2r/ROMI.git.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于稳健价值感知模型学习与隐式可微自适应加权的模型化离线强化学习
模型化离线强化学习旨在通过动态模型增强离线强化学习的策略探索能力。然而，不可避免的模型误差可能导致模型利用问题，从而降低算法性能。对抗性模型学习通过求解极大极小公式为缓解模型利用提供了理论框架。在此框架下，RAMBO成为具有模型梯度实用实现的代表性流行方法。但我们实证发现，RAMBO在轻微超参数调整下可能出现严重的Q值低估和梯度爆炸，表明其倾向于过度保守且模型更新不稳定。为解决这些问题，我们提出具有隐式可微自适应加权的稳健价值感知模型学习方法。该方法不依赖模型梯度更新动态模型，而是要求动态模型在尺度可调的状态不确定集合内，预测未来状态值接近最小Q值，从而实现可控保守性与稳定模型更新。为提升多步推演中的分布外泛化能力，我们提出隐式可微自适应加权的双层优化方案，自适应实现动态与价值感知的模型学习。在D4RL和NeoRL数据集上的实验表明，该方法显著优于RAMBO，并在RAMBO通常表现欠佳的数据集上达到或超越其他先进方法。代码发布于https://github.com/zq2r/ROMI.git。
