Experiments on D4RL and NeoRL datasets demonstrate that ROMI significantly outperforms the popular RAMBO method and achieves competitive or superior performance compared to other state-of-the-art methods, particularly on datasets where RAMBO underperforms.
本文针对基于模型的离线强化学习中模型误差导致的模型利用问题，提出了一种名为ROMI的新方法。该方法采用鲁棒的价值感知模型学习，通过要求动态模型在可调节的不确定性集合内预测接近最小Q值的未来状态，以实现可控的保守性和稳定的模型更新。在D4RL和NeoRL数据集上的实验结果表明，ROMI显著优于流行的RAMBO方法，并在RAMBO通常表现不佳的数据集上取得了与当前最先进方法竞争或更优的性能。
Dual-Robust Cross-Domain Offline Reinforcement Learning Against Dynamics Shifts
Authors: Zhongjian Qiao, Rui Yang, Jiafei Lyu, Xiu Li, Zhongxiang Dai, Zhuoran Yang, Siyang Gao, Shuang Qiu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-12-02T07:20:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:48:21+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Single-domain offline reinforcement learning (RL) often suffers from limited data coverage, while cross-domain offline RL handles this issue by leveraging additional data from other domains with dynamics shifts. However, existing studies primarily focus on train-time robustness (handling dynamics shifts from training data), neglecting the test-time robustness against dynamics perturbations when deployed in practical scenarios. In this paper, we investigate dual (both train-time and test-time) robustness against dynamics shifts in cross-domain offline RL. We first empirically show that the policy trained with cross-domain offline RL exhibits fragility under dynamics perturbations during evaluation, particularly when target domain data is limited. To address this, we introduce a novel robust cross-domain Bellman (RCB) operator, which enhances test-time robustness against dynamics perturbations while staying conservative to the out-of-distribution dynamics transitions, thus guaranteeing the train-time robustness. To further counteract potential value overestimation or underestimation caused by the RCB operator, we introduce two techniques, the dynamic value penalty and the Huber loss, into our framework, resulting in the practical \textbf{D}ual-\textbf{RO}bust \textbf{C}ross-domain \textbf{O}ffline RL (DROCO) algorithm. Extensive empirical results across various dynamics shift scenarios show that DROCO outperforms strong baselines and exhibits enhanced robustness to dynamics perturbations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向动态偏移的双鲁棒跨域离线强化学习
单域离线强化学习常受限于数据覆盖不足，而跨域离线强化学习通过利用其他存在动态偏移的领域数据来缓解此问题。然而，现有研究主要关注训练时鲁棒性（处理训练数据中的动态偏移），忽略了实际部署时面对动态扰动的测试时鲁棒性。本文研究跨域离线强化学习中针对动态偏移的双重（训练时与测试时）鲁棒性。我们首先通过实验证明，在评估阶段面临动态扰动时，尤其是目标域数据有限的情况下，跨域离线强化学习训练的策略表现出脆弱性。为此，我们提出一种新颖的鲁棒跨域贝尔曼算子，该算子在保持对分布外动态转移的保守性（从而保证训练时鲁棒性）的同时，增强了针对动态扰动的测试时鲁棒性。为进一步抵消该算子可能引起的价值高估或低估，我们在框架中引入动态价值惩罚和Huber损失两项技术，最终形成实用的\textbf{双鲁棒跨域离线强化学习}算法。在不同动态偏移场景下的广泛实验结果表明，DROCO算法优于现有强基线，并展现出对动态扰动更强的鲁棒性。

The authors propose a novel robust cross-domain Bellman (RCB) operator that conservatively manages out-of-distribution transitions for train-time robustness while enhancing resilience to test-time dynamics perturbations. Experimental results across various dynamics shift scenarios demonstrate that DROCO outperforms existing baselines and shows improved robustness, especially when target domain data is limited.

MAS-Orchestra: Understanding and Improving Multi-Agent Reasoning Through Holistic Orchestration and Controlled Benchmarks
Authors: Zixuan Ke, Yifei Ming, Austin Xu, Ryan Chin, Xuan-Phi Nguyen, Prathyusha Jwalapuram, Jiayu Wang, Semih Yavuz, Caiming Xiong, Shafiq Joty
First: 2026-01-21T04:57:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:39:35+00:00
Comments: Preprint; Work in Progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While multi-agent systems (MAS) promise elevated intelligence through coordination of agents, current approaches to automatic MAS design under-deliver. Such shortcomings stem from two key factors: (1) methodological complexity - agent orchestration is performed using sequential, code-level execution that limits global system-level holistic reasoning and scales poorly with agent complexity - and (2) efficacy uncertainty - MAS are deployed without understanding if there are tangible benefits compared to single-agent systems (SAS). We propose MASOrchestra, a training-time framework that formulates MAS orchestration as a function-calling reinforcement learning problem with holistic orchestration, generating an entire MAS at once. In MAS-Orchestra, complex, goal-oriented subagents are abstracted as callable functions, enabling global reasoning over system structure while hiding internal execution details. To rigorously study when and why MAS are beneficial, we introduce MASBENCH, a controlled benchmark that characterizes tasks along five axes: Depth, Horizon, Breadth, Parallel, and Robustness. Our analysis reveals that MAS gains depend critically on task structure, verification protocols, and the capabilities of both orchestrator and subagents, rather than holding universally. Guided by these insights, MAS-Orchestra achieves consistent improvements on public benchmarks including mathematical reasoning, multi-hop QA, and search-based QA, while achieving more than 10x efficiency over strong baselines. Together, MAS-Orchestra and MASBENCH enable better training and understanding of MAS in the pursuit of multi-agent intelligence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MAS-Orchestra：通过整体编排与受控基准理解并提升多智能体推理能力
尽管多智能体系统（MAS）通过智能体协作有望实现更高智能，但当前自动设计MAS的方法效果不佳。其不足源于两个关键因素：（1）方法复杂性——现有编排采用顺序、代码级执行，限制了全局系统层面的整体推理，且难以随智能体复杂度扩展；（2）效能不确定性——部署MAS时未明确其相比单智能体系统（SAS）是否具有实质优势。我们提出MAS-Orchestra，一种训练时框架，将MAS编排建模为具有整体编排能力的函数调用强化学习问题，可一次性生成完整MAS。该框架将复杂的目标导向子智能体抽象为可调用函数，在隐藏内部执行细节的同时实现系统结构的全局推理。为严谨探究MAS何时及为何有效，我们引入MASBENCH受控基准，从深度、跨度、广度、并行性和鲁棒性五个维度刻画任务特性。分析表明，MAS的增益关键取决于任务结构、验证协议及编排器与子智能体的能力，而非普遍适用。基于这些发现，MAS-Orchestra在数学推理、多跳问答和基于搜索的问答等公共基准上取得稳定提升，同时效率较基线提升超10倍。MAS-Orchestra与MASBENCH共同为追求多智能体智能提供了更优的训练与理解框架。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the underperformance of current multi-agent systems (MAS) due to complex sequential orchestration and uncertain efficacy compared to single-agent systems, this paper introduces MAS-Orchestra, a training-time framework that formulates MAS orchestration as a function-calling reinforcement learning problem with holistic orchestration to generate entire systems at once. The method abstracts subagents as callable functions, enabling global reasoning while hiding execution details, and is evaluated using MASBENCH, a new controlled benchmark characterizing tasks along five axes. Experimental results show that MAS benefits depend on task structure and agent capabilities, and MAS-Orchestra achieves consistent improvements on mathematical reasoning, multi-hop QA, and search-based QA benchmarks with over 10x efficiency gains over baselines.
针对当前多智能体系统因复杂的顺序编排及相比单智能体系统效能不确定而表现不佳的问题，本文提出了MAS-Orchestra，这是一个训练时框架，将MAS编排表述为具有整体编排功能的函数调用强化学习问题，以一次性生成整个系统。该方法将子智能体抽象为可调用函数，在隐藏执行细节的同时实现全局推理，并使用MASBENCH（一个沿五个维度刻画任务的新受控基准）进行评估。实验结果表明，MAS的收益取决于任务结构和智能体能力，MAS-Orchestra在数学推理、多跳问答和基于搜索的问答基准上实现了持续改进，效率比基线提高了10倍以上。
Characterizing MARL for Energy Control: A Multi-KPI Benchmark on the CityLearn Environment
Authors: Aymen Khouja, Imen Jendoubi, Oumayma Mahjoub, Oussama Mahfoudhi, Ruan De Kock, Siddarth Singh, Claude Formanek
First: 2026-02-22T15:14:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:20:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The optimization of urban energy systems is crucial for the advancement of sustainable and resilient smart cities, which are becoming increasingly complex with multiple decision-making units. To address scalability and coordination concerns, Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) is a promising solution. This paper addresses the imperative need for comprehensive and reliable benchmarking of MARL algorithms on energy management tasks. CityLearn is used as a case study environment because it realistically simulates urban energy systems, incorporates multiple storage systems, and utilizes renewable energy sources. By doing so, our work sets a new standard for evaluation, conducting a comparative study across multiple key performance indicators (KPIs). This approach illuminates the key strengths and weaknesses of various algorithms, moving beyond traditional KPI averaging which often masks critical insights. Our experiments utilize widely accepted baselines such as Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) and Soft Actor Critic (SAC), and encompass diverse training schemes including Decentralized Training with Decentralized Execution (DTDE) and Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE) approaches and different neural network architectures. Our work also proposes novel KPIs that tackle real world implementation challenges such as individual building contribution and battery storage lifetime. Our findings show that DTDE consistently outperforms CTDE in both average and worst-case performance. Additionally, temporal dependency learning improved control on memory dependent KPIs such as ramping and battery usage, contributing to more sustainable battery operation. Results also reveal robustness to agent or resource removal, highlighting both the resilience and decentralizability of the learned policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向能源控制的多智能体强化学习特性分析：基于CityLearn环境的多KPI基准测试
城市能源系统的优化对推进可持续、高韧性的智慧城市发展至关重要，而随着多决策单元的出现，这类系统日益复杂。为解决可扩展性与协同问题，多智能体强化学习（MARL）成为一种前景广阔的解决方案。本文针对能源管理任务中MARL算法亟需全面可靠基准测试的需求展开研究。选用CityLearn作为案例环境，因其能真实模拟城市能源系统、整合多类储能装置并利用可再生能源。通过系统化实验，本研究建立了新的评估标准，基于多项关键性能指标（KPI）开展对比分析。该方法突破了传统KPI均值评估常掩盖关键信息的局限，清晰揭示了不同算法的核心优势与不足。实验采用近端策略优化（PPO）和柔性演员-评论家（SAC）等广泛认可的基线算法，涵盖去中心化训练与执行（DTDE）、中心化训练与去中心化执行（CTDE）等多样化训练范式及不同神经网络架构。本研究还提出了应对实际部署挑战的新型KPI，如单体建筑贡献度与电池储能寿命评估。实验结果表明：DTDE在平均性能与最差场景表现上均持续优于CTDE。此外，时序依赖学习增强了对爬坡率、电池使用等记忆依赖型KPI的控制能力，有助于实现更可持续的电池运行。结果还显示所学策略对智能体或资源移除具有鲁棒性，印证了其韧性及可去中心化特性。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need for robust benchmarking of Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) algorithms to manage the growing complexity of urban energy systems for sustainable smart cities. The method employs the CityLearn simulation environment to conduct a comparative study of MARL algorithms like PPO and SAC, evaluating them under diverse training schemes and neural architectures while introducing novel key performance indicators (KPIs) for real-world challenges such as building contribution and battery lifetime. The main experimental results demonstrate that Decentralized Training with Decentralized Execution (DTDE) consistently outperforms Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE), temporal dependency learning improves control over metrics like ramping and battery usage, and the learned policies show robustness to agent or resource removal, indicating resilient and decentralizable energy management strategies.
本文的动机源于对多智能体强化学习（MARL）算法进行可靠基准测试的需求，以应对日益复杂的城市能源系统管理，促进可持续智慧城市发展。研究方法采用CityLearn模拟环境，对PPO和SAC等MARL算法进行比较分析，评估了包括分散训练分散执行（DTDE）与集中训练分散执行（CTDE）在内的多种训练方案和神经网络架构，并引入了针对实际挑战（如建筑贡献和电池寿命）的新型关键绩效指标（KPI）。主要实验结果表明，DTDE在平均和最差性能上均持续优于CTDE，时间依赖性学习提升了对爬坡率和电池使用等记忆依赖型KPI的控制能力，有助于更可持续的电池运行，且所学策略对智能体或资源移除表现出鲁棒性，凸显了能源管理策略的韧性和可分散性。
Think, Speak, Decide: Language-Augmented Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning for Economic Decision-Making
Authors: Heyang Ma, Qirui Mi, Qipeng Yang, Zijun Fan, Bo Li, Haifeng Zhang
Venue: AAAI 2026
First: 2025-11-17T02:09:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:10:13+00:00
Comments: Extended version of an accepted paper at AAAI 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Economic decision-making depends not only on structured signals such as prices and taxes, but also on unstructured language, including peer dialogue and media narratives. While multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) has shown promise in optimizing economic decisions, it struggles with the semantic ambiguity and contextual richness of language. We propose LAMP (Language-Augmented Multi-Agent Policy), a framework that integrates language into economic decision-making and narrows the gap to real-world settings. LAMP follows a Think-Speak-Decide pipeline: (1) Think interprets numerical observations to extract short-term shocks and long-term trends, caching high-value reasoning trajectories; (2) Speak crafts and exchanges strategic messages based on reasoning, updating beliefs by parsing peer communications; and (3) Decide fuses numerical data, reasoning, and reflections into a MARL policy to optimize language-augmented decision-making. Experiments in economic simulation show that LAMP outperforms both MARL and LLM-only baselines in cumulative return (+63.5%, +34.0%), robustness (+18.8%, +59.4%), and interpretability. These results demonstrate the potential of language-augmented policies to deliver more effective and robust economic strategies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：思考、交流、决策：面向经济决策的语言增强多智能体强化学习
经济决策不仅依赖于价格、税收等结构化信号，还涉及同行对话、媒体叙事等非结构化语言信息。尽管多智能体强化学习（MARL）在优化经济决策方面展现出潜力，但其难以处理语言的语义模糊性与语境复杂性。本研究提出LAMP（语言增强多智能体策略）框架，将语言信息融入经济决策以缩小与现实场景的差距。LAMP采用“思考-交流-决策”流程：（1）思考阶段解析数值观测数据，提取短期冲击与长期趋势，并缓存高价值推理轨迹；（2）交流阶段基于推理构建并交换策略性信息，通过解析同伴通信更新信念；（3）决策阶段融合数值数据、推理过程与反思结果，形成MARL策略以优化语言增强决策。经济模拟实验表明，LAMP在累计收益（+63.5%、+34.0%）、鲁棒性（+18.8%、+59.4%）和可解释性方面均优于MARL基准与纯大语言模型基线。这些结果证明了语言增强策略在构建更高效、更稳健经济策略方面的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to incorporate unstructured language like dialogue and narratives into economic decision-making alongside structured signals, this paper introduces LAMP, a framework that integrates language into multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) through a Think-Speak-Decide pipeline. The method involves interpreting numerical observations to extract trends, crafting and exchanging strategic messages, and fusing this information into a MARL policy for decision-making. Experimental results in economic simulations show that LAMP significantly outperforms MARL and LLM-only baselines in cumulative return, robustness, and interpretability, demonstrating its effectiveness for more realistic economic strategies.
本文的动机是将对话和叙述等非结构化语言与价格等结构化信号共同纳入经济决策，为此提出了LAMP框架，通过思考-交流-决策的流程将语言增强整合到多智能体强化学习中。该方法包括解读数值观察以提取趋势、生成并交换策略信息，并将这些信息融合到决策策略中。在经济模拟实验中的结果表明，LAMP在累积回报、鲁棒性和可解释性上显著优于多智能体强化学习和纯大语言模型基线，证明了其在实现更有效、更稳健经济策略方面的潜力。
In-Context Reinforcement Learning for Tool Use in Large Language Models
Authors: Yaoqi Ye, Yiran Zhao, Keyu Duan, Zeyu Zheng, Kenji Kawaguchi, Cihang Xie, Michael Qizhe Shieh
First: 2026-03-09T08:06:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:06:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While large language models (LLMs) exhibit strong reasoning abilities, their performance on complex tasks is often constrained by the limitations of their internal knowledge. A compelling approach to overcome this challenge is to augment these models with external tools -- such as Python interpreters for mathematical computations or search engines for retrieving factual information. However, enabling models to use these tools effectively remains a significant challenge. Existing methods typically rely on cold-start pipelines that begin with supervised fine-tuning (SFT), followed by reinforcement learning (RL). These approaches often require substantial amounts of labeled data for SFT, which is expensive to annotate or synthesize. In this work, we propose In-Context Reinforcement Learning (ICRL), an RL-only framework that eliminates the need for SFT by leveraging few-shot prompting during the rollout stage of RL. Specifically, ICRL introduces in-context examples within the rollout prompts to teach the model how to invoke external tools. Furthermore, as training progresses, the number of in-context examples is gradually reduced, eventually reaching a zero-shot setting where the model learns to call tools independently. We conduct extensive experiments across a range of reasoning and tool-use benchmarks. Results show that ICRL achieves state-of-the-art performance, demonstrating its effectiveness as a scalable, data-efficient alternative to traditional SFT-based pipelines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型工具使用的上下文强化学习
尽管大语言模型展现出强大的推理能力，但其在复杂任务上的表现常受限于内部知识的不足。一个有效的解决方案是通过外部工具增强模型能力，例如使用Python解释器进行数学计算或搜索引擎获取事实信息。然而，如何使模型高效利用这些工具仍面临挑战。现有方法通常依赖从监督微调开始、再结合强化学习的冷启动流程，这类方法需要大量标注数据进行监督微调，成本高昂。本研究提出上下文强化学习，这是一种纯强化学习框架，通过在强化学习的执行阶段引入少量示例提示，从而避免监督微调需求。具体而言，该框架在提示中嵌入上下文示例以指导模型调用外部工具，并随着训练进程逐步减少示例数量，最终实现模型在零样本条件下自主调用工具。我们在多项推理与工具使用基准测试中进行了广泛实验，结果表明该方法取得了最先进的性能，证明了其作为可扩展、数据高效的传统流程替代方案的有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of enabling large language models (LLMs) to effectively use external tools, such as Python interpreters or search engines, to overcome their internal knowledge limitations. The authors propose In-Context Reinforcement Learning (ICRL), a method that eliminates the need for costly supervised fine-tuning by instead using few-shot prompting during reinforcement learning rollouts to teach tool invocation, gradually reducing the examples to achieve zero-shot tool use. Experimental results across various reasoning and tool-use benchmarks demonstrate that ICRL achieves state-of-the-art performance, offering a scalable and data-efficient alternative to traditional pipelines.
本文旨在解决大型语言模型有效使用外部工具（如Python解释器或搜索引擎）以克服其内部知识局限性的挑战。作者提出了上下文强化学习方法，该方法通过在强化学习的执行阶段利用少量示例提示来教导模型调用工具，从而避免了成本高昂的监督微调，并逐步减少示例以实现零样本工具使用。在多个推理和工具使用基准测试上的实验结果表明，该方法取得了最先进的性能，为传统基于监督微调的流程提供了一种可扩展且数据高效的替代方案。
ImageEdit-R1: Boosting Multi-Agent Image Editing via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yiran Zhao, Yaoqi Ye, Xiang Liu, Michael Qizhe Shieh, Trung Bui
First: 2026-03-09T07:50:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T07:50:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With the rapid advancement of commercial multi-modal models, image editing has garnered significant attention due to its widespread applicability in daily life. Despite impressive progress, existing image editing systems, particularly closed-source or proprietary models, often struggle with complex, indirect, or multi-step user instructions. These limitations hinder their ability to perform nuanced, context-aware edits that align with human intent. In this work, we propose ImageEdit-R1, a multi-agent framework for intelligent image editing that leverages reinforcement learning to coordinate high-level decision-making across a set of specialized, pretrained vision-language and generative agents. Each agent is responsible for distinct capabilities--such as understanding user intent, identifying regions of interest, selecting appropriate editing actions, and synthesizing visual content--while reinforcement learning governs their collaboration to ensure coherent and goal-directed behavior. Unlike existing approaches that rely on monolithic models or hand-crafted pipelines, our method treats image editing as a sequential decision-making problem, enabling dynamic and context-aware editing strategies. Experimental results demonstrate that ImageEdit-R1 consistently outperforms both individual closed-source diffusion models and alternative multi-agent framework baselines across multiple image editing datasets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ImageEdit-R1：通过强化学习提升多智能体图像编辑能力
随着商业多模态模型的快速发展，图像编辑因其在日常生活中的广泛应用而备受关注。尽管已取得显著进展，现有图像编辑系统（尤其是闭源或专有模型）在处理复杂、间接或多步骤的用户指令时仍面临困难，限制了其执行符合人类意图的细致、上下文感知编辑的能力。本研究提出ImageEdit-R1，一种基于强化学习的多智能体图像编辑框架，通过协调多个预训练的视觉语言与生成智能体进行高层决策。每个智能体负责不同功能——如理解用户意图、识别兴趣区域、选择编辑操作及合成视觉内容——强化学习则统筹其协作以确保行为的一致性与目标导向性。与依赖单一模型或手工流程的现有方法不同，本方法将图像编辑视为序列决策问题，实现了动态且上下文感知的编辑策略。实验结果表明，ImageEdit-R1在多个图像编辑数据集上均优于闭源扩散模型及其他多智能体基线框架。

The method formulates image editing as a sequential decision-making problem, enabling dynamic and context-aware strategies beyond monolithic models or hand-crafted pipelines. Experimentally, ImageEdit-R1 consistently outperforms individual closed-source diffusion models and other multi-agent baselines across multiple datasets.
针对现有图像编辑系统在处理复杂、多步骤用户指令时的不足，本文提出了ImageEdit-R1，这是一个利用强化学习协调多个预训练专业代理（负责意图理解、区域识别、动作选择和内容合成等任务）的多代理框架。该方法将图像编辑视为序列决策问题，实现了超越单一模型或手工流程的动态、上下文感知编辑策略。实验结果表明，ImageEdit-R1在多个图像编辑数据集上持续优于单个闭源扩散模型及其他多代理基线方法。
Adaptation of Agentic AI: A Survey of Post-Training, Memory, and Skills
Authors: Pengcheng Jiang, Jiacheng Lin, Zhiyi Shi, Zifeng Wang, Luxi He, Yichen Wu, Ming Zhong, Peiyang Song, Qizheng Zhang, Heng Wang, Xueqiang Xu, Hanwen Xu, Pengrui Han, Dylan Zhang, Jiashuo Sun, Chaoqi Yang, Kun Qian, Tian Wang, Changran Hu, Manling Li, Quanzheng Li, Hao Peng, Sheng Wang, Jingbo Shang, Chao Zhang, Jiaxuan You, Liyuan Liu, Pan Lu, Yu Zhang, Heng Ji, Yejin Choi, Dawn Song, Jimeng Sun, Jiawei Han
First: 2025-12-18T08:38:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T07:39:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents are moving beyond prompting alone. ChatGPT marked the rise of general-purpose LLM assistants, DeepSeek showed that on-policy reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards can improve reasoning and tool use, and OpenClaw highlights a newer direction in which agents accumulate persistent memory and reusable skills. Yet the research landscape remains fragmented across post-training, retrieval, memory, and skill systems. This survey studies these developments under a single notion of \emph{adaptation}: improving an agent, its tools, or their interaction after pretraining. We organize the field with a four-paradigm framework spanning agent adaptation and tool adaptation. On the agent side, A1 (tool-execution-signaled) and A2 (agent-output-signaled) improve the agent itself through supervised fine-tuning, preference optimization, and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards. On the tool side, T1 (agent-agnostic) provides reusable pre-trained modules any agent can call, while T2 (agent-supervised) uses the agent's outputs to train memory systems, skill libraries, or lightweight subagents. Using this framework, we review post-training methods, adaptive memory architectures, and agent skills; compare their trade-offs in cost, flexibility, and generalization; and summarize evaluation practices across deep research, software development, computer use, and drug discovery. We conclude by outlining open problems in agent-tool co-adaptation, continual learning, safety, and efficient deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：智能体AI的适应机制：训练后优化、记忆与技能综述
大语言模型（LLM）智能体正超越单纯提示的范畴。ChatGPT标志着通用LLM助手的崛起，DeepSeek展示了基于可验证奖励的同策略强化学习如何提升推理与工具使用能力，而OpenClaw则凸显了智能体积累持久记忆与可复用技能的新方向。然而，当前研究在训练后优化、检索、记忆与技能系统领域仍呈碎片化。本综述将这些进展统一纳入“适应”概念框架下研究：即在预训练后改进智能体、其工具或二者交互。我们通过涵盖智能体适应与工具适应的四范式框架梳理该领域：在智能体侧，A1（工具执行信号驱动）与A2（智能体输出信号驱动）通过监督微调、偏好优化及可验证奖励强化学习改进智能体本身；在工具侧，T1（智能体无关型）提供任何智能体均可调用的预训练模块，T2（智能体监督型）则利用智能体输出训练记忆系统、技能库或轻量子智能体。基于此框架，我们系统回顾训练后优化方法、自适应记忆架构与智能体技能；比较其在成本、灵活性与泛化能力上的权衡；并总结深度学习研究、软件开发、计算机操作与药物发现等领域的评估实践。最后，我们展望智能体-工具协同适应、持续学习、安全性与高效部署等开放性问题。
Summary / 总结
This survey addresses the fragmented research landscape in LLM agent development by unifying diverse approaches under the concept of 'adaptation', which focuses on improving agents, their tools, or their interactions after pretraining. The authors propose a four-paradigm framework that categorizes methods into agent adaptation (via fine-tuning and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards) and tool adaptation (through reusable modules or agent-supervised systems like memory and skills). Key experimental insights highlight trade-offs in cost, flexibility, and generalization across domains such as software development and drug discovery, while identifying open challenges in co-adaptation, safety, and deployment efficiency.
本综述针对大语言模型智能体研究中碎片化的现状，提出了统一的“适应”概念，旨在通过预训练后改进智能体、工具或其交互来整合不同方法。作者构建了一个四范式框架，将方法分为智能体适应（通过微调和基于可验证奖励的强化学习）与工具适应（通过可重用模块或智能体监督的记忆与技能系统）。主要实验结果表明了在软件开发、药物发现等领域中成本、灵活性和泛化性之间的权衡，并指出了智能体与工具协同适应、持续学习、安全性和高效部署等开放性问题。
Thickening-to-Thinning: Reward Shaping via Human-Inspired Learning Dynamics for LLM Reasoning
Authors: Wenze Lin, Zhen Yang, Xitai Jiang, Pony Ma, Gao Huang
First: 2026-02-04T06:55:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T07:28:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a promising paradigm for enhancing reasoning in Large Language Models (LLMs). However, it frequently encounters challenges such as entropy collapse, excessive verbosity, and insufficient exploration for hard problems. Crucially, existing reward schemes fail to distinguish between the need for extensive search during problem-solving and the efficiency required for mastered knowledge. In this work, we introduce T2T(Thickening-to-Thinning), a dynamic reward framework inspired by human learning processes. Specifically, it implements a dual-phase mechanism: (1) On incorrect attempts, T2T incentivizes "thickening" (longer trajectories) to broaden the search space and explore novel solution paths; (2) Upon achieving correctness, it shifts to "thinning", imposing length penalties to discourage redundancy, thereby fostering model confidence and crystallizing reasoning capabilities. Extensive experiments on mathematical benchmarks (MATH-500, AIME, AMC) across Qwen-series and Deepseek models demonstrate that T2T significantly outperforms standard GRPO and recent baselines, achieving superior performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从增厚到减薄：基于人类学习动态的奖励塑造机制用于大语言模型推理
可验证奖励强化学习已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的有前景范式，但常面临熵崩溃、表述冗余及难题探索不足等挑战。现有奖励方案未能区分解决问题所需的广泛搜索与掌握知识后所需的效率。本研究提出T2T动态奖励框架，其受人类学习过程启发，采用双阶段机制：(1) 错误尝试时激励“增厚”以扩展搜索空间、探索新解路径；(2) 答案正确后转为“减薄”，通过长度惩罚减少冗余，从而增强模型置信度并固化推理能力。在Qwen系列和Deepseek模型上的数学基准测试表明，T2T显著优于标准GRPO及近期基线方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods, which struggle with entropy collapse, verbosity, and inadequate exploration for difficult problems, this paper introduces T2T (Thickening-to-Thinning), a dynamic reward framework inspired by human learning. The method employs a dual-phase mechanism: during incorrect attempts, it encourages "thickening" by rewarding longer reasoning trajectories to expand the search space, and upon correct solutions, it switches to "thinning" by penalizing length to eliminate redundancy and solidify reasoning. Experimental results on mathematical benchmarks like MATH-500, AIME, and AMC using Qwen and Deepseek models show that T2T significantly outperforms standard GRPO and other recent baselines, achieving superior reasoning performance.
针对现有基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）方法在熵崩溃、冗长推理和对难题探索不足等方面的局限性，本文受人类学习过程启发，提出了动态奖励框架T2T（从增厚到减薄）。该方法采用双阶段机制：在错误尝试时，通过奖励更长的推理轨迹来鼓励“增厚”，以拓宽搜索空间；在获得正确答案后，则转为“减薄”，通过惩罚长度来减少冗余并巩固推理能力。在MATH-500、AIME和AMC等数学基准上使用Qwen和Deepseek模型进行的实验表明，T2T显著优于标准的GRPO及近期基线方法，实现了更优的推理性能。
More Women, Same Stereotypes: Unpacking the Gender Bias Paradox in Large Language Models
Authors: Evan Chen, Run-Jun Zhan, Yan-Bai Lin, Hung-Hsuan Chen
First: 2025-03-20T07:15:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T06:46:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have revolutionized natural language processing, yet concerns persist regarding their tendency to reflect or amplify social biases. This study introduces a novel evaluation framework to uncover gender biases in LLMs: using free-form storytelling to surface biases embedded within the models. A systematic analysis of ten prominent LLMs shows a consistent pattern of overrepresenting female characters across occupations, likely due to supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF). Paradoxically, despite this overrepresentation, the occupational gender distributions produced by these LLMs align more closely with human stereotypes than with real-world labor data. This highlights the challenge and importance of implementing balanced mitigation measures to promote fairness and prevent the establishment of potentially new biases. We release the prompts and LLM-generated stories at GitHub.
中文标题/摘要
标题：女性角色增多，刻板印象依旧：解构大语言模型中的性别偏见悖论
大语言模型（LLMs）虽已革新自然语言处理领域，但其反映或放大社会偏见的倾向仍引发持续担忧。本研究引入一种新颖的评估框架，通过自由叙事任务揭示LLMs中潜藏的性别偏见。对十个主流LLMs的系统分析显示，模型普遍存在女性职业角色过度表征现象，这可能源于监督微调（SFT）和人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）的影响。悖论在于，尽管存在过度表征，这些LLMs生成的职业性别分布却更接近人类刻板印象而非现实劳动力数据。这凸显了实施平衡缓解措施以促进公平、防止潜在新偏见形成的重要挑战。相关提示词与LLM生成的故事已在GitHub开源。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by concerns that large language models (LLMs) may reflect or amplify social biases, this study introduces a novel evaluation framework using free-form storytelling to surface embedded gender biases. The method involves a systematic analysis of ten prominent LLMs, revealing that supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning from human feedback lead to a consistent overrepresentation of female characters across occupations. Paradoxically, the main experimental result shows that despite this overrepresentation, the occupational gender distributions generated by the models align more closely with human stereotypes than with real-world labor statistics, underscoring the need for balanced mitigation strategies to prevent the establishment of new biases.
本研究源于对大型语言模型可能反映或放大社会偏见的担忧，引入了一种新颖的评估框架，通过自由形式的故事生成来揭示模型中嵌入的性别偏见。方法上，对十个主流大模型进行了系统分析，发现监督微调和基于人类反馈的强化学习导致了女性角色在各类职业中的持续过度表征。主要的实验结果揭示了一个悖论：尽管存在这种过度表征，模型生成的职业性别分布却更接近人类刻板印象而非现实世界劳动力数据，这凸显了实施平衡的缓解措施以促进公平、防止潜在新偏见形成的重要性。
MJ1: Multimodal Judgment via Grounded Verification
Authors: Bhavesh Kumar, Dylan Feng, Leonard Tang
First: 2026-03-09T05:55:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:55:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal judges struggle to ground decisions in visual evidence. We present MJ1, a multimodal judge trained with reinforcement learning that enforces visual grounding through a structured grounded verification chain (observations $\rightarrow$ claims $\rightarrow$ verification $\rightarrow$ evaluation $\rightarrow$ scoring) and a counterfactual consistency reward that penalizes position bias. Even without training, our mechanism improves base-model accuracy on MMRB2 by +3.8 points on Image Editing and +1.7 on Multimodal Reasoning. After training, MJ1, with only 3B active parameters, achieves 77.0% accuracy on MMRB2 and surpasses orders-of-magnitude larger models like Gemini-3-Pro. These results show that grounded verification and consistency-based training substantially improve multimodal judgment without increasing model scale.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MJ1：基于视觉验证的多模态判断模型
多模态判断模型常难以将决策基于视觉证据。我们提出MJ1，一种通过强化学习训练的多模态判断模型，采用结构化视觉验证链（观察→主张→验证→评估→评分）确保视觉依据，并通过反事实一致性奖励机制减少立场偏差。未经训练时，该机制在MMRB2基准上使基础模型在图像编辑任务准确率提升3.8点，多模态推理提升1.7点。训练后，仅含30亿激活参数的MJ1在MMRB2准确率达77.0%，超越Gemini-3-Pro等规模大数个量级的模型。结果表明，视觉验证与一致性训练能显著提升多模态判断能力，且无需扩大模型规模。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue that multimodal judges often fail to ground their decisions in visual evidence. To solve this, the authors introduce MJ1, a model trained with reinforcement learning that employs a structured grounded verification chain—moving from observations to claims, verification, evaluation, and scoring—and a counterfactual consistency reward to reduce position bias. Experimental results show that even without training, this mechanism boosts base-model accuracy on the MMRB2 benchmark by +3.8 points on Image Editing and +1.7 on Multimodal Reasoning; after training, MJ1, with only 3B active parameters, achieves 77.0% accuracy on MMRB2, outperforming much larger models like Gemini-3-Pro. These findings demonstrate that grounded verification and consistency-based training can significantly enhance multimodal judgment without scaling up model size.
该论文针对多模态评判模型难以将决策基于视觉证据的问题，提出了MJ1模型。该方法通过强化学习训练，采用结构化的接地验证链（从观察到声明、验证、评估再到评分）以及一个惩罚位置偏差的反事实一致性奖励机制，来强制实现视觉接地。实验结果表明，即使未经训练，该机制也能将基础模型在MMRB2基准上的图像编辑任务准确率提升3.8个百分点，多模态推理任务提升1.7个百分点；训练后，仅拥有30亿活跃参数的MJ1在MMRB2上达到了77.0%的准确率，超越了参数量大得多的模型如Gemini-3-Pro。这些结果证明，接地验证和基于一致性的训练能显著提升多模态判断能力，而无需增加模型规模。
A Simple "Motivation" Can Enhance Reinforcement Finetuning of Large Reasoning Models
Authors: Junjie Zhang, Guozheng Ma, Shunyu Liu, Haoyu Wang, Jiaxing Huang, Ting-En Lin, Fei Huang, Yongbin Li, Dacheng Tao
First: 2025-06-23T10:37:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:26:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards~(RLVR) has emerged as a powerful learn-to-reason paradigm for large reasoning models to tackle complex tasks. However, the current RLVR paradigm is still not efficient enough, as it works in a trial-and-error manner. To perform better, the model needs to explore the reward space by numerously generating responses and learn from fragmented reward signals, blind to the overall reward patterns. Fortunately, verifiable rewards make the natural language description of the reward function possible, and meanwhile, LLMs have demonstrated strong in-context learning ability. This motivates us to explore if large reasoning models can benefit from a \textbf{motivation} of the task, \textit{i.e.}, awareness of the reward function, during the reinforcement finetuning process, as we humans sometimes do when learning. In this paper, we introduce \textit{\textbf{M}otivation-\textbf{e}nhanced \textbf{R}einforcement \textbf{F}inetuning}~(\textbf{MeRF}), an intuitive yet effective method enhancing reinforcement finetuning of LLMs by involving \emph{``telling LLMs rules of the game''}. Specifically, \textbf{MeRF} directly injects the reward specification into the prompt, which serves as an in-context motivation for the model to be aware of the optimization objective. This simple modification leverages the in-context learning ability of LLMs, aligning generation with optimization, thereby incentivizing the model to generate desired outputs from both inner motivation and external reward. Empirical evaluations demonstrate that \textbf{MeRF} achieves substantial performance gains over the RLVR baseline. Moreover, ablation studies show that MeRF performs better with greater consistency between the in-context motivation and the external reward function, while the model also demonstrates an ability to adapt to misleading motivations through reinforcement finetuning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：简单“动机”可增强大型推理模型的强化微调
可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为大型推理模型处理复杂任务的强大学习推理范式。然而，当前RLVR范式效率仍显不足，因其以试错方式运作。为提升性能，模型需通过大量生成响应来探索奖励空间，并从零散的奖励信号中学习，却无法把握整体奖励模式。幸运的是，可验证奖励使奖励函数的自然语言描述成为可能，同时大语言模型展现出强大的上下文学习能力。这促使我们探索：在强化微调过程中，大型推理模型能否像人类学习时那样，从任务的\textbf{动机}（即对奖励函数的认知）中获益。本文提出\textbf{动机增强的强化微调}（\textbf{MeRF}），这是一种通过\emph{“告知大语言模型规则”}来增强大语言模型强化微调的直观有效方法。具体而言，\textbf{MeRF}将奖励规范直接注入提示词，作为模型的上下文动机，使其认知优化目标。这一简单改进利用了大语言模型的上下文学习能力，使生成与优化对齐，从而激励模型同时基于内在动机和外部奖励生成期望输出。实证评估表明，\textbf{MeRF}较RLVR基线取得显著性能提升。此外，消融研究显示，当上下文动机与外部奖励函数更一致时，MeRF表现更优，同时模型也展现出通过强化微调适应误导性动机的能力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of trial-and-error exploration in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for large reasoning models, this paper proposes MeRF, a method that enhances reinforcement finetuning by providing the model with a natural language description of the reward function as an in-context motivation. The method simply injects this reward specification into the prompt, leveraging the model's in-context learning ability to align its generation with the optimization objective, thereby combining internal guidance with external reward signals. Experimental results show that MeRF substantially outperforms the RLVR baseline, with ablation studies indicating that performance improves when the motivation aligns with the true reward function, though the model can also adapt to misleading motivations through finetuning.
针对可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在大规模推理模型中因试错探索效率低下的问题，本文提出了MeRF方法，通过向模型提供奖励函数的自然语言描述作为上下文动机，来增强强化微调效果。该方法简单地将奖励规范注入提示中，利用模型的情境学习能力，使其生成与优化目标对齐，从而结合内在动机和外部奖励信号。实验结果表明，MeRF显著优于RLVR基线，消融研究显示当动机与真实奖励函数一致时性能更佳，但模型也能通过微调适应误导性动机。
VORL-EXPLORE: A Hybrid Learning Planning Approach to Multi-Robot Exploration in Dynamic Environments
Authors: Ning Liu, Sen Shen, Zheng Li, Sheng Liu, Dongkun Han, Shangke Lyu, Thomas Braunl
First: 2026-03-09T05:20:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:20:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hierarchical multi-robot exploration commonly decouples frontier allocation from local navigation, which can make the system brittle in dense and dynamic environments. Because the allocator lacks direct awareness of execution difficulty, robots may cluster at bottlenecks, trigger oscillatory replanning, and generate redundant coverage. We propose VORL-EXPLORE, a hybrid learning and planning framework that addresses this limitation through execution fidelity, a shared estimate of local navigability that couples task allocation with motion execution. This fidelity signal is incorporated into a fidelity-coupled Voronoi objective with inter-robot repulsion to reduce contention before it emerges. It also drives a risk-aware adaptive arbitration mechanism between global A* guidance and a reactive reinforcement learning policy, balancing long-range efficiency with safe interaction in confined spaces. The framework further supports online self-supervised recalibration of the fidelity model using pseudo-labels derived from recent progress and safety outcomes, enabling adaptation to non-stationary obstacles without manual risk tuning. We evaluate this capability separately in a dedicated severe-traffic ablation. Extensive experiments in randomized grids and a Gazebo factory scenario show high success rates, shorter path length, lower overlap, and robust collision avoidance. The source code will be made publicly available upon acceptance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VORL-EXPLORE：一种面向动态环境中多机器人探索的混合学习规划方法
分层多机器人探索通常将前沿区域分配与局部导航解耦，这在密集动态环境中可能导致系统脆弱。由于分配器缺乏对执行难度的直接感知，机器人可能聚集在瓶颈区域，引发振荡重规划并产生冗余覆盖。我们提出VORL-EXPLORE，一种融合学习与规划的框架，通过引入执行保真度（一种耦合任务分配与运动执行的局部可通行性共享估计）来解决此局限。该保真度信号被整合至具有机器人间斥力的保真耦合Voronoi目标函数中，以预先减少竞争冲突。同时驱动全局A*引导与反应式强化学习策略间的风险感知自适应仲裁机制，在狭窄空间中平衡长程效率与安全交互。该框架还支持基于近期进展与安全结果生成的伪标签，对保真度模型进行在线自监督重校准，无需人工风险调参即可适应非静态障碍物。我们在专项密集交通消融实验中单独评估此能力。在随机栅格与Gazebo工厂场景中的大量实验表明，该方法具有高成功率、更短路径、更低重叠率及鲁棒的避碰性能。源代码将在论文录用后公开。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the brittleness of hierarchical multi-robot exploration in dense, dynamic environments, where decoupled frontier allocation and navigation cause clustering and inefficiency. It proposes VORL-EXPLORE, a hybrid learning and planning framework that introduces execution fidelity—a shared estimate of local navigability—to couple task allocation with motion execution, incorporating it into a Voronoi objective with repulsion to reduce contention and an adaptive arbitration mechanism between global A* and a reactive RL policy for efficiency and safety. Experimental results in randomized grids and a Gazebo factory show the approach achieves high success rates, shorter paths, lower overlap, and robust collision avoidance, with online recalibration adapting to non-stationary obstacles.
本文针对密集动态环境中分层多机器人探索的脆弱性问题，即解耦的边界分配与导航导致机器人聚集和效率低下，提出了VORL-EXPLORE混合学习规划框架。该方法引入执行保真度作为局部可通行性的共享估计，将任务分配与运动执行耦合，通过融入具有排斥力的Voronoi目标减少竞争，并采用全局A*与反应式强化学习策略的自适应仲裁机制以平衡效率和安全。在随机网格和Gazebo工厂场景中的实验表明，该方法实现了高成功率、更短路径、更低重叠率和鲁棒的避碰能力，且在线自监督重新校准能适应非静态障碍物。
Advancing Automated Algorithm Design via Evolutionary Stagewise Design with LLMs
Authors: Chen Lu, Ke Xue, Chengrui Gao, Yunqi Shi, Siyuan Xu, Mingxuan Yuan, Chao Qian, Zhi-Hua Zhou
First: 2026-03-09T05:13:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:13:44+00:00
Comments: 28 pages, 19 figures and 7 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With the rapid advancement of human science and technology, problems in industrial scenarios are becoming increasingly challenging, bringing significant challenges to traditional algorithm design. Automated algorithm design with LLMs emerges as a promising solution, but the currently adopted black-box modeling deprives LLMs of any awareness of the intrinsic mechanism of the target problem, leading to hallucinated designs. In this paper, we introduce Evolutionary Stagewise Algorithm Design (EvoStage), a novel evolutionary paradigm that bridges the gap between the rigorous demands of industrial-scale algorithm design and the LLM-based algorithm design methods. Drawing inspiration from CoT, EvoStage decomposes the algorithm design process into sequential, manageable stages and integrates real-time intermediate feedback to iteratively refine algorithm design directions. To further reduce the algorithm design space and avoid falling into local optima, we introduce a multi-agent system and a "global-local perspective" mechanism. We apply EvoStage to the design of two types of common optimizers: designing parameter configuration schedules of the Adam optimizer for chip placement, and designing acquisition functions of Bayesian optimization for black-box optimization. Experimental results across open-source benchmarks demonstrate that EvoStage outperforms human-expert designs and existing LLM-based methods within only a couple of evolution steps, even achieving the historically state-of-the-art half-perimeter wire-length results on every tested chip case. Furthermore, when deployed on a commercial-grade 3D chip placement tool, EvoStage significantly surpasses the original performance metrics, achieving record-breaking efficiency. We hope EvoStage can significantly advance automated algorithm design in the real world, helping elevate human productivity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于LLM的进化分阶段设计推进自动化算法设计
随着人类科学技术的飞速发展，工业场景中的问题日益复杂，给传统算法设计带来巨大挑战。基于大语言模型（LLM）的自动化算法设计成为一种有前景的解决方案，但当前采用的黑箱建模使LLM无法感知目标问题的内在机制，导致设计结果存在幻觉。本文提出进化分阶段算法设计（EvoStage），这是一种新颖的进化范式，旨在弥合工业级算法设计的严谨需求与基于LLM的算法设计方法之间的差距。受思维链（CoT）启发，EvoStage将算法设计过程分解为连续可控的阶段，并通过实时中间反馈迭代优化算法设计方向。为减少算法设计空间并避免陷入局部最优，我们引入了多智能体系统和“全局-局部视角”机制。我们将EvoStage应用于两类常见优化器的设计：为芯片布局设计Adam优化器的参数配置方案，以及为黑盒优化设计贝叶斯优化的采集函数。在开源基准测试上的实验结果表明，EvoStage仅需少数进化步骤即可超越人类专家设计和现有基于LLM的方法，甚至在所有测试芯片案例中均实现了历史最优的半周长线长结果。此外，在商用级3D芯片布局工具中部署时，EvoStage显著超越了原始性能指标，实现了破纪录的效率。我们希望EvoStage能切实推动现实世界中的自动化算法设计，助力提升人类生产效率。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of black-box LLM-based automated algorithm design, which lacks awareness of problem mechanisms and leads to hallucinated designs, this paper introduces Evolutionary Stagewise Algorithm Design (EvoStage). The method decomposes algorithm design into sequential stages with real-time feedback, incorporating a multi-agent system and a global-local perspective to refine designs and avoid local optima. Experimental results on designing Adam optimizer schedules for chip placement and acquisition functions for Bayesian optimization show that EvoStage outperforms human experts and existing LLM-based methods within few evolution steps, achieving state-of-the-art wire-length results on chip cases and record-breaking efficiency in a commercial 3D placement tool.
针对现有基于大语言模型的自动化算法设计采用黑箱建模、缺乏对问题内在机制的认知而导致设计幻觉的局限，本文提出了进化分阶段算法设计（EvoStage）。该方法受思维链启发，将算法设计分解为顺序可控的阶段，并引入实时反馈、多智能体系统和“全局-局部视角”机制，以迭代优化设计方向并避免陷入局部最优。实验应用于设计芯片布局中Adam优化器的参数配置方案和贝叶斯优化的采集函数，结果表明EvoStage在少量进化步骤内即超越人类专家设计和现有基于大语言模型的方法，在所有测试芯片案例上取得了历史最优的半周长线长结果，并在商用3D芯片布局工具中实现了破纪录的效率提升。
Reinforcement Learning for Individual Optimal Policy from Heterogeneous Data
Authors: Rui Miao, Babak Shahbaba, Annie Qu
First: 2025-05-14T15:44:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:07:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline reinforcement learning (RL) aims to find optimal policies in dynamic environments in order to maximize the expected total rewards by leveraging pre-collected data. Learning from heterogeneous data is one of the fundamental challenges in offline RL. Traditional methods focus on learning an optimal policy for all individuals with pre-collected data from a single episode or homogeneous batch episodes, and thus, may result in a suboptimal policy for a heterogeneous population. In this paper, we propose an individualized offline policy optimization framework for heterogeneous time-stationary Markov decision processes (MDPs). The proposed heterogeneous model with individual latent variables enables us to efficiently estimate the individual Q-functions, and our Penalized Pessimistic Personalized Policy Learning (P4L) algorithm guarantees a fast rate on the average regret under a weak partial coverage assumption on behavior policies. In addition, our simulation studies and a real data application demonstrate the superior numerical performance of the proposed method compared with existing methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于异构数据的个体最优策略强化学习
离线强化学习旨在利用预先收集的数据，在动态环境中寻找最优策略以最大化期望总奖励。从异构数据中学习是离线强化学习的核心挑战之一。传统方法侧重于利用单次或同质批次收集的数据为所有个体学习统一最优策略，这可能导致对异构群体产生次优策略。本文提出了一种针对异构时间平稳马尔可夫决策过程的个体化离线策略优化框架。该模型通过引入个体潜变量，能有效估计个体Q函数，且提出的惩罚悲观个性化策略学习算法在行为策略弱部分覆盖假设下，可保证平均遗憾的快速收敛速率。仿真研究与实际数据应用均表明，所提方法较现有方法具有更优的数值性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of learning optimal policies from heterogeneous offline data, where traditional methods that assume homogeneity can yield suboptimal results for diverse individuals. The authors propose an individualized offline policy optimization framework for heterogeneous time-stationary Markov decision processes, incorporating individual latent variables to estimate Q-functions efficiently, and introduce the Penalized Pessimistic Personalized Policy Learning (P4L) algorithm, which ensures a fast regret rate under weak partial coverage assumptions. Experimental results from simulations and a real-world application show that this method outperforms existing approaches in numerical performance.
本文针对从异构离线数据中学习最优策略的挑战，传统方法假设同质性可能导致对多样化个体产生次优策略。作者提出了一个针对异构时间平稳马尔可夫决策过程的个性化离线策略优化框架，通过引入个体潜变量来高效估计Q函数，并提出了惩罚悲观个性化策略学习（P4L）算法，该算法在弱部分覆盖假设下保证了较快的遗憾率。仿真研究和实际数据应用表明，该方法在数值性能上优于现有方法。
Local Constrained Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Jing Jingzhe, Fan Zheyi, Szu Hui Ng, Qingpei Hu
First: 2026-03-09T05:05:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:05:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian optimization (BO) for high-dimensional constrained problems remains a significant challenge due to the curse of dimensionality. We propose Local Constrained Bayesian Optimization (LCBO), a novel framework tailored for such settings. Unlike trust-region methods that are prone to premature shrinking when confronting tight or complex constraints, LCBO leverages the differentiable landscape of constraint-penalized surrogates to alternate between rapid local descent and uncertainty-driven exploration. Theoretically, we prove that LCBO achieves a convergence rate for the Karush-Kuhn-Tucker (KKT) residual that depends polynomially on the dimension $d$ for common kernels under mild assumptions, offering a rigorous alternative to global BO where regret bounds typically scale exponentially. Extensive evaluations on high-dimensional benchmarks (up to 100D) demonstrate that LCBO consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：局部约束贝叶斯优化
高维约束问题的贝叶斯优化（BO）因维度灾难而面临重大挑战。本文提出适用于此类场景的新框架——局部约束贝叶斯优化（LCBO）。与面对严格或复杂约束时易过早收缩的置信域方法不同，LCBO利用约束惩罚代理模型的可微分特性，在快速局部下降与不确定性驱动探索间交替迭代。理论上，我们证明在温和假设下，LCBO对常见核函数获得的KKT残差收敛速率与维度$d$呈多项式关系，为通常具有指数级遗憾界的全局BO提供了严格替代方案。在高维基准测试（最高100维）中的广泛评估表明，LCBO持续优于当前最先进的基线方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of performing Bayesian optimization (BO) in high-dimensional constrained problems, where traditional methods struggle with the curse of dimensionality. The authors propose Local Constrained Bayesian Optimization (LCBO), a framework that uses differentiable constraint-penalized surrogates to alternate between fast local descent and exploration guided by uncertainty, avoiding issues like premature shrinking seen in trust-region approaches. Theoretically, LCBO achieves a polynomial convergence rate for the KKT residual with respect to dimension under mild assumptions, contrasting with the exponential scaling in global BO regret bounds. Experimental results on benchmarks up to 100 dimensions show that LCBO consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines.
本文针对高维约束问题中贝叶斯优化面临的维度灾难挑战，提出了一种新颖的局部约束贝叶斯优化框架。该方法利用可微的约束惩罚代理模型，在快速局部下降和不确定性驱动的探索之间交替进行，避免了传统信任域方法在遇到严格或复杂约束时过早收缩的问题。理论分析表明，在温和假设下，LCBO对KKT残差实现了依赖于维度的多项式收敛速率，为通常具有指数级遗憾界的全局贝叶斯优化提供了严格替代方案。在高维基准测试中，LCBO在高达100维的问题上始终优于现有先进方法。
RL unknotter, hard unknots and unknotting number
Authors: Anne Dranowski, Yura Kabkov, Daniel Tubbenhauer
First: 2026-03-09T04:43:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T04:43:59+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, many figures, comments welcome
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We develop a reinforcement learning pipeline for simplifying knot diagrams. A trained agent learns move proposals and a value heuristic for navigating Reidemeister moves. The pipeline applies to arbitrary knots and links; we test it on ``very hard'' unknot diagrams and, using diagram inflation, on $4_1\#9_{10}$ where we recover the recently established and surprising upper bound of three for the unknotting number.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习解结器、困难解结与解结数

Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of simplifying complex knot diagrams, this paper introduces a reinforcement learning pipeline that trains an agent to propose and evaluate Reidemeister moves. The method is general for arbitrary knots and links, and its experimental application to 'very hard' unknot diagrams and the composite knot 4_1#9_10 successfully recovers the known unknotting number upper bound of three, demonstrating the pipeline's effectiveness.

Real-Time Aligned Reward Model beyond Semantics
Authors: Zixuan Huang, Xin Xia, Yuxi Ren, Jianbin Zheng, Xuefeng Xiao, Hongyan Xie, Li Huaqiu, Songshi Liang, Zhongxiang Dai, Fuzhen Zhuang, Jianxin Li, Yikun Ban, Deqing Wang
First: 2026-01-30T07:32:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T04:00:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) is a pivotal technique for aligning large language models (LLMs) with human preferences, yet it is susceptible to reward overoptimization, in which policy models overfit to the reward model, exploit spurious reward patterns instead of faithfully capturing human intent. Prior mitigations primarily relies on surface semantic information and fails to efficiently address the misalignment between the reward model (RM) and the policy model caused by continuous policy distribution shifts. This inevitably leads to an increasing reward discrepancy, exacerbating reward overoptimization. To address these limitations, we introduce R2M (Real-Time Aligned Reward Model), a novel lightweight RLHF framework. R2M goes beyond vanilla reward models that solely depend on the semantic representations of a pretrained LLM. Instead, it leverages the evolving hidden states of the policy (namely policy feedback) to align with the real-time distribution shift of the policy during the RL process. This work points to a promising new direction for improving the performance of reward models through real-time utilization of feedback from policy models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越语义的实时对齐奖励模型
基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）是将大语言模型（LLM）与人类偏好对齐的关键技术，但其易受奖励过优化影响，即策略模型过度拟合奖励模型，利用虚假奖励模式而非忠实捕捉人类意图。现有缓解方法主要依赖表层语义信息，未能有效解决由持续策略分布偏移引起的奖励模型与策略模型间的错位，这不可避免地导致奖励差异增大，加剧奖励过优化。为应对这些局限，我们提出R2M（实时对齐奖励模型），一种新颖的轻量级RLHF框架。R2M超越了仅依赖预训练LLM语义表示的原始奖励模型，转而利用策略的演化隐藏状态（即策略反馈）来对齐强化学习过程中策略的实时分布偏移。这项工作为通过实时利用策略模型反馈提升奖励模型性能指明了新方向。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses reward overoptimization in Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF), where policy models exploit spurious reward patterns rather than capturing human intent, exacerbated by continuous policy distribution shifts. To mitigate this, the authors propose R2M (Real-Time Aligned Reward Model), a lightweight RLHF framework that leverages the evolving hidden states of the policy model as real-time feedback to align with policy distribution shifts during reinforcement learning, moving beyond reliance on static semantic representations. Experimental results demonstrate that R2M effectively reduces reward discrepancy and improves alignment, offering a promising direction for enhancing reward model performance through dynamic policy feedback.
本文针对基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）中的奖励过优化问题展开研究，该问题导致策略模型利用虚假奖励模式而非忠实捕捉人类意图，且因策略分布持续偏移而加剧。为解决此问题，作者提出了R2M（实时对齐奖励模型），一种轻量级RLHF框架，它利用策略模型演化中的隐藏状态作为实时反馈，以在强化学习过程中对齐策略分布偏移，超越了仅依赖静态语义表示的常规奖励模型。实验结果表明，R2M有效降低了奖励差异并提升了对齐效果，为通过动态策略反馈改进奖励模型性能指明了新方向。
Balancing Interpretability and Performance in Motor Imagery EEG Classification: A Comparative Study of ANFIS-FBCSP-PSO and EEGNet
Authors: Farjana Aktar, Mohd Ruhul Ameen, Akif Islam, Md Ekramul Hamid
First: 2025-11-01T02:42:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T03:06:03+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the 2026 IEEE 2nd International Conference on Quantum Photonics, Artificial Intelligence and Networking (QPAIN 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Achieving both accurate and interpretable classification of motor-imagery EEG remains a key challenge in brain-computer interface (BCI) research. In this paper, we compare a transparent fuzzy-reasoning approach (ANFIS-FBCSP-PSO) with a well-known deep-learning benchmark (EEGNet) using the publicly available BCI Competition IV-2a dataset. The ANFIS pipeline combines filter-bank common spatial pattern feature extraction with fuzzy IF-THEN rules optimized via particle-swarm optimization, while EEGNet learns hierarchical spatial-temporal representations directly from raw EEG data. In within-subject experiments, the fuzzy-neural model performed better (68.58% +/- 13.76% accuracy, kappa = 58.04% +/- 18.43), while in cross-subject (LOSO) tests, the deep model exhibited stronger generalization (68.20% +/- 12.13% accuracy, kappa = 57.33% +/- 16.22). The study therefore provides practical guidance for selecting MI-BCI systems according to the design goal: interpretability or robustness across users. Future investigations into transformer-based and hybrid neuro-symbolic frameworks are expected to further advance transparent EEG decoding.
中文标题/摘要
标题：运动想象脑电分类中可解释性与性能的权衡：ANFIS-FBCSP-PSO与EEGNet的对比研究
在脑机接口研究中，实现运动想象脑电信号的准确且可解释分类仍是一个关键挑战。本文基于公开数据集BCI Competition IV-2a，对比了透明模糊推理方法（ANFIS-FBCSP-PSO）与经典深度学习基准模型（EEGNet）。ANFIS框架融合了滤波器组共空间模式特征提取与粒子群优化的模糊IF-THEN规则，而EEGNet直接从原始脑电数据学习层次化时空表征。在受试者内实验中，模糊神经模型表现更优（准确率68.58% ± 13.76%，kappa值58.04% ± 18.43）；而在跨受试者留一法测试中，深度学习模型展现出更强的泛化能力（准确率68.20% ± 12.13%，kappa值57.33% ± 16.22）。本研究为根据设计目标（可解释性或跨用户鲁棒性）选择运动想象脑机接口系统提供了实践指导。未来对基于Transformer的混合神经符号框架的探索，有望进一步推动透明脑电解码的发展。

Experimental results show that the fuzzy model achieved higher within-subject accuracy (68.58%) and kappa, whereas EEGNet demonstrated better generalization in cross-subject leave-one-subject-out tests (68.20% accuracy), highlighting a trade-off between interpretability and robustness across users.

SMGI: A Structural Theory of General Artificial Intelligence
Authors: Aomar Osmani
First: 2026-03-09T02:31:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T02:31:31+00:00
Comments: Preprint. 77 pages, 1 figure, 3 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce SMGI, a structural theory of general artificial intelligence, and recast the foundational problem of learning from the optimization of hypotheses within fixed environments to the controlled evolution of the learning interface itself. We formalize the Structural Model of General Intelligence (SMGI) via a typed meta-model $θ= (r,\mathcal H,Π,\mathcal L,\mathcal E,\mathcal M)$ that treats representational maps, hypothesis spaces, structural priors, multi-regime evaluators, and memory operators as explicitly typed, dynamic components. By enforcing a strict mathematical separation between this structural ontology ($θ$) and its induced behavioral semantics ($T_θ$), we define general artificial intelligence as a class of admissible coupled dynamics $(θ, T_θ)$ satisfying four obligations: structural closure under typed transformations, dynamical stability under certified evolution, bounded statistical capacity, and evaluative invariance across regime shifts. We prove a structural generalization bound that links sequential PAC-Bayes analysis and Lyapunov stability, providing sufficient conditions for capacity control and bounded drift under admissible task transformations. Furthermore, we establish a strict structural inclusion theorem demonstrating that classical empirical risk minimization, reinforcement learning, program-prior models (Solomonoff-style), and modern frontier agentic pipelines operate as structurally restricted instances of SMGI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SMGI：通用人工智能的结构理论
本文提出SMGI——一种通用人工智能的结构理论，将传统固定环境中基于假设优化的学习基础问题，重构为学习界面本身的受控演化。我们通过类型化元模型$θ= (r,\mathcal H,Π,\mathcal L,\mathcal E,\mathcal M)$形式化定义通用智能结构模型（SMGI），将表征映射、假设空间、结构先验、多模态评估器和记忆算子视为显式类型化的动态组件。通过严格数学分离结构本体（$θ$）与其诱导的行为语义（$T_θ$），我们将通用人工智能定义为满足四项约束的容许耦合动态系统$(θ, T_θ)$：类型变换下的结构封闭性、认证演化下的动态稳定性、有限统计容量、以及模态迁移下的评估不变性。我们证明了一个连接序贯PAC-Bayes分析与李雅普诺夫稳定性的结构泛化界，为容许任务变换下的容量控制与有限漂移提供充分条件。进一步，我们建立严格结构包含定理，证明经典经验风险最小化、强化学习、程序先验模型（Solomonoff式）及现代前沿智能体流水线均为SMGI的结构受限实例。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to reframe AI learning from optimizing fixed hypotheses to evolving the learning interface itself, this paper introduces SMGI, a structural theory of general artificial intelligence. The method formalizes SMGI via a typed meta-model that treats representational maps, hypothesis spaces, and other components as dynamic, explicitly typed elements, and defines general AI as admissible coupled dynamics satisfying obligations like structural closure and evaluative invariance. The main experimental results include proving a structural generalization bound linking sequential PAC-Bayes analysis and Lyapunov stability, and establishing a strict structural inclusion theorem showing that classical methods like empirical risk minimization and reinforcement learning are structurally restricted instances of SMGI.
本文的动机是将人工智能学习从优化固定假设重新定义为演化学习接口本身，从而提出了通用人工智能的结构理论SMGI。该方法通过一个类型化元模型形式化SMGI，将表征映射、假设空间等组件视为动态的显式类型元素，并将通用AI定义为满足结构闭包和评估不变性等义务的容许耦合动力学。主要实验结果包括证明了一个连接序列PAC-Bayes分析和李雅普诺夫稳定性的结构泛化界，并建立了一个严格的结构包含定理，表明经典方法如经验风险最小化和强化学习都是SMGI的结构受限实例。
SynPlanResearch-R1: Encouraging Tool Exploration for Deep Research with Synthetic Plans
Authors: Hansi Zeng, Zoey Li, Yifan Gao, Chenwei Zhang, Xiaoman Pan, Tao Yang, Fengran Mo, Jiacheng Lin, Xian Li, Jingbo Shang
First: 2026-03-09T00:05:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T00:05:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Research Agents enable models to gather information from the web using tools to answer user queries, requiring them to dynamically interleave internal reasoning with tool use. While such capabilities can in principle be learned via reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), we observe that agents often exhibit poor exploration behaviors, including premature termination and biased tool usage. As a result, RLVR alone yields limited improvements. We propose SynPlanResearch-R1, a framework that synthesizes tool-use trajectories that encourage deeper exploration to shape exploration during cold-start supervised fine-tuning, providing a strong initialization for subsequent RL. Across seven multi-hop and open-web benchmarks, \framework improves performance by up to 6.0% on Qwen3-8B and 5.8% on Qwen3-4B backbones respectively compared to SOTA baselines. Further analyses of tool-use patterns and training dynamics compared to baselines shed light on the factors underlying these gains. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/HansiZeng/syn-plan-research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SynPlanResearch-R1：通过合成计划鼓励深度研究中的工具探索
研究智能体使模型能够利用工具从网络收集信息以回答用户查询，这要求模型动态交织内部推理与工具使用。虽然此类能力原则上可通过带可验证奖励的强化学习习得，但我们观察到智能体常表现出不良探索行为，包括过早终止和工具使用偏差，导致仅靠强化学习改进有限。为此，我们提出SynPlanResearch-R1框架，通过合成鼓励深度探索的工具使用轨迹，在冷启动监督微调阶段引导探索行为，为后续强化学习提供优质初始化。在七个多跳和开放网络基准测试中，相比前沿基线，该框架在Qwen3-8B和Qwen3-4B骨干模型上分别实现最高6.0%和5.8%的性能提升。对工具使用模式和训练动态的对比分析进一步揭示了性能增益的内在机制。代码已开源：https://github.com/HansiZeng/syn-plan-research。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the observation that research agents, which use tools to gather web information for answering queries, often suffer from poor exploration behaviors like premature termination and biased tool usage when trained solely with reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), leading to limited improvements. To address this, the method introduces SynPlanResearch-R1, a framework that synthesizes tool-use trajectories to encourage deeper exploration, shaping behavior during an initial supervised fine-tuning phase to provide a strong initialization for subsequent reinforcement learning. The main experimental results show that across seven multi-hop and open-web benchmarks, the framework improves performance by up to 6.0% on Qwen3-8B and 5.8% on Qwen3-4B backbones compared to state-of-the-art baselines, with further analyses revealing insights into the tool-use patterns and training dynamics behind these gains.

Whole-Brain Connectomic Graph Model Enables Whole-Body Locomotion Control in Fruit Fly
Authors: Zehao Jin, Yaoye Zhu, Chen Zhang, Yanan Sui
First: 2026-02-20T05:09:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T23:37:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Whole-brain biological neural networks naturally support the learning and control of whole-body movements. However, the use of brain connectomes as neural network controllers in embodied reinforcement learning remains unexplored. We investigate using the exact neural architecture of an adult fruit fly's brain for the control of its body movement. We develop Fly-connectomic Graph Model (FlyGM), whose static structure is identical to the complete connectome of an adult Drosophila for whole-body locomotion control. To perform dynamical control, FlyGM represents the static connectome as a directed message-passing graph to impose a biologically grounded information flow from sensory inputs to motor outputs. Integrated with a biomechanical fruit fly model, our method achieves stable control across diverse locomotion tasks without task-specific architectural tuning. To verify the structural advantages of the connectome-based model, we compare it against a degree-preserving rewired graph, a random graph, and multilayer perceptrons, showing that FlyGM yields higher sample efficiency and superior performance. This work demonstrates that static brain connectomes can be transformed to instantiate effective neural policy for embodied learning of movement control.

标题：全脑连接组图模型实现果蝇全身运动控制
全脑生物神经网络天然支持全身运动的学习与控制，但将大脑连接组作为具身强化学习中的神经网络控制器尚未被探索。本研究利用成年果蝇大脑的精确神经架构控制其身体运动，开发了静态结构与成年黑腹果蝇完整连接组完全一致的果蝇连接组图模型（FlyGM），用于全身运动控制。为实现动态控制，FlyGM将静态连接组表示为有向消息传递图，以建立从感觉输入到运动输出的生物学信息流。结合果蝇生物力学模型，该方法在多种运动任务中实现稳定控制，无需针对任务调整架构。为验证基于连接组模型的结构优势，我们将其与度保持重连图、随机图及多层感知机对比，表明FlyGM具有更高的样本效率和更优性能。本工作证明静态大脑连接组可转化为有效的神经策略，用于运动控制的具身学习。

Ego-Vision World Model for Humanoid Contact Planning
Authors: Hang Liu, Yuman Gao, Sangli Teng, Yufeng Chi, Yakun Sophia Shao, Zhongyu Li, Maani Ghaffari, Koushil Sreenath
First: 2025-10-13T17:47:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T23:33:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Enabling humanoid robots to exploit physical contact, rather than simply avoid collisions, is crucial for autonomy in unstructured environments. Traditional optimization-based planners struggle with contact complexity, while on-policy reinforcement learning (RL) is sample-inefficient and has limited multi-task ability. We propose a framework combining a learned world model with sampling-based Model Predictive Control (MPC), trained on a demonstration-free offline dataset to predict future outcomes in a compressed latent space. To address sparse contact rewards and sensor noise, the MPC uses a learned surrogate value function for dense, robust planning. Our single, scalable model supports contact-aware tasks, including wall support after perturbation, blocking incoming objects, and traversing height-limited arches, with improved sample efficiency and multi-task capability over on-policy RL. Deployed on a physical humanoid, our system achieves robust, real-time contact planning from proprioception and ego-centric depth images. Code and dataset are available at our website: https://ego-vcp.github.io/

标题：人形机器人接触规划的自我视觉世界模型
使人形机器人能够利用物理接触而非单纯避碰，对于非结构化环境中的自主性至关重要。传统基于优化的规划器难以处理接触复杂性，而同策略强化学习（RL）样本效率低且多任务能力有限。我们提出一个框架，将学习的世界模型与基于采样的模型预测控制（MPC）相结合，在无需演示的离线数据集上训练，以在压缩潜在空间中预测未来结果。为解决稀疏接触奖励和传感器噪声问题，MPC采用学习的代理价值函数进行密集鲁棒规划。我们的单一可扩展模型支持接触感知任务，包括扰动后的墙面支撑、拦截来物和穿越限高拱门，相比同策略RL具有更高的样本效率和多任务能力。在实体人形机器人上部署后，该系统通过本体感知和自我中心深度图像实现了鲁棒的实时接触规划。代码与数据集详见项目网站：https://ego-vcp.github.io/
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need for humanoid robots to actively use physical contact for autonomy in unstructured settings, overcoming limitations of traditional optimization planners and sample-inefficient on-policy reinforcement learning. The method introduces a framework that combines a learned world model with sampling-based Model Predictive Control (MPC), trained on an offline dataset without demonstrations to predict outcomes in a compressed latent space, and employs a learned surrogate value function to handle sparse contact rewards and sensor noise for dense, robust planning. Experimental results show that this single, scalable model enables contact-aware tasks such as wall support after perturbation, blocking objects, and traversing arches with improved sample efficiency and multi-task capability over on-policy RL, and it achieves robust, real-time contact planning on a physical humanoid using proprioception and ego-centric depth images.

ARM-FM: Automated Reward Machines via Foundation Models for Compositional Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Roger Creus Castanyer, Faisal Mohamed, Pablo Samuel Castro, Cyrus Neary, Glen Berseth
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-16T00:18:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T23:00:50+00:00
Comments: Published at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms are highly sensitive to reward function specification, which remains a central challenge limiting their broad applicability. We present ARM-FM: Automated Reward Machines via Foundation Models, a framework for automated, compositional reward design in RL that leverages the high-level reasoning capabilities of foundation models (FMs). Reward machines (RMs) -- an automata-based formalism for reward specification -- are used as the mechanism for RL objective specification, and are automatically constructed via the use of FMs. The structured formalism of RMs yields effective task decompositions, while the use of FMs enables objective specifications in natural language. Concretely, we (i) use FMs to automatically generate RMs from natural language specifications; (ii) associate language embeddings with each RM automata-state to enable generalization across tasks; and (iii) provide empirical evidence of ARM-FM's effectiveness in a diverse suite of challenging environments, including evidence of zero-shot generalization.
中文标题/摘要

强化学习算法对奖励函数设定高度敏感，这仍是限制其广泛应用的核心挑战。本文提出ARM-FM：基于基础模型的自动奖励机框架，利用基础模型的高层推理能力实现强化学习中自动化、组合式的奖励设计。奖励机——一种基于自动机的奖励形式化方法——被用作强化学习目标设定的机制，并通过基础模型自动构建。奖励机的结构化形式化方法能产生有效的任务分解，而基础模型的使用支持自然语言目标设定。具体而言，我们（1）使用基础模型从自然语言描述自动生成奖励机；（2）为每个奖励机自动机状态关联语言嵌入以实现跨任务泛化；（3）在多样化挑战性环境中提供ARM-FM有效性的实证证据，包括零样本泛化能力的证明。

Experimental results across diverse environments demonstrate the framework's effectiveness, including evidence of zero-shot generalization to new tasks.
本文针对强化学习中奖励函数设计的难题，提出了ARM-FM框架，利用基础模型自动化实现组合式奖励设计。该方法通过基础模型从自然语言任务描述自动生成奖励机，并引入语言嵌入以实现状态泛化，利用奖励机进行任务分解。在多种挑战性环境中的实验结果表明，该框架有效，并展示了零样本泛化到新任务的能力。
Landscape of Policy Optimization for Finite Horizon MDPs with General State and Action
Authors: Xin Chen, Yifan Hu, Minda Zhao
First: 2024-09-25T17:56:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T22:03:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Policy gradient methods are widely used in reinforcement learning. Yet, the nonconvexity of policy optimization poses significant challenges in understanding the global convergence of policy gradient methods. For a class of finite-horizon Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) with general state and action spaces, we identify a set of structural properties to establish a benign nonconvex landscape, the Polyak-Łojasiewicz-Kurdyka (PŁK) condition of the policy optimization. Leveraging the PŁK condition, policy gradient methods converge to the globally optimal policy with a non-asymptotic rate despite nonconvexity. Our results apply to various control and operations models, including entropy-regularized tabular MDPs, Linear Quadratic Regulator problems, and both stochastic inventory models and stochastic cash balance problems with strongly convex costs. In these models, stochastic policy gradient methods obtain an $ε$-optimal policy using a sample size of $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-1})$ and polynomial in terms of the planning horizon. To the best of our knowledge, we provide the first sample-complexity guarantees for multi-period inventory systems with Markov-modulated demand and for stochastic cash balance problems. We complement the theory with numerical experiments showing that policy gradient methods outperform several benchmark algorithms from the literature across these operations models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一般状态与动作空间下有限时域马尔可夫决策过程的策略优化格局分析
策略梯度方法在强化学习中应用广泛，但策略优化的非凸性给理解其全局收敛性带来重大挑战。针对一类具有一般状态与动作空间的有限时域马尔可夫决策过程，我们通过识别一组结构特性，建立了策略优化的良性非凸格局——Polyak-Łojasiewicz-Kurdyka条件。基于该条件，策略梯度方法能以非渐近速率收敛至全局最优策略。我们的成果适用于多种控制与运营模型，包括熵正则化表格MDP、线性二次调节器问题，以及具有强凸成本函数的随机库存模型与随机现金余额问题。在这些模型中，随机策略梯度方法使用样本量$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-1})$（与规划时域呈多项式关系）即可获得$ε$最优策略。据我们所知，本研究首次为具有马尔可夫调制需求的多周期库存系统及随机现金余额问题提供了样本复杂度保证。我们通过数值实验验证了理论结果，表明策略梯度方法在这些运营模型中均优于文献中的多种基准算法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of global convergence in policy gradient methods for reinforcement learning, which is complicated by the nonconvex nature of policy optimization. The authors identify structural properties in finite-horizon Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) with general state and action spaces that ensure a benign optimization landscape, specifically the Polyak-Łojasiewicz-Kurdyka (PŁK) condition. Leveraging this condition, they prove that policy gradient methods converge to the globally optimal policy with a non-asymptotic rate, and demonstrate that stochastic policy gradient methods achieve an ε-optimal policy with a sample complexity of Õ(ε⁻¹) across various models including entropy-regularized tabular MDPs, Linear Quadratic Regulators, and stochastic inventory and cash balance problems. Numerical experiments further show that these methods outperform existing benchmark algorithms in operations models.
本文针对强化学习中策略梯度方法因策略优化的非凸性而难以保证全局收敛的问题展开研究。作者在具有一般状态和动作空间的有限时域马尔可夫决策过程中识别出一组结构特性，从而确保了良性的优化地形，即满足Polyak-Łojasiewicz-Kurdyka（PŁK）条件。利用这一条件，他们证明了策略梯度方法能够以非渐近速率收敛到全局最优策略，并且随机策略梯度方法在熵正则化表格MDP、线性二次调节器以及具有强凸成本的随机库存模型和现金平衡问题等多种模型中，能以Õ(ε⁻¹)的样本复杂度获得ε-最优策略。数值实验进一步表明，在这些运营模型中，策略梯度方法的表现优于文献中的多种基准算法。
Toward Global Intent Inference for Human Motion by Inverse Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Sarmad Mehrdad, Maxime Sabbah, Vincent Bonnet, Ludovic Righetti
First: 2026-03-08T20:37:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T20:37:19+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper investigates whether a single, unified cost function can explain and predict human reaching movements, in contrast with existing approaches that rely on subject- or posture-specific optimization criteria. Using the Minimal Observation Inverse Reinforcement Learning (MO-IRL) algorithm, together with a seven-dimensional set of candidate cost terms, we efficiently estimate time-varying cost weights for a standard planar reaching task. MO-IRL provides orders-of-magnitude faster convergence than bilevel formulations, while using only a fraction of the available data, enabling the practical exploration of time-varying cost structures. Three levels of generality are evaluated: Subject-Dependent Posture-Dependent, Subject-Dependent Posture-Independent, and Subject-Independent Posture-Independent. Across all cases, time-varying weights substantially improve trajectory reconstruction, yielding an average 27% reduction in RMSE compared to the baseline. The inferred costs consistently highlight a dominant role for joint-acceleration regulation, complemented by smaller contributions from torque-change smoothness. Overall, a single subject- and posture-agnostic time-varying cost function is shown to predict human reaching trajectories with high accuracy, supporting the existence of a unified optimality principle governing this class of movements.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于逆强化学习的全局人类运动意图推断研究
本文探讨了是否能用单一统一的代价函数解释和预测人类的伸展运动，这与现有依赖个体或姿态特定优化准则的方法形成对比。通过采用最小观测逆强化学习算法及七维候选代价项集合，我们高效估计了标准平面伸展任务中时变的代价权重。该算法相比双层优化框架实现了数量级更快的收敛速度，且仅需少量数据即可探索时变代价结构的实际应用。研究评估了三个泛化层级：个体依赖姿态依赖、个体依赖姿态独立、个体独立姿态独立。在所有案例中，时变权重显著提升了轨迹重建效果，与基线相比均方根误差平均降低27%。推断出的代价函数一致凸显关节加速度调节的主导作用，辅以扭矩变化平滑性的次要贡献。总体而言，研究表明单一且不依赖个体与姿态的时变代价函数能高精度预测人类伸展轨迹，支持了支配此类运动的统一最优性原理的存在。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to find a unified principle for human movement rather than relying on subject- or posture-specific criteria, this paper employs the Minimal Observation Inverse Reinforcement Learning (MO-IRL) algorithm with a seven-dimensional set of candidate cost terms to efficiently estimate time-varying cost weights for planar reaching tasks. The method enables rapid convergence and uses limited data to explore time-varying cost structures across three generality levels: Subject-Dependent Posture-Dependent, Subject-Dependent Posture-Independent, and Subject-Independent Posture-Independent. Experimental results show that time-varying weights substantially improve trajectory reconstruction, reducing RMSE by an average of 27% compared to baselines, with joint-acceleration regulation consistently emerging as the dominant cost term, supported by torque-change smoothness, thereby demonstrating that a single subject- and posture-agnostic time-varying cost function can accurately predict human reaching movements.
本文旨在探索是否存在一个统一的最优性原则来解释人类运动，而非依赖特定个体或姿势的优化标准，为此采用最小观测逆强化学习算法和七维候选成本项集合，高效估计平面伸手任务中的时变成本权重。该方法实现了快速收敛，并利用有限数据探索了时变成本结构，评估了三种通用性级别：个体依赖姿势依赖、个体依赖姿势独立以及个体独立姿势独立。实验结果表明，时变权重显著改善了轨迹重建，相比基线平均降低均方根误差27%，推断出的成本函数一致突显关节加速度调节的主导作用，辅以扭矩变化平滑性的较小贡献，最终证明一个与个体和姿势无关的时变成本函数能够高精度预测人类伸手轨迹。
ProgAgent:A Continual RL Agent with Progress-Aware Rewards
Authors: Jinzhou Tan, Gabriel Adineera, Jinoh Kim
First: 2026-03-08T19:58:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T19:58:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present ProgAgent, a continual reinforcement learning (CRL) agent that unifies progress-aware reward learning with a high-throughput, JAX-native system architecture. Lifelong robotic learning grapples with catastrophic forgetting and the high cost of reward specification. ProgAgent tackles these by deriving dense, shaped rewards from unlabeled expert videos through a perceptual model that estimates task progress across initial, current, and goal observations. We theoretically interpret this as a learned state-potential function, delivering robust guidance in line with expert behaviors. To maintain stability amid online exploration - where novel, out-of-distribution states arise - we incorporate an adversarial push-back refinement that regularizes the reward model, curbing overconfident predictions on non-expert trajectories and countering distribution shift. By embedding this reward mechanism into a JIT-compiled loop, ProgAgent supports massively parallel rollouts and fully differentiable updates, rendering a sophisticated unified objective feasible: it merges PPO with coreset replay and synaptic intelligence for an enhanced stability-plasticity balance. Evaluations on ContinualBench and Meta-World benchmarks highlight ProgAgent's advantages: it markedly reduces forgetting, boosts learning speed, and outperforms key baselines in visual reward learning (e.g., Rank2Reward, TCN) and continual learning (e.g., Coreset, SI) - surpassing even an idealized perfect memory agent. Real-robot trials further validate its ability to acquire complex manipulation skills from noisy, few-shot human demonstrations.

本文提出ProgAgent，一种持续强化学习智能体，将进度感知奖励学习与基于JAX的高吞吐系统架构相结合。终身机器人学习面临灾难性遗忘和奖励标注成本高昂的挑战。ProgAgent通过感知模型从无标注专家视频中推导密集的成形奖励，该模型能基于初始、当前和目标观测估计任务进度。理论分析表明该机制等价于学习状态势函数，能提供符合专家行为的鲁棒指导。为应对在线探索中分布外状态导致的稳定性问题，我们引入对抗性修正机制，通过正则化奖励模型抑制对非专家轨迹的过度自信预测，缓解分布偏移。通过将奖励机制嵌入JIT编译循环，ProgAgent支持大规模并行推演和完全可微更新，实现了融合PPO、核心集回放与突触智能的稳定-可塑性平衡目标。在ContinualBench和Meta-World基准测试中，ProgAgent显著降低遗忘率、提升学习速度，在视觉奖励学习（如Rank2Reward、TCN）和持续学习（如Coreset、SI）方面超越关键基线模型，性能甚至优于理想化完美记忆智能体。真实机器人实验进一步验证其从少量带噪声人类示教中学习复杂操作技能的能力。

Scaling Data Difficulty: Improving Coding Models via Reinforcement Learning on Fresh and Challenging Problems
Authors: Zongqian Li, Tengchao Lv, Shaohan Huang, Yixuan Su, Qinzheng Sun, Qiufeng Yin, Ying Xin, Scarlett Li, Lei Cui, Nigel Collier, Furu Wei
First: 2026-03-08T19:45:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T19:45:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training next-generation code generation models requires high-quality datasets, yet existing datasets face difficulty imbalance, format inconsistency, and data quality problems. We address these challenges through systematic data processing and difficulty scaling. We introduce a four-stage Data Processing Framework encompassing collection, processing, filtering, and verification, incorporating Automatic Difficulty Filtering via an LLM-based predict-calibrate-select framework that leverages multi-dimensional difficulty metrics across five weighted dimensions to retain challenging problems while removing simplistic ones. The resulting MicroCoder dataset comprises tens of thousands of curated real competitive programming problems from diverse platforms, emphasizing recency and difficulty. Evaluations on strictly unseen LiveCodeBench demonstrate that MicroCoder achieves 3x larger performance gains within 300 training steps compared to widely-used baseline datasets of comparable size, with consistent advantages under both GRPO and its variant training algorithms. The MicroCoder dataset delivers obvious improvements on medium and hard problems across different model sizes, achieving up to 17.2% relative gains in overall performance where model capabilities are most stretched. These results validate that difficulty-aware data curation improves model performance on challenging tasks, providing multiple insights for dataset creation in code generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：数据难度扩展：通过强化学习解决新颖挑战性问题以提升代码生成模型性能
训练新一代代码生成模型需要高质量数据集，但现有数据集面临难度失衡、格式不一致和数据质量问题。我们通过系统性数据处理与难度扩展应对这些挑战，提出包含收集、处理、筛选和验证的四阶段数据处理框架，并引入基于大语言模型的自动难度筛选机制——该机制采用预测-校准-选择框架，通过五个加权维度的多维度难度指标保留挑战性问题并剔除简单问题。最终构建的MicroCoder数据集包含来自多平台数万个精选的真实竞赛编程问题，突出时效性与难度。在严格未见过的LiveCodeBench评估中，MicroCoder在300训练步内实现比同等规模基线数据集高3倍的性能增益，在GRPO及其变体训练算法下均保持稳定优势。该数据集在不同规模模型的中高难度问题上均带来显著改进，在模型能力极限处实现最高17.2%的相对性能提升。这些结果验证了难度感知的数据策展能提升模型在挑战性任务上的表现，为代码生成领域的数据集构建提供了多维洞见。

Breaking Training Bottlenecks: Effective and Stable Reinforcement Learning for Coding Models
Authors: Zongqian Li, Shaohan Huang, Zewen Chi, Yixuan Su, Lexin Zhou, Li Dong, Nigel Collier, Furu Wei
First: 2026-03-08T19:40:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T19:40:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern code generation models exhibit longer outputs, accelerated capability growth, and changed training dynamics, rendering traditional training methodologies, algorithms, and datasets ineffective for improving their performance. To address these training bottlenecks, we propose MicroCoder-GRPO, an improved Group Relative Policy Optimization approach with three innovations: conditional truncation masking to improve long output potential while maintaining training stability, diversity-determined temperature selection to maintain and encourage output diversity, and removal of KL loss with high clipping ratios to facilitate solution diversity. MicroCoder-GRPO achieves up to 17.6% relative improvement over strong baselines on LiveCodeBench v6, with more pronounced gains under extended context evaluation. Additionally, we release MicroCoder-Dataset, a more challenging training corpus that achieves 3x larger performance gains than mainstream datasets on LiveCodeBench v6 within 300 training steps, and MicroCoder-Evaluator, a robust framework with approximately 25% improved evaluation accuracy and around 40% faster execution. Through comprehensive analysis across more than thirty controlled experiments, we reveal 34 training insights across seven main aspects, demonstrating that properly trained models can achieve competitive performance with larger counterparts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破训练瓶颈：面向代码模型的高效稳定强化学习方法
现代代码生成模型呈现出输出更长、能力增长加速、训练动态变化等特征，导致传统训练方法、算法与数据集难以有效提升其性能。为突破这些训练瓶颈，我们提出MicroCoder-GRPO——一种改进的组相对策略优化方法，包含三项创新：条件截断掩码在保持训练稳定性的同时提升长文本生成潜力，多样性驱动的温度选择机制维持并促进输出多样性，以及通过高裁剪比移除KL损失以增强解空间多样性。在LiveCodeBench v6基准测试中，MicroCoder-GRPO相较强基线取得最高17.6%的相对性能提升，在扩展上下文评估中增益更为显著。同时，我们开源了MicroCoder-Dataset（在300训练步内比主流数据集在LiveCodeBench v6上实现3倍性能增益的挑战性训练语料）与MicroCoder-Evaluator（评估准确率提升约25%、执行速度加快约40%的鲁棒评估框架）。通过对三十余组对照实验的系统分析，我们提炼出涵盖七大维度的34项训练洞见，证明经恰当训练的模型可获得与更大规模模型相竞争的性能。
