Reinforcing Numerical Reasoning in LLMs for Tabular Prediction via Structural Priors
Authors: Pengxiang Cai, Zihao Gao, Wanchen Lian, Jintai Chen
First: 2025-10-20T10:22:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T18:21:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tabular prediction traditionally relies on gradient-boosted decision trees and deep learning models, which excel in specific tasks but lack interpretability and transferability. Reasoning large language models (LLMs) promise cross-task adaptability with transparent reasoning traces, yet their potential for tabular data remains unrealized. To bridge this gap, we propose a reasoning framework centered on Permutation Relative Policy Optimization (PRPO), a reinforcement learning method that encodes column-permutation invariance as a structural prior. By estimating advantages across label-preserving permutations, PRPO transforms sparse rewards into dense signals, activating latent numerical reasoning capabilities of LLMs with limited supervision. Extensive experiments show that our method matches fully supervised baselines and dominates in zero-shot settings, performing on par with 32-shot strong baselines. Remarkably, our 8B model significantly outperforms much larger LLMs, achieving up to a 53.17% improvement over DeepSeek-R1 (685B).

Experimental results demonstrate that the approach matches fully supervised baselines and excels in zero-shot settings, with an 8B model notably outperforming much larger LLMs, achieving up to a 53.17% improvement over DeepSeek-R1 (685B).
本文针对表格预测任务中模型可解释性和可迁移性不足的问题，提出了一种强化学习框架，通过引入结构先验来增强大语言模型的数值推理能力。该方法采用置换相对策略优化，将列置换不变性作为先验知识，将稀疏奖励转化为密集信号，从而在有限监督下激活模型的潜在推理能力。实验结果表明，该方法在完全监督基准上表现相当，并在零样本设置中占据优势，其8B参数模型显著优于更大规模的大语言模型，相比DeepSeek-R1实现了高达53.17%的性能提升。
TDM-R1: Reinforcing Few-Step Diffusion Models with Non-Differentiable Reward
Authors: Yihong Luo, Tianyang Hu, Weijian Luo, Jing Tang
First: 2026-03-08T15:57:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T15:57:10+00:00
Comments: https://luo-yihong.github.io/TDM-R1-Page/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3 · Project1
Abstract
While few-step generative models have enabled powerful image and video generation at significantly lower cost, generic reinforcement learning (RL) paradigms for few-step models remain an unsolved problem. Existing RL approaches for few-step diffusion models strongly rely on back-propagating through differentiable reward models, thereby excluding the majority of important real-world reward signals, e.g., non-differentiable rewards such as humans' binary likeness, object counts, etc. To properly incorporate non-differentiable rewards to improve few-step generative models, we introduce TDM-R1, a novel reinforcement learning paradigm built upon a leading few-step model, Trajectory Distribution Matching (TDM). TDM-R1 decouples the learning process into surrogate reward learning and generator learning. Furthermore, we developed practical methods to obtain per-step reward signals along the deterministic generation trajectory of TDM, resulting in a unified RL post-training method that significantly improves few-step models' ability with generic rewards. We conduct extensive experiments ranging from text-rendering, visual quality, and preference alignment. All results demonstrate that TDM-R1 is a powerful reinforcement learning paradigm for few-step text-to-image models, achieving state-of-the-art reinforcement learning performances on both in-domain and out-of-domain metrics. Furthermore, TDM-R1 also scales effectively to the recent strong Z-Image model, consistently outperforming both its 100-NFE and few-step variants with only 4 NFEs. Project page: https://github.com/Luo-Yihong/TDM-R1
中文标题/摘要
标题：TDM-R1：利用不可微奖励增强少步扩散模型
尽管少步生成模型已能以显著更低成本实现强大的图像与视频生成，但适用于少步模型的通用强化学习范式仍是未解难题。现有针对少步扩散模型的强化学习方法严重依赖可微奖励模型的反向传播，从而排除了多数重要的现实世界奖励信号（如人类二元喜好、物体计数等不可微奖励）。为有效整合不可微奖励以改进少步生成模型，我们提出TDM-R1——一种基于领先少步模型轨迹分布匹配（TDM）的新型强化学习范式。TDM-R1将学习过程解耦为代理奖励学习与生成器学习，并开发了在TDM确定性生成轨迹上获取逐步奖励信号的实用方法，形成统一的强化学习后训练方案，显著提升少步模型处理通用奖励的能力。我们在文本渲染、视觉质量与偏好对齐等维度开展广泛实验，所有结果均表明TDM-R1是针对少步文生图模型的强大强化学习范式，在领域内外指标上均达到最先进的强化学习性能。此外，TDM-R1还能有效扩展至近期强大的Z-Image模型，仅用4次NFE即持续超越其100-NFE及少步变体。项目页面：https://github.com/Luo-Yihong/TDM-R1

Main experimental results show that TDM-R1 significantly improves few-step text-to-image models across text-rendering, visual quality, and preference alignment tasks, achieving state-of-the-art RL performance on both in-domain and out-of-domain metrics, and it scales effectively to models like Z-Image, outperforming variants with more steps using only 4 NFEs.

Global Convergence of Average Reward Constrained MDPs with Neural Critic and General Policy Parameterization
Authors: Anirudh Satheesh, Pankaj Kumar Barman, Washim Uddin Mondal, Vaneet Aggarwal
First: 2026-03-08T15:53:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T15:53:59+00:00
Comments: Submitted to UAI 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study infinite-horizon Constrained Markov Decision Processes (CMDPs) with general policy parameterizations and multi-layer neural network critics. Existing theoretical analyses for constrained reinforcement learning largely rely on tabular policies or linear critics, which limits their applicability to high-dimensional and continuous control problems. We propose a primal-dual natural actor-critic algorithm that integrates neural critic estimation with natural policy gradient updates and leverages Neural Tangent Kernel (NTK) theory to control function-approximation error under Markovian sampling, without requiring access to mixing-time oracles. We establish global convergence and cumulative constraint violation rates of $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^-1/4)$ up to approximation errors induced by the policy and critic classes. Our results provide the first such guarantees for CMDPs with general policies and multi-layer neural critics, substantially extending the theoretical foundations of actor-critic methods beyond the linear-critic regime.
中文标题/摘要
标题：带神经评论家与通用策略参数化的平均奖励约束MDP全局收敛性研究
本文研究具有通用策略参数化和多层神经网络评论家的无限时域约束马尔可夫决策过程。现有约束强化学习的理论分析主要依赖表格策略或线性评论家，限制了其在高维连续控制问题中的应用。我们提出一种原始-对偶自然行动者-评论家算法，将神经评论家估计与自然策略梯度更新相结合，并利用神经正切核理论控制马尔可夫采样下的函数逼近误差，无需混合时间预言机。我们建立了$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{-1/4})$的全局收敛速率与累积约束违反率（受策略和评论家类逼近误差影响）。该成果首次为具有通用策略和多层神经评论家的CMDP提供此类理论保证，显著拓展了行动者-评论家方法在线性评论家体系之外的理论基础。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the theoretical limitations of existing constrained reinforcement learning methods, which are often restricted to tabular policies or linear critics and thus not well-suited for high-dimensional continuous control. The authors propose a primal-dual natural actor-critic algorithm that combines neural critic estimation with natural policy gradient updates, utilizing Neural Tangent Kernel theory to manage function-approximation errors under Markovian sampling without needing mixing-time oracles. Their main experimental results demonstrate global convergence and cumulative constraint violation rates of $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{-1/4})$, up to approximation errors, marking the first such guarantees for Constrained MDPs with general policy parameterizations and multi-layer neural network critics.
本文针对现有约束强化学习方法多局限于表格策略或线性评论家、难以适用于高维连续控制问题的理论局限，提出了一种原始-对偶自然行动者-评论家算法。该方法将神经评论家估计与自然策略梯度更新相结合，并利用神经正切核理论在马尔可夫采样下控制函数逼近误差，无需混合时间预言机。主要实验结果表明，在策略和评论家类引起的逼近误差范围内，算法实现了全局收敛和累积约束违反率为$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{-1/4})$，这为具有通用策略参数化和多层神经评论家的约束马尔可夫决策过程提供了首个此类理论保证。
Mitigating the Memory Bottleneck with Machine Learning-Driven and Data-Aware Microarchitectural Techniques
Authors: Rahul Bera
First: 2026-03-08T15:34:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T15:34:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern applications process massive data volumes that overwhelm the storage and retrieval capabilities of memory systems, making memory the primary performance and energy-efficiency bottleneck of computing systems. Although many microarchitectural techniques attempt to hide or tolerate long memory access latency, rapidly growing data footprints continue to outpace technology scaling, requiring more effective solutions. This dissertation shows that modern processors observe large amounts of application and system data during execution, yet many microarchitectural mechanisms make decisions largely independent of this information. Through four case studies, we demonstrate that such data-agnostic design leads to substantial missed opportunities for improving performance and energy efficiency. To address this limitation, this dissertation advocates shifting microarchitecture design from data-agnostic to data-informed. We propose mechanisms that (1) learn policies from observed execution behavior (data-driven design) and (2) exploit semantic characteristics of application data (data-aware design). We apply lightweight machine learning techniques and previously underexplored data characteristics across four processor components: a reinforcement learning-based hardware data prefetcher that learns memory access patterns online; a perceptron predictor that identifies memory requests likely to access off-chip memory; a reinforcement learning mechanism that coordinates data prefetching and off-chip prediction; and a mechanism that exploits repeatability in memory addresses and loaded values to eliminate predictable load instructions. Our extensive evaluation shows that the proposed techniques significantly improve performance and energy efficiency compared to prior state-of-the-art approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用机器学习驱动与数据感知的微架构技术缓解内存瓶颈
现代应用处理的海量数据已超出内存系统的存储与检索能力，使内存成为计算系统性能和能效的主要瓶颈。尽管许多微架构技术试图隐藏或容忍较长的内存访问延迟，但快速增长的数据规模持续超越技术扩展速度，亟需更有效的解决方案。本论文指出，现代处理器在执行过程中可观测到大量应用与系统数据，但多数微架构机制在决策时基本独立于这些信息。通过四个案例研究，我们证明这种数据无关的设计会错失大量提升性能与能效的机会。 为突破此局限，本论文主张将微架构设计从数据无关转向数据知情。我们提出两种机制：(1) 从观测到的执行行为中学习策略（数据驱动设计）；(2) 利用应用数据的语义特征（数据感知设计）。我们在四个处理器组件中应用轻量级机器学习技术与先前未充分探索的数据特征：基于强化学习的硬件数据预取器（在线学习内存访问模式）；感知器预测器（识别可能访问片外内存的请求）；协调数据预取与片外预测的强化学习机制；以及利用内存地址与加载值可重复性以消除可预测加载指令的机制。 大量实验表明，相较于现有先进方案，所提技术能显著提升性能与能效。

The proposed method shifts microarchitecture design from data-agnostic to data-informed approaches, using lightweight machine learning to learn from execution behavior and exploit data semantics across four processor components, including a reinforcement learning-based prefetcher and a perceptron predictor for off-chip memory access. Experimental results demonstrate that these techniques significantly enhance performance and energy efficiency compared to prior state-of-the-art methods.
本论文的动机是计算系统中日益严重的内存瓶颈问题，即海量数据量超出内存处理能力，限制了性能和能效。所提出的方法将微架构设计从数据无关转向数据感知，通过轻量级机器学习从执行行为中学习并利用数据语义，应用于四个处理器组件，包括基于强化学习的预取器和用于片外内存访问的感知器预测器。实验结果表明，与现有先进方法相比，这些技术显著提升了性能和能效。
A Primer on Evolutionary Frameworks for Near-Field Multi-Source Localization
Authors: Seyed Jalaleddin Mousavirad, Parisa Ramezani, Mattias O'Nils, Emil Björnson
First: 2026-03-08T15:22:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T15:22:19+00:00
Comments: This paper is submitted to a related Journal
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper introduces a novel class of model-driven evolutionary frameworks for near-field multi-source localization, addressing the major limitations of grid-based subspace methods such as MUSIC and data-dependent deep learning approaches. To this end, we develop two complementary evolutionary localization frameworks that operate directly on the continuous spherical-wave signal model and support arbitrary array geometries without requiring labeled data, discretized angle--range grids, or architectural constraints. The first framework, termed NEar-field MultimOdal DE (NEMO-DE) associates each individual in the evolutionary population to a single source and optimizes a residual least-squares objective in a sequential manner, updating the data residual and enforcing spatial separation to estimate multiple source locations. To overcome the limitation of NEMO-DE under large power imbalances among the sources, we propose the second framework, named NEar-field Eigen-subspace Fitting DE (NEEF-DE), which jointly encodes all source locations and minimizes a subspace-fitting criterion that aligns a model-based array response subspace with the received signal subspace. Although the proposed frameworks are algorithm-agnostic and compatible with various evolutionary optimizers, differential evolution (DE) is adopted in this work as a representative search strategy due to its simplicity, robustness, and strong empirical performance. We provide extensive numerical experiments to evaluate the performance of the proposed frameworks under different system configurations. This work establishes evolutionary computation as a powerful and flexible paradigm for model-based near-field localization, paving the way for future innovations in this domain.
中文标题/摘要
标题：近场多源定位的进化框架入门
本文提出了一类新颖的模型驱动进化框架，用于近场多源定位，解决了基于网格的子空间方法（如MUSIC）和数据依赖的深度学习方法的主要局限。为此，我们开发了两种互补的进化定位框架，它们直接基于连续球面波信号模型运行，支持任意阵列几何结构，无需标记数据、离散化的角度-距离网格或架构约束。第一种框架称为近场多模态差分进化（NEMO-DE），将进化种群中的每个个体关联到单个源，以顺序方式优化残差最小二乘目标，更新数据残差并强制空间分离以估计多个源位置。为克服NEMO-DE在源间功率严重不平衡时的局限，我们提出了第二种框架，即近场特征子空间拟合差分进化（NEEF-DE），它联合编码所有源位置，并最小化一个子空间拟合准则，使基于模型的阵列响应子空间与接收信号子空间对齐。尽管所提框架与算法无关且兼容多种进化优化器，但本文采用差分进化（DE）作为代表性搜索策略，因其简单性、鲁棒性和强大的实证性能。我们提供了广泛的数值实验，以评估所提框架在不同系统配置下的性能。这项工作确立了进化计算作为基于模型的近场定位的强大灵活范式，为该领域的未来创新铺平了道路。

Meta-RL Induces Exploration in Language Agents
Authors: Yulun Jiang, Liangze Jiang, Damien Teney, Michael Moor, Maria Brbic
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-12-18T18:22:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T15:00:07+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has enabled the training of large language model (LLM) agents to interact with the environment and to solve multi-turn long-horizon tasks. However, the RL-trained agents often struggle in tasks that require active exploration and fail to efficiently adapt from trial-and-error experiences. In this paper, we present LaMer, a general Meta-RL framework that enables LLM agents to actively explore and learn from the environment feedback at test time. LaMer consists of two key components: (i) a cross-episode training framework to encourage exploration and long-term rewards optimization; and (ii) in-context policy adaptation via reflection, allowing the agent to adapt their policy from task feedback signal without gradient update. Experiments across diverse environments show that LaMer significantly improves performance over RL baselines, with 11%, 14%, and 19% performance gains on Sokoban, MineSweeper and Webshop, respectively. Moreover, LaMer also demonstrates better generalization to more challenging or previously unseen tasks compared to the RL-trained agents. Overall, our results demonstrate that Meta-RL provides a principled approach to induce exploration in language agents, enabling more robust adaptation to novel environments through learned exploration strategies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：元强化学习引导语言智能体进行探索
强化学习（RL）已能训练大型语言模型（LLM）智能体与环境交互，以解决多轮长程任务。然而，RL训练的智能体在需要主动探索的任务中常表现不佳，且难以从试错经验中高效适应。本文提出LaMer，一种通用的元强化学习框架，使LLM智能体能在测试时主动探索并从环境反馈中学习。LaMer包含两个关键组件：（i）跨回合训练框架，以鼓励探索和长期奖励优化；（ii）通过反思进行上下文策略适应，使智能体无需梯度更新即可根据任务反馈信号调整策略。多环境实验表明，LaMer性能显著优于RL基线，在Sokoban、扫雷和Webshop任务上分别提升11%、14%和19%。此外，与RL训练的智能体相比，LaMer在更具挑战性或未见任务上展现出更好的泛化能力。总体而言，我们的结果表明，元强化学习为语言智能体提供了一种引导探索的原则性方法，通过习得的探索策略实现对新颖环境更稳健的适应。

Helix: Evolutionary Reinforcement Learning for Open-Ended Scientific Problem Solving
Authors: Chang Su, Zhongkai Hao, Zhizhou Zhang, Zeyu Xia, Youjia Wu, Hang Su, Jun Zhu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-08T14:08:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T14:08:52+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) with reasoning abilities have demonstrated growing promise for tackling complex scientific problems. Yet such tasks are inherently domain-specific, unbounded and open-ended, demanding exploration across vast and flexible solution spaces. Existing approaches, whether purely learning-based or reliant on carefully designed workflows, often suffer from limited exploration efficiency and poor generalization. To overcome these challenges, we present HELIX -- a Hierarchical Evolutionary reinforcement Learning framework with In-context eXperiences. HELIX introduces two key novelties: (i) a diverse yet high-quality pool of candidate solutions that broadens exploration through in-context learning, and (ii) reinforcement learning for iterative policy refinement that progressively elevates solution quality. This synergy enables the discovery of more advanced solutions. On the circle packing task, HELIX achieves state-of-the-art result with a sum of radii of 2.63598308 using only a 14B model. Across standard machine learning benchmarks, HELIX further surpasses GPT-4o with a carefully engineered pipeline, delivering an average F1 improvement of 5.95 points on the Adult and Bank Marketing datasets.

标题：Helix：面向开放式科学问题求解的进化强化学习框架

Exoskeleton Control through Learning to Reduce Biological Joint Moments in Simulations
Authors: Zihang You, Xianlian Zhou
First: 2026-03-08T13:31:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T13:31:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Data-driven joint-moment predictors offer a scalable alternative to laboratory-based inverse-dynamics pipelines for biomechanics estimation and exoskeleton control. Meanwhile, physics-based reinforcement learning (RL) enables simulation-trained controllers to learn dynamics-aware assistance strategies without extensive human experimentation. However, quantitative verification of simulation-trained exoskeleton torque predictors, and their impact on human joint power injection, remains limited. This paper presents (1) an RL framework to learn exoskeleton assistance policies that reduce biological joint moments, and (2) a validation pipeline that verifies the trained control networks using an open-source gait dataset through inference and comparison with biological joint moments. Simulation-trained multilayer perceptron (MLP) controllers are developed for level-ground and ramp walking, mapping short-horizon histories of bilateral hip and knee kinematics to normalized assistance torques. Results show that predicted assistance preserves task-intensity trends across speeds and inclines. Agreement is particularly strong at the hip, with cross-correlation coefficients reaching 0.94 at 1.8 m/s and 0.98 during 5° decline walking, demonstrating near-matched temporal structure. Discrepancies increase at higher speeds and steeper inclines, especially at the knee, and are more pronounced in joint power comparisons. Delay tuning biases assistance toward greater positive power injection; modest timing shifts increase positive power and improve agreement in specific gait intervals. Together, these results establish a quantitative validation framework for simulation-trained exoskeleton controllers, demonstrate strong sim-to-data consistency at the torque level, and highlight both the promise and the remaining challenges for sim-to-real transfer.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过仿真学习降低生物关节力矩的外骨骼控制方法

This paper is motivated by the need for scalable, data-driven methods to estimate biomechanics and control exoskeletons, leveraging physics-based reinforcement learning (RL) to develop assistance strategies without extensive human trials, yet quantitative validation of such simulation-trained controllers remains limited. The method introduces an RL framework to learn exoskeleton policies that reduce biological joint moments, along with a validation pipeline using an open-source gait dataset to compare predicted assistance torques from multilayer perceptron controllers against biological joint moments for level-ground and ramp walking. 本文的动机在于需要可扩展的数据驱动方法来估计生物力学和控制外骨骼，利用基于物理的强化学习开发辅助策略而无需大量人体实验，但此类仿真训练控制器的定量验证仍显不足。方法上提出了一个强化学习框架来学习降低生物关节力矩的外骨骼策略，并结合一个验证流程，使用开源步态数据集，将多层感知机控制器预测的辅助力矩与生物关节力矩进行比较，适用于平地与斜坡行走。实验结果表明，预测的辅助能保持不同速度和坡度下的任务强度趋势，在髋关节处一致性较强（互相关系数高达0.94-0.98），但在更高速度和更陡坡度下差异增大，尤其在膝关节功率方面，延迟调整可提高正功率注入并在特定步态区间改善时间一致性，从而建立了一个验证框架并凸显了仿真到现实迁移的挑战。
Evolving Diffusion and Flow Matching Policies for Online Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Chubin Zhang, Zhenglin Wan, Feng Chen, Fuchao Yang, Lang Feng, Yaxin Zhou, Xingrui Yu, Yang You, Ivor Tsang, Bo An
First: 2025-12-02T09:49:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T12:44:32+00:00
Comments: Ver 2
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Diffusion and flow matching policies offer expressive, multimodal action modeling, yet they are frequently unstable in online reinforcement learning (RL) due to intractable likelihoods and gradients propagating through long sampling chains. Conversely, tractable parameterizations such as Gaussians lack the expressiveness needed for complex control -- exposing a persistent tension between optimization stability and representational power. We address this tension with a key structural principle: decoupling optimization from generation. Building on this, we introduce GoRL (Generative Online Reinforcement Learning), an algorithm-agnostic framework that trains expressive policies from scratch by confining policy optimization to a tractable latent space while delegating action synthesis to a conditional generative decoder. Using a two-timescale alternating schedule and anchoring decoder refinement to a fixed prior, GoRL enables stable optimization while continuously expanding expressiveness. Empirically, GoRL consistently outperforms unimodal and generative baselines across diverse continuous-control tasks. Notably, on the challenging HopperStand task, it achieves episodic returns exceeding 870 -- more than $3\times$ that of the strongest baseline -- demonstrating a practical path to policies that are both stable and highly expressive. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/bennidict23/GoRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向在线强化学习的扩散与流匹配策略演进
扩散与流匹配策略虽能提供富有表现力的多模态动作建模，但在在线强化学习中常因难以处理的似然函数和长采样链梯度传播而失稳。相比之下，高斯分布等易处理参数化方法又缺乏复杂控制所需的表达能力——这揭示了优化稳定性与表征能力间的持久矛盾。我们通过一个关键结构原则解决这一矛盾：将优化与生成解耦。基于此，我们提出GoRL（生成式在线强化学习），这是一个算法无关的框架，通过将策略优化限制在易处理的隐空间，并将动作合成委托给条件生成解码器，从而从零开始训练高表达能力策略。采用双时间尺度交替调度并将解码器优化锚定于固定先验，GoRL在持续扩展表达能力的同时实现了稳定优化。实验表明，GoRL在多样连续控制任务中持续优于单模态与生成式基线。值得注意的是，在挑战性的HopperStand任务中，其回合回报超过870——达到最强基线的3倍以上——为兼具稳定性与高表达能力的策略提供了可行路径。代码已开源：https://github.com/bennidict23/GoRL。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the tension between the expressive, multimodal action modeling of diffusion and flow matching policies and their instability in online reinforcement learning (RL) due to intractable likelihoods and long sampling chains, compared to tractable but less expressive unimodal policies. To address this, the method introduces GoRL, an algorithm-agnostic framework that decouples optimization from generation by confining policy optimization to a tractable latent space and using a conditional generative decoder for action synthesis, stabilized via a two-timescale alternating schedule and anchoring to a fixed prior. The main experimental results show that GoRL consistently outperforms unimodal and generative baselines across diverse continuous-control tasks, achieving episodic returns exceeding 870 on the challenging HopperStand task, which is more than three times the strongest baseline, demonstrating stable and highly expressive policies.
本文的动机在于扩散和流匹配策略在在线强化学习中虽能提供表达性强、多模态的动作建模，但由于难以处理的似然和长采样链导致不稳定，而易于优化的单模态策略则表达能力不足。为解决这一矛盾，方法提出了GoRL，这是一个算法无关的框架，通过将策略优化限制在易于处理的潜在空间，并使用条件生成解码器进行动作合成，实现了优化与生成的解耦，并采用双时间尺度交替调度和固定先验锚定来确保稳定性。主要实验结果表明，GoRL在多种连续控制任务中持续优于单模态和生成基线，在具有挑战性的HopperStand任务上获得了超过870的回合回报，是最强基线的三倍以上，证明了其稳定且高表达性的策略能力。
A Champion-level Vision-based Reinforcement Learning Agent for Competitive Racing in Gran Turismo 7
Authors: Hojoon Lee, Takuma Seno, Jun Jet Tai, Kaushik Subramanian, Kenta Kawamoto, Peter Stone, Peter R. Wurman
First: 2025-04-12T00:20:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T11:22:13+00:00
Comments: Accepted for Publication at the IEEE Robotics and Automation Letters (RA-L) 2025
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep reinforcement learning has achieved superhuman racing performance in high-fidelity simulators like Gran Turismo 7 (GT7). It typically utilizes global features that require instrumentation external to a car, such as precise localization of agents and opponents, limiting real-world applicability. To address this limitation, we introduce a vision-based autonomous racing agent that relies solely on ego-centric camera views and onboard sensor data, eliminating the need for precise localization during inference. This agent employs an asymmetric actor-critic framework: the actor uses a recurrent neural network with the sensor data local to the car to retain track layouts and opponent positions, while the critic accesses the global features during training. Evaluated in GT7, our agent consistently outperforms GT7's built-drivers. To our knowledge, this work presents the first vision-based autonomous racing agent to demonstrate champion-level performance in competitive racing scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：《Gran Turismo 7》竞技赛车场景中冠军级视觉强化学习智能体的研究
深度强化学习已在《Gran Turismo 7》等高保真模拟器中实现超越人类的赛车性能。传统方法通常依赖需要车辆外部仪器的全局特征（如智能体与对手的精确定位），限制了实际应用。为突破此局限，我们提出一种仅依赖以自我为中心的摄像头视角与车载传感器数据的视觉自主赛车智能体，在推理过程中无需精确定位。该智能体采用非对称行动者-评论家框架：行动者通过循环神经网络处理车辆本地传感器数据以记忆赛道布局与对手位置，评论家则在训练期间访问全局特征。在《Gran Turismo 7》中的评估表明，该智能体持续超越游戏内置驾驶员。据我们所知，本研究首次实现了在竞技赛车场景中展现冠军级性能的视觉自主赛车智能体。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of prior deep reinforcement learning agents that rely on external instrumentation for precise localization, which hinders real-world deployment, this paper introduces a vision-based autonomous racing agent that uses only ego-centric camera views and onboard sensors during inference. The method employs an asymmetric actor-critic framework where the actor, a recurrent neural network, processes local sensor data to retain track and opponent information, while the critic leverages global features during training to guide learning. Experimental results in Gran Turismo 7 demonstrate that the agent consistently outperforms the game's built-in drivers, achieving champion-level performance in competitive racing scenarios, marking a significant step toward real-world applicability.
针对先前依赖外部仪器进行精确定位的深度强化学习智能体在现实世界应用受限的问题，本文提出了一种仅使用自中心摄像头视角和车载传感器的视觉自主赛车智能体。该方法采用非对称行动者-评论家框架：行动者通过循环神经网络处理局部传感器数据以记忆赛道布局和对手位置，而评论家在训练期间利用全局特征指导学习。在《GT赛车7》中的实验结果表明，该智能体持续超越游戏内置驾驶员，在竞争性赛车场景中达到冠军级性能，标志着向现实世界应用迈出了重要一步。
Constraints Matrix Diffusion based Generative Neural Solver for Vehicle Routing Problems
Authors: Zhenwei Wang, Tiehua Zhang, Ning Xue, Ender Ozcan, Ling Wang, Ruibin Bai
First: 2026-03-08T10:03:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T10:03:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Over the past decade, neural network solvers powered by generative artificial intelligence have garnered significant attention in the domain of vehicle routing problems (VRPs), owing to their exceptional computational efficiency and superior reasoning capabilities. In particular, autoregressive solvers integrated with reinforcement learning have emerged as a prominent trend. However, much of the existing work emphasizes large-scale generalization of neural approaches while neglecting the limited robustness of attention-based methods across heterogeneous distributions of problem parameters. Their improvements over heuristic search remain largely restricted to hand-curated, fixed-distribution benchmarks. Furthermore, these architectures tend to degrade significantly when node representations are highly similar or when tasks involve long decision horizons. To address the aforementioned limitations, we propose a novel fusion neural network framework that employs a discrete noise graph diffusion model to learn the underlying constraints of vehicle routing problems and generate a constraint assignment matrix. This matrix is subsequently integrated adaptively into the feature representation learning and decision process of the autoregressive solver, serving as a graph structure mask that facilitates the formation of solutions characterized by both global vision and local feature integration. To the best of our knowledge, this work represents the first comprehensive experimental investigation of neural network model solvers across a 378-combinatorial space spanning four distinct dimensions within the CVRPlib public dataset. Extensive experimental evaluations demonstrate that our proposed fusion model effectively captures and leverages problem constraints, achieving state-of-the-art performance across multiple benchmark datasets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于约束矩阵扩散的生成式神经网络求解器在车辆路径问题中的应用
过去十年间，基于生成式人工智能的神经网络求解器因其卓越的计算效率和推理能力，在车辆路径问题领域受到广泛关注。其中，结合强化学习的自回归求解器已成为主流趋势。然而，现有研究多侧重于神经网络方法的大规模泛化能力，却忽视了基于注意力机制的方法在问题参数异质分布下鲁棒性不足的缺陷。这些方法对启发式搜索的改进仍主要局限于人工构建的固定分布基准测试集。此外，当节点表征高度相似或任务决策周期较长时，此类架构性能往往显著下降。为克服上述局限，本文提出一种新型融合神经网络框架：采用离散噪声图扩散模型学习车辆路径问题的底层约束，生成约束分配矩阵。该矩阵随后自适应地整合到自回归求解器的特征表征学习与决策过程中，作为图结构掩码，促进形成兼具全局视野与局部特征融合的解决方案。据我们所知，本研究首次在CVRPlib公开数据集的四维378组合空间中对神经网络模型求解器进行了系统性实验验证。大量实验评估表明，所提出的融合模型能有效捕捉并利用问题约束，在多个基准数据集上实现了最先进的性能表现。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limited robustness and generalization of existing autoregressive neural solvers for vehicle routing problems (VRPs), especially under heterogeneous parameter distributions or with highly similar node representations, this paper introduces a novel fusion neural network framework. The method employs a discrete noise graph diffusion model to learn VRP constraints and generate a constraint assignment matrix, which is adaptively integrated into an autoregressive solver's feature representation and decision process as a graph structure mask, enabling solutions with global vision and local feature integration. Experimental results, including a comprehensive evaluation across a 378-combinatorial space in the CVRPlib dataset, demonstrate that the proposed model effectively captures constraints and achieves state-of-the-art performance on multiple benchmarks.
针对现有基于自回归的车辆路径问题神经求解器在异构参数分布或节点表示高度相似时鲁棒性和泛化能力不足的问题，本文提出了一种新颖的融合神经网络框架。该方法采用离散噪声图扩散模型学习问题约束并生成约束分配矩阵，将其作为图结构掩码自适应地集成到自回归求解器的特征表示与决策过程中，从而形成兼具全局视野与局部特征整合的解决方案。实验结果表明，在CVRPlib数据集上跨越四个维度的378种组合空间进行全面评估后，所提出的模型能有效捕捉并利用约束，在多个基准测试中取得了最先进的性能。
COOL-MC: Verifying and Explaining RL Policies for Multi-bridge Network Maintenance
Authors: Dennis Gross
First: 2026-03-08T09:11:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T09:11:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aging bridge networks require proactive, verifiable, and interpretable maintenance strategies, yet reinforcement learning (RL) policies trained solely on reward signals provide no formal safety guarantees and remain opaque to infrastructure managers. We demonstrate COOL-MC as a tool for verifying and explaining RL policies for multi-bridge network maintenance, building on a single-bridge Markov decision process (MDP) from the literature and extending it to a parallel network of three heterogeneous bridges with a shared periodic budget constraint, encoded in the PRISM modeling language. We train an RL agent on this MDP and apply probabilistic model checking and explainability methods to the induced discrete-time Markov chain (DTMC) that arises from the interaction between the learned policy and the underlying MDP. Probabilistic model checking reveals that the trained policy has a safety-violation probability of 3.5\% over the planning horizon, being slightly above the theoretical minimum of 0\% and indicating the suboptimality of the learned policy, noting that these results are based on artificially constructed transition probabilities and deterioration rates rather than real-world data, so absolute performance figures should be interpreted with caution. The explainability analysis further reveals, for instance, a systematic bias in the trained policy toward the state of bridge 1 over the remaining bridges in the network. These results demonstrate COOL-MC's ability to provide formal, interpretable, and practical analysis of RL maintenance policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：COOL-MC：多桥梁网络维护中强化学习策略的验证与解释
老化的桥梁网络需要主动、可验证且可解释的维护策略，但仅基于奖励信号训练的强化学习（RL）策略缺乏正式的安全保证，且对基础设施管理者而言仍不透明。本文展示了COOL-MC作为验证和解释多桥梁网络维护RL策略的工具，基于文献中的单桥梁马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），将其扩展为具有共享周期性预算约束的三座异质桥梁并行网络，并使用PRISM建模语言进行编码。我们在此MDP上训练RL智能体，并对由学习策略与底层MDP交互产生的离散时间马尔可夫链（DTMC）应用概率模型检验与可解释性方法。概率模型检验显示，训练策略在规划周期内的安全违规概率为3.5%，略高于理论最小值0%，表明学习策略的次优性；需注意这些结果基于人工构建的转移概率与退化率而非真实数据，因此绝对性能指标应谨慎解读。可解释性分析进一步揭示，例如训练策略对网络中桥梁1的状态存在系统性偏好。这些结果证明了COOL-MC为RL维护策略提供形式化、可解释且实用分析的能力。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the lack of formal safety guarantees and interpretability in reinforcement learning (RL) policies for maintaining aging bridge networks. The method involves developing COOL-MC, a tool that extends a single-bridge Markov decision process (MDP) to a network of three heterogeneous bridges with a shared budget, encodes it in PRISM, trains an RL agent, and then applies probabilistic model checking and explainability methods to the resulting discrete-time Markov chain. The main experimental results show that the trained policy has a 3.5% safety-violation probability, slightly above the theoretical minimum, indicating suboptimality, and explainability analysis reveals a systematic bias in the policy toward one bridge over others, demonstrating COOL-MC's ability to provide formal and interpretable analysis.
本研究的动机是解决用于老化桥梁网络维护的强化学习策略缺乏形式化安全保证和可解释性的问题。方法上，开发了COOL-MC工具，将文献中的单桥马尔可夫决策过程扩展为具有共享预算约束的三座异质桥梁并行网络，使用PRISM建模语言编码，训练强化学习智能体，并对由此产生的离散时间马尔可夫链应用概率模型检验和可解释性方法。主要实验结果表明，训练出的策略安全违规概率为3.5%，略高于理论最小值，表明其并非最优；可解释性分析进一步揭示了该策略对网络中一座桥梁存在系统性偏好，这证明了COOL-MC能为强化学习维护策略提供形式化、可解释且实用的分析能力。
A Simple and Effective Reinforcement Learning Method for Text-to-Image Diffusion Fine-tuning
Authors: Shashank Gupta, Chaitanya Ahuja, Tsung-Yu Lin, Sreya Dutta Roy, Harrie Oosterhuis, Maarten de Rijke, Satya Narayan Shukla
First: 2025-03-02T13:43:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T08:38:17+00:00
Comments: Published at Transactions on Machine Learning Research (TMLR), 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL)-based fine-tuning has emerged as a powerful approach for aligning diffusion models with black-box objectives. Proximal policy optimization (PPO) is a popular choice of method for policy optimization. While effective in terms of performance and sample complexity, PPO is highly sensitive to hyper-parameters and involves substantial computational overhead. REINFORCE, on the other hand, mitigates some implementation complexities such as high memory overhead and sensitive hyper-parameter tuning, but has suboptimal performance due to high variance and crucially sample inefficiency, which is the primary notion of efficiency we study in this work. While the variance of the REINFORCE can be reduced by sampling multiple actions per input prompt and using a baseline correction term, it still suffers from sample inefficiency. To address these challenges, we systematically analyze the sample efficiency-effectiveness trade-off between REINFORCE and PPO, and propose leave-one-out PPO ( LOOP), a novel RL for diffusion fine-tuning method. LOOP combines variance reduction techniques from REINFORCE, such as sampling multiple actions per input prompt and a baseline correction term, with the robustness and sample efficiency of PPO via clipping and importance sampling. Our results demonstrate that LOOP effectively improves diffusion models on various black-box objectives, and achieves a better balance between sample efficiency and final performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种简单有效的文本到图像扩散模型微调强化学习方法
基于强化学习（RL）的微调已成为将扩散模型与黑盒目标对齐的强大方法。近端策略优化（PPO）是策略优化的常用选择，虽然在性能和样本复杂度方面有效，但PPO对超参数高度敏感且计算开销大。相比之下，REINFORCE减少了高内存开销和敏感超参数调优等实现复杂性，但由于高方差和关键的样本低效性（本文研究的核心效率指标），其性能欠佳。尽管可通过每个输入提示采样多个动作并使用基线校正项降低REINFORCE的方差，样本低效问题依然存在。为应对这些挑战，我们系统分析了REINFORCE与PPO在样本效率与效果间的权衡，并提出留一法PPO（LOOP）——一种新颖的扩散模型微调强化学习方法。LOOP结合了REINFORCE的方差缩减技术（如多动作采样和基线校正项）与PPO通过剪裁和重要性采样实现的鲁棒性及样本效率。实验表明，LOOP能有效提升扩散模型在各种黑盒目标上的性能，并在样本效率与最终性能间取得更好平衡。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitations of existing reinforcement learning methods for fine-tuning text-to-image diffusion models, where PPO is sample-efficient but computationally heavy and hyperparameter-sensitive, while REINFORCE is simpler but suffers from high variance and poor sample efficiency. The authors propose Leave-One-Out PPO (LOOP), a novel method that integrates variance reduction techniques from REINFORCE, such as multiple action sampling and baseline correction, with the robustness and efficiency of PPO via clipping and importance sampling. Experimental results show that LOOP effectively improves diffusion models on various black-box objectives, achieving a superior balance between sample efficiency and final performance.
本文针对现有强化学习方法在微调文本到图像扩散模型时的局限性展开研究，其中PPO方法样本效率高但计算开销大且对超参数敏感，而REINFORCE方法虽简化了实现却存在高方差和样本效率低的问题。作者提出了留一法PPO（LOOP）这一新方法，它结合了REINFORCE中的方差减少技术（如多动作采样和基线校正）与PPO通过裁剪和重要性采样实现的鲁棒性和样本效率。实验结果表明，LOOP能有效提升扩散模型在各种黑盒目标上的性能，并在样本效率和最终性能之间取得了更好的平衡。
Reinforcement learning-based dynamic cleaning scheduling framework for solar energy system
Authors: Heungjo An
Venue: Journal of Korean Institute of Intelligent Systems, 35(1), 84-97, 2025
First: 2026-03-08T08:13:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T08:13:36+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 6 figures, This is an accepted manuscript of the article published in Journal of Korean Institute of Intelligent Systems, 35(1), 84-97, 2025
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Advancing autonomous green technologies in solar photovoltaic (PV) systems is key to improving sustainability and efficiency in renewable energy production. This study presents a reinforcement learning (RL)-based framework to autonomously optimize the cleaning schedules of PV panels in arid regions, where soiling from dust and other airborne particles significantly reduces energy output. By employing advanced RL algorithms, Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) and Soft Actor-Critic (SAC), the framework dynamically adjusts cleaning intervals based on uncertain environmental conditions. The proposed approach was applied to a case study in Abu Dhabi, UAE, demonstrating that PPO outperformed SAC and traditional simulation optimization (Sim-Opt) methods, achieving up to 13% cost savings by dynamically responding to weather uncertainties. The results highlight the superiority of flexible, autonomous scheduling over fixed-interval methods, particularly in adapting to stochastic environmental dynamics. This aligns with the goals of autonomous green energy production by reducing operational costs and improving the efficiency of solar power generation systems. This work underscores the potential of RL-driven autonomous decision-making to optimize maintenance operations in renewable energy systems. In future research, it is important to enhance the generalization ability of the proposed RL model, while also considering additional factors and constraints to apply it to different regions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习的太阳能系统动态清洁调度框架

Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to enhance sustainability and efficiency in solar energy production, particularly in arid regions where soiling reduces PV panel output, this study proposes a reinforcement learning (RL) framework to dynamically optimize cleaning schedules. The method employs Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) and Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) algorithms to adjust cleaning intervals based on uncertain environmental conditions. In a case study in Abu Dhabi, PPO outperformed SAC and traditional simulation optimization, achieving up to 13% cost savings by flexibly adapting to weather uncertainties, demonstrating the superiority of autonomous scheduling over fixed methods for improving operational efficiency in renewable energy systems.
本研究旨在提高太阳能生产的可持续性和效率，特别是在积尘降低光伏板输出的干旱地区，提出了一个基于强化学习的动态清洁调度框架。方法采用近端策略优化和柔性演员-评论家算法，根据不确定的环境条件调整清洁间隔。在阿布扎比的案例研究中，近端策略优化优于柔性演员-评论家及传统模拟优化方法，通过灵活适应天气不确定性实现了高达13%的成本节约，证明了自主调度相对于固定方法在提升可再生能源系统运行效率方面的优越性。
InterReal: A Unified Physics-Based Imitation Framework for Learning Human-Object Interaction Skills
Authors: Dayang Liang, Yuhang Lin, Xinzhe Liu, Jiyuan Shi, Yunlong Liu, Chenjia Bai
First: 2026-03-08T07:44:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T07:44:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Interaction is one of the core abilities of humanoid robots. However, most existing frameworks focus on non-interactive whole-body control, which limits their practical applicability. In this work, we develop InterReal, a unified physics-based imitation learning framework for Real-world human-object Interaction (HOI) control. InterReal enables humanoid robots to track HOI reference motions, facilitating the learning of fine-grained interactive skills and their deployment in real-world settings. Within this framework, we first introduce a HOI motion data augmentation scheme with hand-object contact constraints, and utilize the augmented motions to improve policy stability under object perturbations. Second, we propose an automatic reward learner to address the challenge of large-scale reward shaping. A meta-policy guided by critical tracking error metrics explores and allocates reward signals to the low-level reinforcement learning objective, which enables more effective learning of interactive policies. Experiments on HOI tasks of box-picking and box-pushing demonstrate that InterReal achieves the best tracking accuracy and the highest task success rate compared to recent baselines. Furthermore, we validate the framework on the real-world robot Unitree G1, which demonstrates its practical effectiveness and robustness beyond simulation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：InterReal：一种基于物理的统一模仿框架，用于学习人-物交互技能
交互是人形机器人的核心能力之一。然而，现有框架大多专注于非交互式的全身控制，限制了其实际应用。本研究提出了InterReal，一个基于物理的统一模仿学习框架，用于现实世界中人-物交互控制。该框架使人形机器人能够跟踪HOI参考动作，促进细粒度交互技能的学习及其在真实场景中的部署。框架中，我们首先引入了一种带手-物接触约束的HOI动作数据增强方案，并利用增强动作提升策略在物体扰动下的稳定性；其次，提出了一种自动奖励学习器以应对大规模奖励设计的挑战，通过关键跟踪误差指标引导的元策略探索并将奖励信号分配至底层强化学习目标，从而更有效地学习交互策略。在取箱和推箱等HOI任务上的实验表明，InterReal相比近期基线方法实现了最优跟踪精度和最高任务成功率。此外，我们在真实机器人Unitree G1上验证了该框架，证明了其在仿真环境之外的实际有效性和鲁棒性。

Why Code, Why Now: Learnability, Computability, and the Real Limits of Machine Learning
Authors: Zhimin Zhao
First: 2026-02-15T00:14:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T06:03:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Code generation has progressed more reliably than reinforcement learning, largely because code has an information structure that makes it learnable. Code provides dense, local, verifiable feedback at every token, whereas most reinforcement learning problems do not. This difference in feedback quality is not binary but graded. We propose a five-level hierarchy of learnability based on information structure and argue that the ceiling on ML progress depends less on model size than on whether a task is learnable at all. The hierarchy rests on a formal distinction among three properties of computational problems (expressibility, computability, and learnability). We establish their pairwise relationships, including where implications hold and where they fail, and present a unified template that makes the structural differences explicit. The analysis suggests why supervised learning on code scales predictably while reinforcement learning does not, and why the common assumption that scaling alone will solve remaining ML challenges warrants scrutiny.
中文标题/摘要
标题：为何是代码，为何是现在：可学习性、可计算性与机器学习的真实局限
代码生成比强化学习进展更稳定，主要因为代码具有使其可学习的信息结构。代码在每个标记处提供密集、局部、可验证的反馈，而大多数强化学习问题则不然。这种反馈质量的差异并非二元对立而是渐进的。我们基于信息结构提出五级可学习性层次，并论证机器学习进展的上限更取决于任务是否可学习，而非模型规模。该层次建立在计算问题三个属性（可表达性、可计算性、可学习性）的形式化区分之上。我们确立了它们之间的两两关系，包括哪些蕴含关系成立、哪些失效，并提出使结构差异显式化的统一模板。分析揭示了为何代码的监督学习可预测地扩展而强化学习不能，以及为何'仅靠扩展就能解决剩余机器学习挑战'这一普遍假设值得审视。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the observation that code generation advances more reliably than reinforcement learning, attributing this to the superior information structure of code which provides dense, local, and verifiable feedback per token. The method involves proposing a five-level hierarchy of learnability based on information structure, formally distinguishing expressibility, computability, and learnability, and analyzing their relationships through a unified template. The main experimental results are conceptual, showing that the ceiling on machine learning progress depends more on a task's inherent learnability than on model scaling, thereby explaining why supervised learning on code scales predictably while reinforcement learning often does not.
本文的动机源于观察到代码生成比强化学习进展更可靠，这归因于代码具有优越的信息结构，能为每个标记提供密集、局部且可验证的反馈。方法上，作者提出了一个基于信息结构的五级可学习性层次，形式化区分了可表达性、可计算性和可学习性，并通过统一模板分析了它们之间的关系。主要实验结果属于概念性分析，表明机器学习进展的上限更多取决于任务本身的可学习性而非模型规模，从而解释了为什么代码的监督学习可预测地扩展，而强化学习则往往不能。
Mean Flow Policy with Instantaneous Velocity Constraint for One-step Action Generation
Authors: Guojian Zhan, Letian Tao, Pengcheng Wang, Yixiao Wang, Yiheng Li, Yuxin Chen, Hongyang Li, Masayoshi Tomizuka, Shengbo Eben Li
Venue: ICLR Oral Presentation
First: 2026-02-14T14:44:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T04:57:06+00:00
Comments: ICLR Oral Presentation
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning expressive and efficient policy functions is a promising direction in reinforcement learning (RL). While flow-based policies have recently proven effective in modeling complex action distributions with a fast deterministic sampling process, they still face a trade-off between expressiveness and computational burden, which is typically controlled by the number of flow steps. In this work, we propose mean velocity policy (MVP), a new generative policy function that models the mean velocity field to achieve the fastest one-step action generation. To ensure its high expressiveness, an instantaneous velocity constraint (IVC) is introduced on the mean velocity field during training. We theoretically prove that this design explicitly serves as a crucial boundary condition, thereby improving learning accuracy and enhancing policy expressiveness. Empirically, our MVP achieves state-of-the-art success rates across several challenging robotic manipulation tasks from Robomimic and OGBench. It also delivers substantial improvements in training and inference speed over existing flow-based policy baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于瞬时速度约束的均值流策略用于一步动作生成
学习表达力强且高效的政策函数是强化学习（RL）中一个前景广阔的方向。尽管基于流的策略最近被证明能通过快速确定性采样过程有效建模复杂动作分布，它们仍面临表达力与计算负担之间的权衡，这通常由流步骤数量控制。本文提出均值速度策略（MVP），这是一种新的生成式政策函数，通过建模均值速度场实现最快的一步动作生成。为确保其高表达力，训练过程中在均值速度场上引入了瞬时速度约束（IVC）。我们从理论上证明，该设计明确起到了关键边界条件的作用，从而提升学习精度并增强策略表达力。实证表明，我们的MVP在Robomimic和OGBench的多个挑战性机器人操作任务中达到了最先进的成功率，同时在训练和推理速度上较现有基于流的策略基线有显著提升。

To address this, the authors propose the Mean Velocity Policy (MVP), a generative policy that models the mean velocity field to enable one-step action generation, and introduce an Instantaneous Velocity Constraint (IVC) during training to enhance expressiveness by acting as a boundary condition. Distributionally Robust Self Paced Curriculum Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Anirudh Satheesh, Keenan Powell, Vaneet Aggarwal
First: 2025-11-07T20:25:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T03:27:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A central challenge in reinforcement learning is that policies trained in controlled environments often fail under distribution shifts at deployment into real-world environments. Distributionally Robust Reinforcement Learning (DRRL) addresses this by optimizing for worst-case performance within an uncertainty set defined by a robustness budget $ε$. However, fixing $ε$ results in a tradeoff between performance and robustness: small values yield high nominal performance but weak robustness, while large values can result in instability and overly conservative policies. We propose Distributionally Robust Self-Paced Curriculum Reinforcement Learning (DR-SPCRL), a method that overcomes this limitation by treating $ε$ as a continuous curriculum. DR-SPCRL adaptively schedules the robustness budget according to the agent's progress, enabling a balance between nominal and robust performance. Empirical results across multiple environments demonstrate that DR-SPCRL not only stabilizes training but also achieves a superior robustness-performance trade-off, yielding an average 11.8\% increase in episodic return under varying perturbations compared to fixed or heuristic scheduling strategies, and achieving approximately 1.9$\times$ the performance of the corresponding nominal RL algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分布鲁棒自步课程强化学习
强化学习中的一个核心挑战是，在受控环境中训练的策略在部署到现实世界时，常因分布偏移而失效。分布鲁棒强化学习通过在一个由鲁棒性预算$ε$定义的不确定性集合内优化最坏情况性能来解决此问题。然而，固定$ε$会导致性能与鲁棒性之间的权衡：较小的值能获得较高的标称性能但鲁棒性较弱，而较大的值可能导致训练不稳定和策略过于保守。我们提出分布鲁棒自步课程强化学习方法，该方法将$ε$视为连续课程，从而克服了这一限制。DR-SPCRL根据智能体的学习进度自适应地调度鲁棒性预算，实现了标称性能与鲁棒性能的平衡。在多个环境中的实验结果表明，DR-SPCRL不仅稳定了训练过程，还实现了更优的鲁棒性-性能权衡：与固定或启发式调度策略相比，在多种扰动下其回合回报平均提升11.8%，且性能达到相应标称强化学习算法的约1.9倍。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge in reinforcement learning where policies trained in controlled settings often fail under real-world distribution shifts, noting that Distributionally Robust Reinforcement Learning (DRRL) with a fixed robustness budget creates a trade-off between performance and robustness. To overcome this, the authors propose Distributionally Robust Self-Paced Curriculum Reinforcement Learning (DR-SPCRL), which treats the robustness budget as a continuous curriculum and adaptively schedules it based on the agent's learning progress to balance nominal and robust performance. Experimental results across multiple environments show that DR-SPCRL stabilizes training and achieves a superior robustness-performance trade-off, yielding an average 11.8% increase in episodic return under perturbations and approximately 1.9 times the performance of nominal RL algorithms compared to fixed or heuristic scheduling strategies.
本文针对强化学习中策略在受控环境中训练后常因现实世界分布变化而失效的挑战，指出采用固定鲁棒性预算的分布鲁棒强化学习（DRRL）会导致性能与鲁棒性之间的权衡问题。为此，作者提出了分布鲁棒自步课程强化学习（DR-SPCRL），该方法将鲁棒性预算视为连续课程，并根据智能体的学习进度自适应调度，以平衡名义性能和鲁棒性能。在多个环境中的实验结果表明，DR-SPCRL稳定了训练过程，实现了更优的鲁棒性-性能权衡，在扰动下平均回合回报提高了11.8%，且性能约为名义强化学习算法的1.9倍，优于固定或启发式调度策略。
Cost-Driven Representation Learning for Linear Quadratic Gaussian Control: Part II
Authors: Yi Tian, Kaiqing Zhang, Russ Tedrake, Suvrit Sra
First: 2026-03-08T03:20:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T03:20:52+00:00
Comments: 38 pages; preliminary version appeared in IEEE CDC 2023; this is the extended journal version, with an end-to-end guarantee added
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the problem of state representation learning for control from partial and potentially high-dimensional observations. We approach this problem via cost-driven state representation learning, in which we learn a dynamical model in a latent state space by predicting cumulative costs. In particular, we establish finite-sample guarantees on finding a near-optimal representation function and a near-optimal controller using the learned latent model for infinite-horizon time-invariant Linear Quadratic Gaussian (LQG) control. We study two approaches to cost-driven representation learning, which differ in whether the transition function of the latent state is learned explicitly or implicitly. The first approach has also been investigated in Part I of this work, for finite-horizon time-varying LQG control. The second approach closely resembles MuZero, a recent breakthrough in empirical reinforcement learning, in that it learns latent dynamics implicitly by predicting cumulative costs. A key technical contribution of this Part II is to prove persistency of excitation for a new stochastic process that arises from the analysis of quadratic regression in our approach, and may be of independent interest.
中文标题/摘要
标题：线性二次高斯控制的成本驱动表征学习：第二部分
我们研究从部分且可能高维的观测中学习控制所需的状态表征问题。通过成本驱动的状态表征学习方法，在潜在状态空间中通过学习预测累积成本来建立动态模型。特别地，我们针对无限时域时不变线性二次高斯控制，证明了使用学习得到的潜在模型寻找近似最优表征函数和近似最优控制器的有限样本保证。我们研究了两种成本驱动表征学习途径，区别在于潜在状态的转移函数是显式学习还是隐式学习。第一种途径在本研究第一部分中已针对有限时域时变LQG控制进行探讨。第二种途径与近期实证强化学习的突破性成果MuZero高度相似，通过预测累积成本隐式学习潜在动态。本第二部分的关键技术贡献在于证明了一种新型随机过程的持续激励性，该过程产生于我们方法中二次回归的分析过程，可能具有独立研究价值。

This paper addresses the challenge of learning state representations for control from partial, high-dimensional observations by introducing cost-driven representation learning, where a latent dynamical model is learned by predicting cumulative costs. The method explores two approaches: one with an explicit latent transition function and another, resembling MuZero, that learns dynamics implicitly through cost prediction, both aimed at infinite-horizon Linear Quadratic Gaussian (LQG) control. The main experimental results establish finite-sample guarantees for finding near-optimal representations and controllers, with a key technical contribution proving persistency of excitation for a stochastic process arising from quadratic regression analysis.

Cost-Driven Representation Learning for Linear Quadratic Gaussian Control: Part I
Authors: Yi Tian, Kaiqing Zhang, Russ Tedrake, Suvrit Sra
First: 2022-12-30T01:42:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T03:20:26+00:00
Comments: 51 pages; preliminary version appeared in L4DC 2023; this is the extended journal version, with an end-to-end guarantee added
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the task of learning state representations from potentially high-dimensional observations, with the goal of controlling an unknown partially observable system. We pursue a cost-driven approach, where a dynamic model in some latent state space is learned by predicting the costs without predicting the observations or actions. In particular, we focus on an intuitive cost-driven state representation learning method for solving Linear Quadratic Gaussian (LQG) control, one of the most fundamental partially observable control problems. As our main results, we establish finite-sample guarantees of finding a near-optimal state representation function and a near-optimal controller using the directly learned latent model, for finite-horizon time-varying LQG control problems. To the best of our knowledge, despite various empirical successes, finite-sample guarantees of such a cost-driven approach remain elusive. Our result underscores the value of predicting multi-step costs, an idea that is key to our theory, and notably also an idea that is known to be empirically valuable for learning state representations. A second part of this work, that is to appear as Part II, addresses the infinite-horizon linear time-invariant setting; it also extends the results to an approach that implicitly learns the latent dynamics, inspired by the recent empirical breakthrough of MuZero in model-based reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向线性二次高斯控制的成本驱动表征学习：第一部分
我们研究从可能的高维观测中学习状态表征的任务，旨在控制一个未知的部分可观测系统。我们采用成本驱动方法，通过在潜在状态空间学习动态模型来预测成本，而无需预测观测值或动作。特别地，我们聚焦于一种直观的成本驱动状态表征学习方法，用于求解线性二次高斯（LQG）控制——这一最基础的部分可观测控制问题之一。作为主要成果，我们为有限时域时变LQG控制问题建立了有限样本保证，证明能够通过直接学习的潜在模型找到近似最优的状态表征函数和控制器。据我们所知，尽管已有诸多实证成功案例，此类成本驱动方法的有限样本保证仍属空白。我们的结果凸显了预测多步成本的价值——这一思想既是理论的核心，也被实证证明对学习状态表征具有重要价值。本工作的第二部分（将作为第二部分发表）针对无限时域线性时不变场景，并受MuZero在基于模型的强化学习中近期实证突破的启发，将结果扩展到隐式学习潜在动力学的方法。

This paper addresses the challenge of learning state representations from high-dimensional observations to control unknown partially observable systems, motivated by the need for efficient control without predicting full observations or actions. The method introduces a cost-driven approach for Linear Quadratic Gaussian (LQG) control, where a latent dynamic model is learned by predicting multi-step costs rather than observations or actions. The main experimental results provide finite-sample guarantees for finding near-optimal state representations and controllers in finite-horizon time-varying LQG problems, highlighting the empirical value of cost prediction in representation learning.
本文研究从高维观测中学习状态表示以控制未知部分可观测系统的任务，其动机在于无需预测完整观测或动作即可实现高效控制。方法针对线性二次高斯控制提出了一种成本驱动的表示学习策略，通过预测多步成本而非观测或动作来学习潜在动态模型。主要实验结果在有限时域时变线性二次高斯控制问题中，为找到近似最优的状态表示和控制器提供了有限样本保证，强调了成本预测在表示学习中的实证价值。
Generalization in Online Reinforcement Learning for Mobile Agents
Authors: Li Gu, Zihuan Jiang, Zhixiang Chi, Huan Liu, Ziqiang Wang, Yuanhao Yu, Glen Berseth, Yang Wang
First: 2026-03-08T03:08:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T03:08:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Graphical user interface (GUI)-based mobile agents automate digital tasks on mobile devices by interpreting natural-language instructions and interacting with the screen. While recent methods apply reinforcement learning (RL) to train vision-language-model(VLM) agents in interactive environments with a primary focus on performance, generalization remains underexplored due to the lack of standardized benchmarks and open-source RL systems. In this work, we formalize the problem as a Contextual Markov Decision Process (CMDP) and introduce \textbf{AndroidWorld-Generalization}, a benchmark with three increasingly challenging regimes for evaluating zero-shot generalization to unseen task instances, templates, and applications. We further propose an RL training system that integrates Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with a scalable rollout collection system, consisting of containerized infrastructure and asynchronous execution % , and error recovery to support reliable and efficient training. Experiments on AndroidWorld-Generalization show that RL enables a 7B-parameter VLM agent to surpass supervised fine-tuning baselines, yielding a 26.1\% improvement on unseen instances but only limited gains on unseen templates (15.7\%) and apps (8.3\%), underscoring the challenges of generalization. As a preliminary step, we demonstrate that few-shot adaptation at test-time improves performance on unseen apps, motivating future research in this direction. To support reproducibility and fair comparison, we open-source the full RL training system, including the environment, task suite, models, prompt configurations, and the underlying infrastructure \footnote{https://github.com/zihuanjiang/AndroidWorld-Generalization}.

标题：移动智能体在线强化学习的泛化研究
基于图形用户界面（GUI）的移动智能体通过解析自然语言指令并与屏幕交互，实现移动设备上数字化任务的自动化。尽管现有方法主要运用强化学习（RL）在交互环境中训练视觉语言模型（VLM）智能体并聚焦于性能提升，但由于缺乏标准化基准和开源RL系统，其泛化能力仍未得到充分探索。本研究将问题形式化为上下文马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP），并推出**AndroidWorld-Generalization**基准，该基准包含三个难度递增的测试机制，用于评估智能体对未见过的任务实例、任务模板及应用程序的零样本泛化能力。我们进一步提出一种RL训练系统，该系统将组相对策略优化（GRPO）与可扩展的轨迹收集系统相结合，后者包含容器化基础设施和异步执行机制，以支持可靠高效的训练。在AndroidWorld-Generalization上的实验表明，RL能使一个70亿参数的VLM智能体超越监督微调基线，在未见实例上实现26.1%的性能提升，但在未见模板（15.7%）和应用程序（8.3%）上提升有限，凸显了泛化问题的挑战性。作为初步探索，我们验证了测试时少量样本适配能提升在未见应用程序上的性能，这为未来研究提供了方向。为支持可复现性和公平比较，我们开源了完整的RL训练系统，包括环境、任务集、模型、提示配置及底层基础设施（详见脚注链接）。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the underexplored challenge of generalization in reinforcement learning (RL) for GUI-based mobile agents, motivated by the lack of standardized benchmarks and open-source RL systems for this domain. The method formalizes the problem as a Contextual Markov Decision Process and introduces the AndroidWorld-Generalization benchmark with three regimes of increasing difficulty to evaluate zero-shot generalization. It also proposes an RL training system integrating Group Relative Policy Optimization with scalable, containerized infrastructure for efficient rollout collection. Experimental results show that RL enables a 7B-parameter vision-language model agent to outperform supervised fine-tuning baselines, achieving a 26.1% improvement on unseen task instances but only limited gains of 15.7% on unseen templates and 8.3% on unseen applications, highlighting the difficulty of generalization; few-shot adaptation at test-time is shown to improve performance on unseen apps, pointing to a direction for future work.

Dynamic Vehicle Routing Problem with Prompt Confirmation of Advance Requests
Authors: Amutheezan Sivagnanam, Ayan Mukhopadhyay, Samitha Samaranayake, Abhishek Dubey, Aron Laszka
First: 2026-03-08T02:34:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T02:34:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Transit agencies that operate on-demand transportation services have to respond to trip requests from passengers in real time, which involves solving dynamic vehicle routing problems with pick-up and drop-off constraints. Based on discussions with public transit agencies, we observe a real-world problem that is not addressed by prior work: when trips are booked in advance (e.g., trip requests arrive a few hours in advance of their requested pick-up times), the agency needs to promptly confirm whether a request can be accepted or not, and ensure that accepted requests are served as promised. State-of-the-art computational approaches either provide prompt confirmation but lack the ability to continually optimize and improve routes for accepted requests, or they provide continual optimization but cannot guarantee serving all accepted requests. To address this gap, we introduce a novel problem formulation of dynamic vehicle routing with prompt confirmation and continual optimization. We propose a novel computational approach for this vehicle routing problem, which integrates a quick insertion search for prompt confirmation with an anytime algorithm for continual optimization. To maximize the number requests served, we train a non-myopic objective function using reinforcement learning, which guides both the insertion and the anytime algorithms towards optimal, non-myopic solutions. We evaluate our computational approach on a real-world microtransit dataset from a public transit agency in the U.S., demonstrating that our proposed approach provides prompt confirmation while significantly increasing the number of requests served compared to existing approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：支持提前请求即时确认的动态车辆路径规划问题
运营按需交通服务的公交机构需实时响应乘客出行请求，这涉及解决带接送约束的动态车辆路径问题。基于与公交机构的研讨，我们发现现有研究未解决一个实际问题：当行程被提前预订时（例如出行请求在预约上车时间前数小时到达），机构需即时确认请求能否受理，并确保已受理请求按承诺履行。现有先进计算方法要么能提供即时确认但缺乏对已受理请求的持续路径优化能力，要么能持续优化但无法保证服务所有已受理请求。为填补这一空白，我们提出一种融合即时确认与持续优化的新型动态车辆路径问题框架。针对该车辆路径问题，我们提出一种创新计算方法，将用于即时确认的快速插入搜索与用于持续优化的随时算法相结合。为最大化服务请求数量，我们通过强化学习训练非近视目标函数，以引导插入算法和随时算法获得最优的非近视解。我们在美国某公交机构的真实微出行数据集上评估该方法，结果表明：相较于现有方法，我们提出的方法在提供即时确认的同时，显著提升了可服务的请求数量。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses a practical gap in dynamic vehicle routing for on-demand transit services, where agencies must promptly confirm advance trip bookings while ensuring accepted requests are served and routes are continually optimized. The authors propose a novel computational approach that combines a quick insertion search for immediate confirmation with an anytime algorithm for ongoing optimization, guided by a reinforcement-learned non-myopic objective to maximize served requests. Experimental evaluation on a real-world U.S. microtransit dataset shows the method provides prompt confirmation and significantly increases the number of requests served compared to existing approaches.
本文针对按需交通服务中的动态车辆路径规划问题，解决了实际中需即时确认提前预约行程、同时确保接受请求得到服务并持续优化路线的需求。作者提出了一种新颖的计算方法，将用于即时确认的快速插入搜索与用于持续优化的随时算法相结合，并通过强化学习训练的非短视目标函数引导以最大化服务请求数量。基于美国公共交通机构的真实微交通数据集实验表明，该方法能提供即时确认，并显著提高了服务请求数量，优于现有方法。
A Mathematical Theory of Agency and Intelligence
Authors: Wael Hafez, Chenan Wei, Rodrigo Pena, Amir Nazeri, Cameron Reid
First: 2026-02-26T01:26:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-08T01:03:43+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 4 figuers
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
To operate reliably under changing conditions, complex systems require feedback on how effectively they use resources, not just whether objectives are met. Current AI systems process vast information to produce sophisticated predictions, yet predictions can appear successful while the underlying interaction with the environment degrades. What is missing is a principled measure of how much of the total information a system deploys is actually shared between its observations, actions, and outcomes. We prove this shared fraction, which we term bipredictability, P, is intrinsic to any interaction, derivable from first principles, and strictly bounded: P can reach unity in quantum systems, P equal to, or smaller than 0.5 in classical systems, and lower once agency (action selection) is introduced. We confirm these bounds in a physical system (double pendulum), reinforcement learning agents, and multi turn LLM conversations. These results distinguish agency from intelligence: agency is the capacity to act on predictions, whereas intelligence additionally requires learning from interaction, self-monitoring of its learning effectiveness, and adapting the scope of observations, actions, and outcomes to restore effective learning. By this definition, current AI systems achieve agency but not intelligence. Inspired by thalamocortical regulation in biological systems, we demonstrate a feedback architecture that monitors P in real time, establishing a prerequisite for adaptive, resilient AI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：代理与智能的数学理论
为在变化条件下可靠运行，复杂系统需要关于其资源使用效率的反馈，而不仅仅是目标是否达成。当前人工智能系统处理海量信息以生成复杂预测，但预测可能看似成功，而系统与环境的底层交互却在退化。缺失的是一个原则性度量，用于衡量系统部署的总信息中，有多少实际在其观察、行动与结果之间共享。我们证明这一共享比例（称为双可预测性P）内在于任何交互，可从第一性原理推导，且严格有界：P在量子系统中可达1，在经典系统中等于或小于0.5，引入代理（行动选择）后进一步降低。我们在物理系统（双摆）、强化学习智能体及多轮大语言模型对话中验证了这些界限。这些结果区分了代理与智能：代理是基于预测行动的能力，而智能还需从交互中学习、自我监测学习效率，并调整观察、行动与结果的范围以恢复有效学习。按此定义，当前人工智能系统实现了代理而非智能。受生物系统中丘脑皮质调节的启发，我们展示了一种实时监测P的反馈架构，为自适应、强韧的人工智能奠定了基础。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for complex systems to assess their resource effectiveness beyond mere objective achievement, this paper introduces 'bipredictability' (P) as a fundamental measure of the shared information between a system's observations, actions, and outcomes. The method derives this measure from first principles, proving it is intrinsic to any interaction and establishing theoretical bounds: P can reach 1 in quantum systems, is ≤0.5 in classical systems, and is further reduced by agency. Experimental results confirm these bounds in a physical double pendulum, reinforcement learning agents, and multi-turn LLM conversations. The findings distinguish agency (acting on predictions) from intelligence (which additionally requires learning from interaction and self-monitoring), concluding current AI systems possess agency but not intelligence, and the paper proposes a thalamocortical-inspired feedback architecture to monitor P for building adaptive AI.
本文的动机在于复杂系统需要评估其资源使用效率，而不仅仅是目标达成情况，为此引入了“双可预测性”（P）作为衡量系统观察、行动与结果之间共享信息的基本指标。方法上从第一性原理推导出这一度量，证明其内在于任何交互，并建立了理论界限：在量子系统中P可达1，在经典系统中P≤0.5，且引入主体性（行动选择）后会进一步降低。主要实验结果在物理双摆、强化学习智能体和多轮大语言模型对话中验证了这些界限。研究区分了主体性（基于预测行动）与智能（还需从交互中学习并自我监控），指出当前AI系统只具备主体性而非智能，并受生物丘脑皮质调节启发，提出了一种实时监控P的反饋架构，为构建自适应、有韧性的AI奠定了基础。
ARLArena: A Unified Framework for Stable Agentic Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xiaoxuan Wang, Han Zhang, Haixin Wang, Yidan Shi, Ruoyan Li, Kaiqiao Han, Chenyi Tong, Haoran Deng, Renliang Sun, Alexander Taylor, Yanqiao Zhu, Jason Cong, Yizhou Sun, Wei Wang
First: 2026-02-25T03:43:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-07T23:51:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic reinforcement learning (ARL) has rapidly gained attention as a promising paradigm for training agents to solve complex, multi-step interactive tasks. Despite encouraging early results, ARL remains highly unstable, often leading to training collapse. This instability limits scalability to larger environments and longer interaction horizons, and constrains systematic exploration of algorithmic design choices. In this paper, we first propose ARLArena, a stable training recipe and systematic analysis framework that examines training stability in a controlled and reproducible setting. ARLArena first constructs a clean and standardized testbed. Then, we decompose policy gradient into four core design dimensions and assess the performance and stability of each dimension. Through this fine-grained analysis, we distill a unified perspective on ARL and propose SAMPO, a stable agentic policy optimization method designed to mitigate the dominant sources of instability in ARL. Empirically, SAMPO achieves consistently stable training and strong performance across diverse agentic tasks. Overall, this study provides a unifying policy gradient perspective for ARL and offers practical guidance for building stable and reproducible LLM-based agent training pipelines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARLArena：稳定智能体强化学习的统一框架
智能体强化学习（ARL）作为一种训练智能体解决复杂多步交互任务的前沿范式，已迅速受到关注。尽管早期成果令人鼓舞，但ARL仍存在高度不稳定性，常导致训练崩溃。这种不稳定性限制了其向更大环境和更长交互周期的扩展，并制约了对算法设计选择的系统性探索。本文首先提出ARLArena——一个稳定的训练方案与系统性分析框架，可在受控可复现环境中检验训练稳定性。ARLArena首先构建了清晰标准化的测试平台，随后将策略梯度分解为四个核心设计维度，并评估各维度的性能与稳定性。通过这种细粒度分析，我们提炼出ARL的统一视角，进而提出SAMPO方法——一种旨在缓解ARL主要不稳定源的稳定智能体策略优化方法。实验表明，SAMPO在多样化智能体任务中均能实现持续稳定的训练与优异性能。本研究为ARL提供了统一的策略梯度视角，并为构建稳定可复现的基于大语言模型的智能体训练流程提供了实践指导。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the instability and training collapse issues that hinder the scalability and systematic exploration of agentic reinforcement learning (ARL) for complex tasks. The method introduces ARLArena, a framework that first establishes a standardized testbed and then decomposes policy gradient into four core design dimensions to analyze stability, leading to the proposal of SAMPO, a stable optimization method designed to mitigate key instability sources. The main experimental results demonstrate that SAMPO achieves consistently stable training and strong performance across diverse agentic tasks, providing a unified perspective and practical guidance for stable LLM-based agent training.

Learning to Reflect: Hierarchical Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning for CSI-Free mmWave Beam-Focusing
Authors: Hieu Le, Oguz Bedir, Mostafa Ibrahim, Jian Tao, Sabit Ekin
First: 2026-03-07T22:46:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-07T22:46:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces promise to transform wireless environments, yet practical deployment is hindered by the prohibitive overhead of Channel State Information (CSI) estimation and the dimensionality explosion inherent in centralized optimization. This paper proposes a Hierarchical Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (HMARL) framework for the control of mechanically reconfigurable reflective surfaces in millimeter-wave (mmWave) systems. We introduce a "CSI-free" paradigm that substitutes pilot-based channel estimation with readily available user localization data. To manage the massive combinatorial action space, the proposed architecture utilizes Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (MAPPO) under a Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE) paradigm. The proposed architecture decomposes the control problem into two abstraction levels: a high-level controller for user-to-reflector allocation and decentralized low-level controllers for low-level focal point optimization. Comprehensive ray-tracing evaluations demonstrate that the framework achieves 2.81-7.94 dB RSSI improvements over centralized baselines, with the performance advantage widening as system complexity increases. Scalability analysis reveals that the system maintains sustained efficiency, exhibiting minimal per-user performance degradation and stable total power utilization even when user density doubles. Furthermore, robustness validation confirms the framework's viability across varying reflector aperture sizes (45-99 tiles) and demonstrates graceful performance degradation under localization errors up to 0.5 m. By eliminating CSI overhead while maintaining high-fidelity beam-focusing, this work establishes HMARL as a practical solution for intelligent mmWave environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学会反射：基于分层多智能体强化学习的免CSI毫米波波束聚焦
可重构智能表面有望变革无线环境，但实际部署受限于信道状态信息估计的过高开销以及集中式优化固有的维度爆炸问题。本文提出一种分层多智能体强化学习框架，用于控制毫米波系统中的机械可重构反射表面。我们引入一种“免CSI”范式，以易获取的用户定位数据替代基于导频的信道估计。为应对巨大的组合动作空间，该架构采用集中训练分散执行范式下的多智能体近端策略优化算法。该架构将控制问题分解为两个抽象层级：高层控制器负责用户-反射器分配，分散的低层控制器则进行低层焦点优化。全面的射线追踪评估表明，该框架相比集中式基线实现了2.81-7.94 dB的接收信号强度指示提升，且系统复杂度越高性能优势越显著。可扩展性分析显示系统能持续保持效率，在用户密度翻倍时仍维持极低的单用户性能衰减与稳定的总功率利用率。鲁棒性验证进一步证实框架在不同反射面孔径尺寸（45-99个单元）下的可行性，并在定位误差达0.5米时仅出现平缓的性能衰减。本工作通过消除CSI开销并保持高精度波束聚焦，确立了分层多智能体强化学习作为智能毫米波环境实用解决方案的地位。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the prohibitive overhead of Channel State Information (CSI) estimation and the scalability challenges of centralized optimization for Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces, this paper proposes a Hierarchical Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (HMARL) framework for CSI-free millimeter-wave beam-focusing. The method replaces pilot-based channel estimation with user localization data and employs a Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution paradigm using Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization, decomposing control into high-level user allocation and low-level focal point optimization. Experimental results from ray-tracing evaluations show the framework achieves 2.81-7.94 dB RSSI improvements over centralized baselines, scales efficiently with doubled user density, and remains robust across varying reflector sizes and localization errors up to 0.5 meters.
本文的动机是解决可重构智能表面部署中信道状态信息估计开销巨大以及集中式优化维度爆炸的难题，提出了一种用于免信道状态信息的毫米波波束聚焦的层次化多智能体强化学习框架。该方法用用户定位数据替代基于导频的信道估计，采用集中训练分散执行的范式与多智能体近端策略优化，将控制问题分解为高层用户分配和低层焦点优化。基于射线追踪的综合实验表明，该框架相比集中式基线实现了2.81-7.94 dB的接收信号强度指示提升，在用户密度翻倍时仍能保持高效可扩展性，并且在不同反射面尺寸和高达0.5米的定位误差下均表现出良好的鲁棒性。
Accelerating Robotic Reinforcement Learning with Agent Guidance
Authors: Haojun Chen, Zili Zou, Chengdong Ma, Yaoxiang Pu, Haotong Zhang, Yuanpei Chen, Yaodong Yang
First: 2026-02-12T14:09:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-07T19:58:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) offers a powerful paradigm for autonomous robots to master generalist manipulation skills through trial-and-error. However, its real-world application is stifled by low sample efficiency. Recent Human-in-the-Loop (HIL) methods accelerate training by using human corrections, yet this approach faces a scalability barrier. Reliance on human supervisors imposes a 1:1 supervision ratio that limits scalability, suffers from operator fatigue over extended sessions, and introduces high variance due to inconsistent human proficiency. We present Agent-guided Policy Search (AGPS), a framework that automates the training pipeline by replacing human supervisors with a multimodal agent. Our key insight is that the agent can be viewed as a semantic world model, injecting intrinsic value priors to structure physical exploration. By using tools, the agent provides precise guidance via corrective waypoints and spatial constraints for exploration pruning. We validate our approach on three tasks, ranging from precision insertion to deformable object manipulation. Results demonstrate that AGPS outperforms HIL methods in sample efficiency. This automates the supervision pipeline, unlocking the path to labor-free and scalable robot learning. Project website: https://agps-rl.github.io/agps/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于智能体引导的机器人强化学习加速方法
强化学习（RL）为自主机器人通过试错掌握通用操作技能提供了强大范式，但其在现实世界的应用受限于低样本效率。现有的人机协同（HIL）方法通过人工修正加速训练，但面临可扩展性瓶颈：依赖人工监督导致1:1监督比例限制扩展性、长时间操作易引发人员疲劳、且人工技能差异会引入高方差。本文提出智能体引导策略搜索（AGPS）框架，通过多模态智能体替代人工监督实现训练流程自动化。核心思路是将智能体视为语义世界模型，通过注入内在价值先验来结构化物理探索。智能体借助工具提供精确引导，包括修正路径点和空间约束以剪枝探索空间。我们在精密插装到可变形物体操作等三项任务中验证了该方法。实验表明AGPS在样本效率上优于HIL方法，实现了监督流程自动化，为无需人工干预且可扩展的机器人学习开辟了新路径。项目网站：https://agps-rl.github.io/agps/。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the scalability limitations of Human-in-the-Loop reinforcement learning for robotic manipulation, which suffers from low sample efficiency and human supervisory burdens. The proposed method, Agent-guided Policy Search (AGPS), automates supervision by replacing human operators with a multimodal agent that acts as a semantic world model to provide intrinsic value priors, using tools to offer corrective waypoints and spatial constraints for efficient exploration. Experimental validation on tasks including precision insertion and deformable object manipulation shows that AGPS achieves superior sample efficiency compared to human-in-the-loop methods, enabling a more scalable and labor-free training pipeline.
本文针对机器人强化学习中人为干预方法存在的可扩展性限制问题，该方法样本效率低且依赖人力监督。提出的智能体引导策略搜索框架通过用多模态智能体替代人类监督者，将其视为语义世界模型以注入内在价值先验，利用工具提供纠正路径点和空间约束来优化探索。在精密插入和可变形物体操作等任务上的实验结果表明，该框架在样本效率上优于人为干预方法，为实现无需人工、可扩展的机器人学习提供了路径。
